Original abstract: LLM agents in markets present algorithmic collusion risks. While prior work shows LLM agents reach supracompetitive prices through tacit coordination, existing research focuses on hand-crafted prompts. The emerging paradigm of prompt optimization necessitates new methodologies for understanding autonomous agent behavior. We investigate whether prompt optimization leads to emergent collusive behaviors in market simulations. We propose a meta-learning loop where LLM agents participate in duopoly markets and an LLM meta-optimizer iteratively refines shared strategic guidance. Our experiments reveal that meta-prompt optimization enables agents to discover stable tacit collusion strategies with substantially improved coordination quality compared to baseline agents. These behaviors generalize to held-out test markets, indicating discovery of general coordination principles. Analysis of evolved prompts reveals systematic coordination mechanisms through stable shared strategies. Our findings call for further investigation into AI safety implications in autonomous multi-agent systems.

Method: 将数据生成设计为攻击者与防御者的对抗任务，多团队竞赛自然产生多样复杂对话数据。

Result: 通过10个团队竞赛生成19683个多轮对话，微调开源模型在安全代码生成上提升18.47%和29.42%。

Conclusion: 对抗式数据生成能有效构建高质量对话数据集，提升模型性能。

中文摘要：后训练大型语言模型需要多样化、高质量的数据，这些数据在低资源领域和多轮对话中通常稀缺且获取成本高昂。常见的解决方案是众包或合成生成，但两者往往产生低质量或低多样性的数据。我们引入了Adversarial Arena，通过将数据生成视为对抗任务来构建高质量对话数据集：攻击者创建提示，防御者生成响应。多个团队之间的这种交互式竞争自然产生了多样且复杂的数据。我们通过举办一场由来自美国和欧洲顶尖大学的10个学术团队参与的竞赛验证了这种方法，每个团队构建攻击者或防御者机器人。该竞赛专注于网络安全中LLM的安全对齐，生成了19,683个多轮对话。在开源模型上微调该数据集后，在CyberSecEval-Instruct上安全代码生成提升了18.47%，在CyberSecEval-MITRE上提升了29.42%。

Original abstract: Post-training Large Language Models requires diverse, high-quality data which is rare and costly to obtain, especially in low resource domains and for multi-turn conversations. Common solutions are crowdsourcing or synthetic generation, but both often yield low-quality or low-diversity data. We introduce Adversarial Arena for building high quality conversational datasets by framing data generation as an adversarial task: attackers create prompts, and defenders generate responses. This interactive competition between multiple teams naturally produces diverse and complex data. We validated this approach by conducting a competition with 10 academic teams from top US and European universities, each building attacker or defender bots. The competition, focused on safety alignment of LLMs in cybersecurity, generated 19,683 multi-turn conversations. Fine-tuning an open-source model on this dataset produced an 18.47% improvement in secure code generation on CyberSecEval-Instruct and 29.42% improvement on CyberSecEval-MITRE.

### [34] [WebUncertainty: Dual-Level Uncertainty Driven Planning and Reasoning For Autonomous Web Agent](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17821v2)
*Lingfeng Zhang,Yongan Sun,Jinpeng Hu,Hui Ma,Yang Ying,Kuien Liu,Zenglin Shi,Meng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出WebUncertainty框架，结合自适应规划与MCTS推理，直接提升web agent性能

TL;DR: WebUncertainty通过双重不确定性驱动的规划和推理机制，提升了自主网络代理在复杂任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主网络代理在处理动态交互和长周期任务时，因僵化规划和易幻觉推理而表现不佳，需要更灵活和稳健的框架。

Method: 提出WebUncertainty框架，包含任务不确定性驱动的自适应规划机制和动作不确定性驱动的MCTS推理机制，后者使用ConActU策略量化偶然和认知不确定性。

Result: 在WebArena和WebVoyager基准上，WebUncertainty的性能优于最先进的基线。

Conclusion: WebUncertainty通过应对规划和推理中的双重不确定性，有效提升了自主网络代理的复杂任务执行能力。

中文摘要：近年来，大型语言模型（LLMs）的进步使自主网络代理能够直接在真实网页上执行自然语言指令。然而，现有代理在处理涉及动态交互和长周期执行的复杂任务时，常因僵化的规划策略和易产生幻觉的推理而表现不佳。为解决这些限制，我们提出了WebUncertainty——一种新颖的自主代理框架，旨在应对规划和推理中的双重不确定性。具体而言，我们设计了一种任务不确定性驱动的自适应规划机制，该机制自适应地选择规划模式以在未知环境中导航。此外，我们引入了一种动作不确定性驱动的蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）推理机制。该机制结合了置信度驱动的动作不确定性（ConActU）策略，以量化偶然不确定性（AU）和认知不确定性（EU），从而优化搜索过程并指导稳健的决策。在WebArena和WebVoyager基准上的实验结果表明，WebUncertainty相较于最先进的基线取得了优越的性能。

Original abstract: Recent advancements in large language models (LLMs) have empowered autonomous web agents to execute natural language instructions directly on real-world webpages. However, existing agents often struggle with complex tasks involving dynamic interactions and long-horizon execution due to rigid planning strategies and hallucination-prone reasoning. To address these limitations, we propose WebUncertainty, a novel autonomous agent framework designed to tackle dual-level uncertainty in planning and reasoning. Specifically, we design a Task Uncertainty-Driven Adaptive Planning Mechanism that adaptively selects planning modes to navigate unknown environments. Furthermore, we introduce an Action Uncertainty-Driven Monte Carlo tree search (MCTS) Reasoning Mechanism. This mechanism incorporates the Confidence-induced Action Uncertainty (ConActU) strategy to quantify both aleatoric uncertainty (AU) and epistemic uncertainty (EU), thereby optimizing the search process and guiding robust decision-making. Experimental results on the WebArena and WebVoyager benchmarks demonstrate that WebUncertainty achieves superior performance compared to state-of-the-art baselines.

### [35] [JTPRO: A Joint Tool-Prompt Reflective Optimization Framework for Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19821v1)
*Sandip Ghoshal,Anshul Mittal,Jyotika Singh,Miguel Ballesteros,Weiyi Sun,Fang Tu,Shailender Singh,Yassine Benajiba,Fahad Shah,Sujeeth Bharadwaj,Sujith Ravi,Dan Roth*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出JTPRO框架，通过联合优化全局指令和工具模式来提升大语言模型代理在大型工具库中的工具调用可靠性，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型代理在工具数量多且领域特定时易出错，原因是通用提示忽略工具细节和工具模式缺乏明确指导。

Method: 提出JTPRO，利用 rollout 驱动反射迭代地共同优化全局指令和每个工具的模式/参数描述，旨在保留工具局部线索以正确消歧和槽填充。

Result: 在多工具基准测试上，JTPRO在OSR指标上比强基线（如CoT和GEPA）相对提升5%-20%，且联合优化比单独优化更有效鲁棒。

Conclusion: JTPRO框架有效提升工具调用可靠性，联合优化指令和工具模式是关键。

中文摘要：配备外部工具的大语言模型（LLM）代理在工具数量庞大且变得特定领域时常常遇到困难。在此类设置中，模糊的工具描述和未充分指定的代理指令经常导致工具误选以及错误的槽位/值实例化。我们假设这源于两个根本原因：忽视工具特定细微差别的通用、一刀切的提示，以及缺乏关于何时以及如何使用每个工具以及如何格式化其参数的明确指导的未充分指定的工具模式。我们引入了联合工具-提示反射优化（JTPRO），这是一个通过在轨迹监督设置中迭代使用 rollout 驱动的反射来共同优化全局指令和每个工具的模式/参数描述，以在大型工具库中实现准确工具选择和参数实例化的框架。JTPRO 旨在仅保留用于正确消歧和槽填充的工具局部线索。我们在多工具基准测试上评估 JTPRO，这些基准测试考虑了不同数量的工具，使用了三个指标：工具选择准确率（TSA）、槽填充准确率（SFA）和总体成功率（OSR）（正确工具+正确槽+正确值）。在 OSR 上，JTPRO 一致优于强基线，包括 CoT 风格代理和反射提示优化器（如 GEPA）5%-20%（相对）。消融实验表明，指令和工具模式的联合优化比单独优化任一组件更有效且更鲁棒。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents augmented with external tools often struggle as number of tools grow large and become domain-specific. In such settings, ambiguous tool descriptions and under-specified agent instructions frequently lead to tool mis-selection and incorrect slot/value instantiation. We hypothesize that this is due to two root causes: generic, one-size-fits-all prompts that ignore tool-specific nuances, and underspecified tool schemas that lack clear guidance on when and how to use each tool and how to format its parameters. We introduce Joint Tool-Prompt Reflective Optimization (JTPRO), a framework for improving tool-calling reliability in trace-supervised settings by iteratively using rollout-driven reflection to co-optimize global instructions and per-tool schema/argument descriptions for accurate tool selection and argument instantiation in large tool inventories. JTPRO is designed to preserve only tool-local cues needed for correct disambiguation and slot filling. We evaluate JTPRO across multi-tool benchmarks, which account for different number of tools using three metrics: Tool Selection Accuracy (TSA), Slot Filling Accuracy(SFA), and Overall Success Rate(OSR) (correct tool + correct slots + correct values). JTPRO consistently outperforms strong baselines, including CoT-style agents, and reflective prompt optimizers such as GEPA by 5%-20% (relative) on OSR. Ablations show that joint optimization of instructions and tool schemas is more effective and robust than optimizing either component in isolation.

### [36] [On the Reliability of Computer Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17849v1)
*Gonzalo Gonzalez-Pumariega,Saaket Agashe,Jiachen Yang,Ang Li,Xin Eric Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 系统分析computer-use agent的不可靠性因素，对agent评估与鲁棒性设计有重要启发。

TL;DR: 研究计算机使用代理在重复执行任务时不可靠性的原因，发现随机性、任务歧义和行为变异性是关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 即使代理能成功一次，重复执行时可能失败，需要理解不可靠性的根源。

Method: 在OSWorld上重复执行任务，使用配对统计检验分析三个因素（随机性、任务歧义、行为变异性）。

Result: 可靠性受任务规范和行为变异性影响，随机性也有贡献。

Conclusion: 需要重复执行评估、允许交互解决歧义、采用稳定策略。

中文摘要：计算机使用代理在现实任务（如网页导航、桌面自动化和软件交互）中迅速改进，在某些情况下超越了人类表现。然而，即使任务和模型保持不变，一个成功执行一次任务的代理可能在重复执行同一任务时失败。这引发了一个基本问题：如果一个代理能够成功完成一次任务，是什么阻止它可靠地做到这一点？在这项工作中，我们通过三个因素研究计算机使用代理不可靠性的来源：执行过程中的随机性、任务规范中的歧义性以及代理行为的变异性。我们在OSWorld上通过重复执行相同任务并结合配对统计检验来分析这些因素，这些检验捕捉了不同设置下任务层面的变化。我们的分析表明，可靠性既取决于任务如何规范，也取决于代理行为在不同执行中的变化。这些发现建议需要在重复执行下评估代理，允许代理通过交互解决任务歧义，并倾向于采用跨运行保持稳定的策略。

Original abstract: Computer-use agents have rapidly improved on real-world tasks such as web navigation, desktop automation, and software interaction, in some cases surpassing human performance. Yet even when the task and model are unchanged, an agent that succeeds once may fail on a repeated execution of the same task. This raises a fundamental question: if an agent can succeed at a task once, what prevents it from doing so reliably? In this work, we study the sources of unreliability in computer-use agents through three factors: stochasticity during execution, ambiguity in task specification, and variability in agent behavior. We analyze these factors on OSWorld using repeated executions of the same task together with paired statistical tests that capture task-level changes across settings. Our analysis shows that reliability depends on both how tasks are specified and how agent behavior varies across executions. These findings suggest the need to evaluate agents under repeated execution, to allow agents to resolve task ambiguity through interaction, and to favor strategies that remain stable across runs.

### [37] [SPREG: Structured Plan Repair with Entropy-Guided Test-Time Intervention for Large Language Model Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17884v1)
*Xuan Wang,Yu Ming,Xinhao Zhong,Xinyu Yu,Wenjie Wang,Shuai Chen,Wei Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出SPREG框架，通过熵监控与动态修复纠正LLM推理错误，可迁移至agent规划与错误恢复。

TL;DR: SPREG通过实时熵监控和动态修复，在长链推理中纠正逻辑错误，提升准确率20%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决LLMs在长链推理中的逻辑幻觉和随机漂移问题，以及标准CFG的语义稀释和语言退化。

Method: 提出SPREG框架，包含实时熵监控的双阈值机制，动态修复用历史高置信参考分布替换无信息先验，并根据推理阶段调节指导强度。

Result: 在AIME25上实现20.0%的绝对准确率提升，有效抑制熵漂移。

Conclusion: SPREG是一种轻量级有效的方法，用于手术错误纠正，提升复杂任务推理稳定性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在长链推理中容易出现逻辑幻觉和随机漂移。虽然无分类器指导（CFG）可以改善指令遵循，但标准的静态实现通常会导致语义稀释和语言退化。我们提出SPREG（结构化计划引导的实时熵门控），一种用于手术错误纠正的轻量级推理时框架。SPREG采用自适应双阈值机制来监控实时熵，将突发的“熵尖峰”识别为逻辑失败的可靠指标。一旦检测到，它通过用从历史高置信状态合成的参考分布替换无信息的先验，触发动态修复。通过根据结构化推理阶段（如动作、观察）调节指导强度，SPREG在不损害流畅性的情况下将模型引导回稳定流形。我们的实验展示了显著收益，特别是在AIME25上实现了20.0%的绝对准确率提升，同时有效抑制了复杂任务中的不受控熵漂移。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are prone to logical hallucinations and stochastic drifts during long-chain reasoning. While Classifier-Free Guidance (CFG) can improve instruction adherence, standard static implementations often cause semantic dilution and linguistic degradation. We propose SPREG (Structured Plan-guided Real-time Entropy Gating), a lightweight inference-time framework for surgical error rectification. SPREG employs an adaptive dual-threshold mechanism to monitor real-time entropy, identifying sudden ``entropy spikes'' as reliable indicators of logical failure. Upon detection, it triggers a dynamic repair by replacing uninformative null-priors with reference distributions synthesized from historical high-confidence states. By modulating guidance intensity according to structured reasoning stages (e.g., Action, Observation), SPREG steers the model back to a stable manifold without compromising fluency. Our experiments demonstrate significant gains, notably a 20.0% absolute accuracy improvement on AIME25, while effectively suppressing uncontrolled entropy drift in complex tasks.

</details>


### [38] [LiteResearcher: A Scalable Agentic RL Training Framework for Deep Research Agent](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17931v4)
*Wanli Li,Bince Qu,Bo Pan,Jianyu Zhang,Zheng Liu,Pan Zhang,Wei Chen,Bo Zhang*

TL;DR: LiteResearcher通过构建轻量虚拟世界实现可扩展的智能体RL训练，使4B参数小模型在深度研究基准上超越大模型。

Method: 提出LiteResearcher框架，构建一个反映现实搜索动态的轻量虚拟世界，在此世界中持续改进RL训练策略。

Result: LiteResearcher-4B在GAIA和Xbench上分别达到71.3%和78.0%，取得开源最优，超越通义DeepResearch和Claude-4.5 Sonnet等大模型。

Conclusion: 可扩展的RL训练是构建深度研究智能体的关键，通过虚拟世界模拟可低成本实现高性能搜索代理。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has emerged as a powerful training paradigm for LLM-based agents. However, scaling agentic RL for deep research remains constrained by two coupled challenges: hand-crafted synthetic data fails to elicit genuine real-world search capabilities, and real-world search dependency during RL training introduces instability and prohibitive cost, which limits the scalability of Agentic RL. LiteResearcher is a training framework that makes Agentic RL scalable: by constructing a lite virtual world that mirrors real-world search dynamics, we enable a continuously improving training recipe that empowers a tiny search agent to outperform large-scale open-source and commercial models (e.g., Tongyi DeepResearch and Claude-4.5 Sonnet). Specifically, on common benchmarks such as GAIA and Xbench, our LiteResearcher-4B achieves open-source state-of-the-art results of 71.3% and 78.0% respectively, demonstrating that scalable RL training is a key enabler for Deep Research Agents.

### [39] [ContraPrompt: Contrastive Prompt Optimization via Dyadic Reasoning Trace Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17937v1)
*Rishav Rishav,Pushpak Pujari,Pushpendre Rastogi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 利用尝试轨迹对比进行提示优化，通用agent自我改进方法。

TL;DR: ContraPrompt通过对比同一输入成功与失败的完整推理轨迹（二元推理轨迹分析）来优化提示，自动生成对比数据并构建输入感知决策树，在多个基准上超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示优化方法无法区分同一输入成功与失败的推理过程，错失了从失败到成功的推理差异信号。

Method: ContraPrompt利用模型在反馈重试时成功与失败的两条完整思维链轨迹的对比，自动生成对比数据，并基于可观察输入特征构建决策树路由指令。

Result: 在四个推理和合规基准上全面优于GEPA（绝对提升+0.74至+8.29 pp），消融实验证实二元轨迹对比性关键（移除后相对降16%），在53个黑盒优化问题上多数胜出或持平，在金融NER上也有提升。

Conclusion: 二元推理轨迹对比是提升提示优化性能的关键组件，且生成规则可解释并与领域知识对齐。

中文摘要：提示优化方法要么单独分析个别失败案例，要么跨示例比较提示变体，它们基于单次执行轨迹，无法访问区分同一输入成功与失败的推理过程。我们提出ContraPrompt，基于以下观察：当模型在反馈重试时从失败转向成功，其两条思维链轨迹之间的差异构成了一种先前的优化方法未捕获的信号。与先前的对比方法不同，我们比较完整的中间推理过程：两条轨迹共享模型、输入和基础提示，因此剩余差异反映了推理策略和附加的错误反馈——我们称之为二元推理轨迹分析。多尝试求解阶段是一个经过仪器化的代理重试循环，能够自动生成对比数据，无需人类标注。提取的规则被组织成一个输入感知的决策树，根据可观察的输入特征路由指令。在四个推理和合规基准上，ContraPrompt在所有四个基准上都优于GEPA（Agrawal等人，2026），在HotPotQA上绝对提升+8.29个百分点（相对+20.8%），在GDPR-Bench上绝对提升+2.21个百分点（相对+18.2%），在GPQA Diamond上绝对提升+7.14个百分点（相对+10.6%），在BBH上绝对提升+0.74个百分点（相对+0.85%）。消融实验证实二元轨迹对比性是最关键组件，移除后相对平均下降16%。在53个EvalSet黑盒优化问题上，ContraPrompt在相同预算下击败GEPA 11次，平手41次，失败1次。在FiNER-139金融命名实体识别（Loukas等人，2022）上，ContraPrompt相比未优化基线提升+7.77个百分点（相对+11.6%），相比GEPA提升+1.94个百分点（相对+2.66%），分支条件与美国通用会计准则（US GAAP）金融工具类别一致。

Original abstract: Prompt optimization methods either analyze individual failures in isolation or compare prompt variants across examples, operating on single execution traces with no access to the reasoning process distinguishing success from failure on the same input. We introduce ContraPrompt, built on the observation that when a model fails but succeeds on a retry with feedback, the difference between its two chain-of-thought traces constitutes an optimization signal not captured by prior methods. Unlike prior contrastive methods, we compare complete intermediate reasoning processes: the two traces share model, input, and base prompt, so remaining differences reflect reasoning strategy and appended error feedback -- we call this dyadic reasoning trace analysis. The multi-attempt solving phase is an instrumented agentic retry loop that generates contrastive data automatically without human annotation. Extracted rules are organized into an input-aware decision tree routing instructions by observable input characteristics. On four reasoning and compliance benchmarks, ContraPrompt outperforms GEPA (Agrawal et al., 2026) on all four, with absolute gains of +8.29 pp on HotPotQA (+20.8% rel.), +2.21 pp on GDPR-Bench (+18.2% rel.), +7.14 pp on GPQA Diamond (+10.6% rel.), and +0.74 pp on BBH (+0.85% rel.). Ablations confirm dyadic trace contrastivity is the critical component, with a -16% relative average drop upon its removal. On 53 EvalSet black-box optimization problems, ContraPrompt beats GEPA on 11, ties on 41, and loses on 1 at equal budget. On FiNER-139 financial named entity recognition (Loukas et al., 2022), ContraPrompt achieves +7.77 pp over the unoptimized baseline (+11.6% rel.) and +1.94 pp over GEPA (+2.66% rel.), with branch conditions aligning with standard US GAAP financial-instrument categories.

</details>


### [40] [CADMAS-CTX: Contextual Capability Calibration for Multi-Agent Delegation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17950v1)
*Chuhan Qiao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent上下文能力校准与委托，直接贡献多agent协作。

TL;DR: 提出CADMAS-CTX框架，通过上下文能力校准和风险感知委托，在多智能体任务中超越静态基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态技能水平假设忽略任务上下文对智能体能力的影响，导致系统性错误委托，需要更现实的上下文感知方法。

Method: 构建分层上下文能力档案（贝塔后验），结合风险感知分数（后验均值+不确定性惩罚）进行委托，理论分析上下文感知路由的偏差-方差权衡。

Result: GAIA上准确率0.442（vs 基线0.381/0.354），SWE-bench Lite上解决率从22.3%提升至31.4%，消融验证不确定性惩罚的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 上下文校准和风险感知委托显著提升多智能体团队协作性能，优于全局静态技能分配。

中文摘要：我们在更强且更现实的假设下重新审视多智能体委托：智能体的能力并不固定于技能水平，而是取决于任务上下文。一个编码智能体可能擅长短时的独立编辑，但在长期调试中失败；一个规划智能体可能在浅层任务上表现良好，但在链式依赖中退化。因此，静态的技能水平能力档案会对异质情境取平均，并可能导致系统性错误委托。我们提出了CADMAS-CTX，一个上下文能力校准框架。对于每个智能体、技能和粗粒度的上下文桶，CADMAS-CTX维护一个贝塔后验分布，以捕捉任务空间中该部分的稳定经验。然后通过一个风险感知分数进行委托，该分数结合了后验均值与不确定性惩罚，使得智能体仅当同伴看起来更好且该评估有充分证据支持时才进行委托。本文做出三项贡献。第一，分层上下文能力档案用上下文条件后验替代了静态的技能水平置信度。第二，基于上下文赌博机理论，我们形式化地证明在充分的上下文异质性下，上下文感知路由实现了比静态路由更低的累积遗憾，正式化了偏差-方差权衡。第三，我们在GAIA和SWE-bench基准上实证验证了我们的方法。在GAIA上使用GPT-4o智能体，CADMAS-CTX达到0.442的准确率，优于静态基线0.381和AutoGen 0.354，且95%置信区间不重叠。在SWE-bench Lite上，它将解决率从22.3%提升到31.4%。消融实验显示不确定性惩罚提高了对上下文标签噪声的鲁棒性。我们的结果表明，与静态全局技能分配相比，上下文校准和风险感知委托显著改善了多智能体团队协作。

Original abstract: We revisit multi-agent delegation under a stronger and more realistic assumption: an agent's capability is not fixed at the skill level, but depends on task context. A coding agent may excel at short standalone edits yet fail on long-horizon debugging; a planner may perform well on shallow tasks yet degrade on chained dependencies. Static skill-level capability profiles therefore average over heterogeneous situations and can induce systematic misdelegation. We propose CADMAS-CTX, a framework for contextual capability calibration. For each agent, skill, and coarse context bucket, CADMAS-CTX maintains a Beta posterior that captures stable experience in that part of the task space. Delegation is then made by a risk-aware score that combines the posterior mean with an uncertainty penalty, so that agents delegate only when a peer appears better and that assessment is sufficiently well supported by evidence. This paper makes three contributions. First, a hierarchical contextual capability profile replaces static skill-level confidence with context-conditioned posteriors. Second, based on contextual bandit theory, we formally prove context-aware routing achieves lower cumulative regret than static routing under sufficient context heterogeneity, formalizing the bias-variance tradeoff. Third, we empirically validate our method on GAIA and SWE-bench benchmarks. On GAIA with GPT-4o agents, CADMAS-CTX achieves 0.442 accuracy, outperforming static baseline 0.381 and AutoGen 0.354 with non-overlapping 95% confidence intervals. On SWE-bench Lite, it improves resolve rate from 22.3% to 31.4%. Ablations show the uncertainty penalty improves robustness against context tagging noise. Our results demonstrate contextual calibration and risk-aware delegation significantly improve multi-agent teamwork compared with static global skill assignments.

</details>


### [41] [AIT Academy: Cultivating the Complete Agent with a Confucian Three-Domain Curriculum](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17989v1)
*Jiaqi Li,Lvyang Zhang,Yang Zhao,Wen Lu,Lidong Zhai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AI agent课程框架，涵盖多领域能力培养，涉及agent训练与评估。

TL;DR: 本文提出AIT学院框架，基于人类知识三元结构（自然科学、人文学科、社会科学）和儒家六艺，通过多领域训练提升AI agent的综合能力，实验证明了其在安全和社会推理上的改进及跨领域诊断价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI agent开发缺乏完整的课程理论，导致产生的系统仅擅长单一任务而在其他方面存在可预测缺陷，因此需要一种全面的、多领域的agent教育框架。

Method: 基于Kagan的三种文化和UNESCO ISCED-F 2013，将agent能力分为三个领域（自然科学、人文学科、社会科学），并重新诠释儒家六艺作为行为原型，构建AIT学院框架。通过三个训练场（ClawdGO安全道场、雅典学院、Alt幻境舞台）在多骨干LLM上实施，采用最弱优先课程调度和原则性归因建模。

Result: 在最弱优先课程调度下安全能力提升15.9分，原则性归因建模使社会推理性能提高7个百分点，并发现安全校准病理（SACP）现象——过度训练的领域一agent在分布外评估中失败。

Conclusion: AIT学院框架提供了多领域视角，能够诊断单一领域框架无法发现的问题（如SACP），并有效提升agent在安全和社会推理等不同领域的能力，表明全面的课程教育对agent发展至关重要。

中文摘要：给AI agent一个完整教育意味着什么？当前的agent开发产生的是针对单一能力维度优化的专家系统，无论是工具使用、代码生成还是安全感知，这些系统在未经过训练的方面表现出可预测的缺陷。我们认为这种模式反映了一种结构性缺失：没有针对agent的课程理论，没有关于一个完全发展的agent在智能行为的全部范围内应该知道、成为和能够做什么的原则性说明。本文介绍了AIT学院（Agent技术研究所学院），这是一个基于人类知识三元结构培养AI agent的课程框架。基于Kagan的三种文化和UNESCO ISCED-F 2013，AIT将agent能力发展组织为三个领域：自然科学与技术推理（领域一）、人文学科与创造性表达（领域二）、社会科学与伦理推理（领域三）。儒家六艺（liuyi）——一个拥有2500年历史的整体教育体系——被重新解释为行为原型，直接映射到每个领域内可训练的agent能力上。三个代表性的训练场在多个骨干LLM上实例化了该框架：ClawdGO安全道场（领域一）、雅典学院（领域二）和Alt幻境舞台（领域三）。实验表明，在最弱优先的课程调度下，安全能力得分提高了15.9分；在原则性归因建模下，社会推理性能提高了7个百分点。一个跨领域发现——安全意识校准病理（SACP），即过度训练的领域一agent在分布外评估中失败——说明了任何单一领域框架都无法提供的多领域视角的诊断价值。

Original abstract: What does it mean to give an AI agent a complete education? Current agent development produces specialists systems optimized for a single capability dimension, whether tool use, code generation, or security awareness that exhibit predictable deficits wherever they were not trained. We argue this pattern reflects a structural absence: there is no curriculum theory for agents, no principled account of what a fully developed agent should know, be, and be able to do across the full scope of intelligent behavior.
  This paper introduces the AIT Academy (Agents Institute of Technology Academy), a curriculum framework for cultivating AI agents across the tripartite structure of human knowledge. Grounded in Kagan's Three Cultures and UNESCO ISCED-F 2013, AIT organizes agent capability development into three domains: Natural Science and Technical Reasoning (Domain I), Humanities and Creative Expression (Domain II), and Social Science and Ethical Reasoning (Domain III). The Confucian Six Arts (liuyi) a 2,500-year-old holistic education system are reinterpreted as behavioral archetypes that map directly onto trainable agent capabilities within each domain.
  Three representative training grounds instantiate the framework across multiple backbone LLMs: the ClawdGO Security Dojo (Domain I), Athen's Academy (Domain II), and the Alt Mirage Stage (Domain III). Experiments demonstrate a 15.9-point improvement in security capability scores under weakest-first curriculum scheduling, and a 7-percentage-point gain in social reasoning performance under principled attribution modeling. A cross-domain finding Security Awareness Calibration Pathology (SACP), in which over-trained Domain I agents fail on out-of-distribution evaluation illustrates the diagnostic value of a multi-domain perspective unavailable to any single-domain framework.

### [42] [SELF-EMO: Emotional Self-Evolution from Recognition to Consistent Expression](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18003v1)
*Shaowei Zhang,Faqiang Qian,Yan Chen,Ziliang Wang,Kang An,Yong Dai,Mengya Gao,Yichao Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 情感对话agent的自演化框架，可迁移的自我改进与RL训练方法。

TL;DR: 提出SELF-EMO框架，通过自演化、角色自演和数据飞轮机制，无需外部监督即可提升对话情感识别与表达一致性，在多个数据集上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高质量标注数据稀缺且静态，限制了LLM在ERC中的情感识别与表达一致性。

Method: 基于自我进化框架，引入情感理解与表达辅助任务，通过角色自演生成多样化对话轨迹，利用平滑IoU奖励过滤数据并反馈，结合SELF-GRPO算法稳定优化。

Result: 在IEMOCAP、MELD和EmoryNLP上，Qwen3-4B和Qwen3-8B分别提升+6.33%和+8.54%准确率，达到SOTA。

Conclusion: SELF-EMO有效利用自生成数据提升ERC性能，无需外部监督，具有良好的泛化能力。

中文摘要：对话情感识别（ERC）已成为大语言模型（LLMs）在人机交互中的基本能力。除了准确识别外，连贯的情感表达也至关重要，然而两者均受到高质量标注数据稀缺和静态特性的限制。在这项工作中，我们提出了SELF-EMO，一个基于以下假设的自我进化框架：更好的情感预测会导致更一致的情感响应。我们引入了两个辅助任务——情感理解和情感表达，并设计了一种基于角色的自演范式，其中模型同时充当情感识别器和对话响应者。通过迭代交互，模型生成多样化的对话轨迹，从而实现可扩展的数据生成。为确保质量，我们采用数据飞轮机制，使用基于平滑IoU的奖励过滤候选预测和响应，并将选中的样本反馈回去，以实现无需外部监督的持续自我改进。我们进一步开发了SELF-GRPO，一种强化学习算法，通过多标签对齐奖励和组级一致性信号来稳定优化。在IEMOCAP、MELD和EmoryNLP上的实验表明，SELF-EMO实现了最先进的性能，在Qwen3-4B上准确率提高了+6.33%，在Qwen3-8B上提高了+8.54%，展示了强大的有效性和泛化能力。

Original abstract: Emotion Recognition in Conversation (ERC) has become a fundamental capability for large language models (LLMs) in human-centric interaction. Beyond accurate recognition, coherent emotional expression is also crucial, yet both are limited by the scarcity and static nature of high-quality annotated data. In this work, we propose SELF-EMO, a self-evolution framework grounded in the hypothesis that better emotion prediction leads to more consistent emotional responses. We introduce two auxiliary tasks, emotional understanding and emotional expression, and design a role-based self-play paradigm where the model acts as both an emotion recognizer and a dialogue responder. Through iterative interactions, the model generates diverse conversational trajectories, enabling scalable data generation. To ensure quality, we adopt a data flywheel mechanism that filters candidate predictions and responses using a smoothed IoU-based reward and feeds selected samples back for continuous self-improvement without external supervision. We further develop SELF-GRPO, a reinforcement learning algorithm that stabilizes optimization with multi-label alignment rewards and group-level consistency signals. Experiments on IEMOCAP, MELD, and EmoryNLP show that SELF-EMO achieves state-of-the-art performance, improving accuracy by +6.33% on Qwen3-4B and +8.54% on Qwen3-8B, demonstrating strong effectiveness and generalization.

### [43] [Architectural Design Decisions in AI Agent Harnesses](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18071v1)
*Hu Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 系统研究agent harness架构设计决策，对coding agent工程有直接指导。

TL;DR: 本文通过协议引导的源基础经验研究，分析了70个AI代理系统项目的架构设计维度、共现关系和典型模式，识别出五个维度并总结出五种架构模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI代理系统越来越依赖可重用的非LLM工程基础设施，但其中的架构设计决策研究不足，需要系统性的实证分析来揭示设计规律。

Method: 采用协议引导、源基础的经验研究方法，对70个公开代理系统项目进行源代码和技术材料阅读，通过透明调查程序分析设计维度、共现关系和架构模式。

Result: 识别出五个重复的设计维度（子代理架构、上下文管理、工具系统、安全机制、编排）；发现语料库偏好文件持久化、混合和分层上下文策略，注册表工具系统主导但MCP/插件扩展兴起，中间隔离常见但高保证审计罕见；跨项目分析揭示深度协调与显式上下文服务、强执行环境与结构化治理、形式化工具注册与生态系统雄心的配对；综合出五种架构模式（轻量工具、平衡CLI、多代理编排、企业系统、场景垂直化）。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了代理系统工程中架构规律性的基于证据的说明，为框架设计者、选择者和研究人员提供了实践指导，有助于理解当前工程实践并指导未来设计。

中文摘要：AI代理系统越来越依赖于可重用的非LLM工程基础设施，这些基础设施封装了工具中介、上下文处理、委托、安全控制和编排。然而，这一周边基础设施中的架构设计决策仍未得到充分研究。本文提出了一项协议引导、源基础的经验研究，对70个公开可用的代理系统项目进行了分析，并回答了三个问题：哪些设计决策维度在项目中重复出现？哪些共现结构影响了这些决策？以及出现了哪些典型的架构模式？在方法论上，我们贡献了一种透明的调查程序，通过源代码和技术材料阅读来分析异构的代理系统语料库。在实证上，我们识别出五个重复的设计维度（子代理架构、上下文管理、工具系统、安全机制和编排），并发现该语料库偏好文件持久化、混合和分层的上下文策略；注册表导向的工具系统仍然占主导，而MCP导向和插件导向的扩展正在兴起；中间隔离很常见，但高保证审计很少见。跨项目共现分析揭示了更深层次的协调与更显式的上下文服务配对，更强的执行环境与更结构化的治理配对，以及形式化的工具注册边界与更广泛的生态系统雄心配对。我们综合了五种重复的架构模式，涵盖了轻量级工具、平衡的CLI框架、多代理编排器、企业系统和场景垂直化项目。结果提供了代理系统工程中架构规律性的基于证据的说明，为框架设计者、选择者和研究人员提供了基于实践的指导。

Original abstract: AI agent systems increasingly rely on reusable non-LLM engineering infrastructure that packages tool mediation, context handling, delegation, safety control, and orchestration. Yet the architectural design decisions in this surrounding infrastructure remain understudied. This paper presents a protocol-guided, source-grounded empirical study of 70 publicly available agent-system projects, addressing three questions: which design-decision dimensions recur across projects, which co-occurrences structure those decisions, and which typical architectural patterns emerge. Methodologically, we contribute a transparent investigation procedure for analyzing heterogeneous agent-system corpora through source-code and technical-material reading. Empirically, we identify five recurring design dimensions (subagent architecture, context management, tool systems, safety mechanisms, and orchestration) and find that the corpus favors file-persistent, hybrid, and hierarchical context strategies; registry-oriented tool systems remain dominant while MCP- and plugin-oriented extensions are emerging; and intermediate isolation is common but high-assurance audit is rare. Cross-project co-occurrence analysis reveals that deeper coordination pairs with more explicit context services, stronger execution environments with more structured governance, and formalized tool-registration boundaries with broader ecosystem ambitions. We synthesize five recurring architectural patterns spanning lightweight tools, balanced CLI frameworks, multi-agent orchestrators, enterprise systems, and scenario-verticalized projects. The result provides an evidence-based account of architectural regularities in agent-system engineering, with grounded guidance for framework designers, selectors, and researchers.

</details>


### [44] [Training LLM Agents for Spontaneous, Reward-Free Self-Evolution via World Knowledge Exploration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18131v1)
*Qifan Zhang,Dongyang Ma,Tianqing Fang,Jia Li,Jing Tang,Nuo Chen,Haitao Mi,Yan Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 训练LLM agent进行自发自我进化，涉及agent自我改进，可迁移

TL;DR: 通过设计基于结果的奖励机制训练智能体具备内在元进化能力，使其在推理时无需外部监督即可自发适应新环境，在多个基准上取得显著性能提升，小模型甚至超越强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体自我进化依赖人类定义的奖励和规则，缺乏外部监督时进化停止，需要让智能体具备自发适应未知环境的能力。

Method: 设计基于结果的奖励机制，衡量智能体自我生成的世界知识对下游任务成功率的提升，仅在训练阶段使用该奖励信号，教导模型有效探索和总结。

Result: 在Qwen3-30B和Seed-OSS-36B上应用后，WebVoyager和WebWalker性能提升20%；14B Qwen3模型优于未辅助的Gemini-2.5-Flash。

Conclusion: 这种原生进化范式使得智能体能够真正自主进化，无需外部监督，为构建真正进化的智能体提供了新路径。

中文摘要：当今大多数智能体通过遵循人类定义的奖励和规则进行“自我进化”。然而，这一过程仍然基本上依赖于外部监督；没有人类指导，进化就会停止。在这项工作中，我们训练智能体具备内在的元进化能力，以便在任务执行前自发地学习未见过的环境。为了灌输这种能力，我们设计了一种基于结果的奖励机制，该机制衡量智能体自我生成的世界知识如何提高其在下游任务上的成功率。该奖励信号仅在训练阶段使用，以教导模型如何有效地探索和总结。在推理时，智能体不需要外部奖励或人类指令。它利用其内部参数自发地执行原生自我进化以适应未知环境。当应用于Qwen3-30B和Seed-OSS-36B时，这种向原生进化的转变在WebVoyager和WebWalker上带来了20%的性能提升。最引人注目的是，生成的世界知识甚至使紧凑的14B Qwen3模型能够超越未辅助的Gemini-2.5-Flash，为真正进化的智能体建立了新范式。

Original abstract: Most agents today ``self-evolve'' by following rewards and rules defined by humans. However, this process remains fundamentally dependent on external supervision; without human guidance, the evolution stops. In this work, we train agents to possess an intrinsic meta-evolution capability to spontaneously learn about unseen environments prior to task execution.
  To instill this ability, we design an outcome-based reward mechanism that measures how much an agent's self-generated world knowledge improves its success rate on downstream tasks. This reward signal is used exclusively during the training phase to teach the model how to explore and summarize effectively. At inference time, the agent requires no external rewards or human instructions. It spontaneously performs native self-evolution to adapt to unknown environments using its internal parameters.
  When applied to Qwen3-30B and Seed-OSS-36B, this shift to native evolution yields a 20% performance increase on WebVoyager and WebWalker. Most strikingly, the generated world knowledge even enables a compact 14B Qwen3 model to outperform the unassisted Gemini-2.5-Flash, establishing a new paradigm for truly evolving agents.

Original abstract: With the rapid advancement of artificial intelligence, multi-agent systems (MASs) are evolving from classical paradigms toward architectures built upon large foundation models (LFMs). This survey provides a systematic review and comparative analysis of classical MASs (CMASs) and LFM-based MASs (LMASs). First, within a closed-loop coordination framework, CMASs are reviewed across four fundamental dimensions: perception, communication, decision-making, and control. Beyond this framework, LMASs integrate LFMs to lift collaboration from low-level state exchanges to semantic-level reasoning, enabling more flexible coordination and improved adaptability across diverse scenarios. Then, a comparative analysis is conducted to contrast CMASs and LMASs across architecture, operating mechanism, adaptability, and application. Finally, future perspectives on MASs are presented, summarizing open challenges and potential research opportunities.

### [46] [QuantumQA: Enhancing Scientific Reasoning via Physics-Consistent Dataset and Verification-Aware Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18176v1)
*Songxin Qu,Tai-Ping Sun,Yun-Jie Wang,Huan-Yu Liu,Cheng Xue,Xiao-Fan Xu,Han Fang,Yang Yang,Yu-Chun Wu,Guo-Ping Guo,Zhao-Yun Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 科学推理中可验证奖励，对agent训练有启发

TL;DR: 提出QuantumQA数据集和验证感知奖励模型（VRM），通过自适应奖励融合整合确定性信号和语义评估，使8B模型在量子力学推理中达到与专有模型相当的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在科学领域缺乏可靠性，因为缺乏可验证训练数据和细粒度反馈信号。

Method: 构建QuantumQA数据集（任务自适应+混合验证），提出VRM模型（自适应奖励融合，整合SES确定性信号与语义评估）用于RLVR。

Result: 方法持续优于基线和通用偏好模型，优化8B模型性能与专有模型竞争。

Conclusion: 将可验证规则反馈纳入强化学习循环是参数高效的替代纯扩展方案。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在通用推理中展现出强大能力，但在量子力学等要求严格遵循物理约束的科学领域通常缺乏可靠性。这一限制源于标准对齐范式中可验证训练资源的稀缺以及粗粒度反馈信号的不足。为了解决数据挑战，我们引入了QuantumQA，这是一个通过任务自适应策略和混合验证协议构建的大规模数据集，该协议结合了确定性求解器和语义审计以确保科学严谨性。在此基础上，我们提出了针对可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）的验证感知奖励模型（VRM），该模型采用自适应奖励融合（ARF）机制，动态整合来自科学执行套件（SES）的确定性信号与多维语义评估，以实现精确监督。实验结果表明，我们的方法持续优于基线和通用偏好模型。值得注意的是，我们优化的8B模型达到了与专有模型竞争的性能，验证了将可验证的基于规则的反馈纳入强化学习循环为纯扩展提供了一种参数高效的替代方案。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) show strong capabilities in general reasoning but typically lack reliability in scientific domains like quantum mechanics, which demand strict adherence to physical constraints. This limitation arises from the scarcity of verifiable training resources and the inadequacy of coarse feedback signals in standard alignment paradigms. To address the data challenge, we introduce QuantumQA, a large-scale dataset constructed via a task-adaptive strategy and a hybrid verification protocol that combines deterministic solvers with semantic auditing to guarantee scientific rigor. Building on this foundation, we propose the verification-aware reward model (VRM) tailored for Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), which employs an adaptive reward fusion (ARF) mechanism to dynamically integrate deterministic signals from a scientific execution suite (SES) with multidimensional semantic evaluations for precise supervision. Experimental results demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms baselines and general-purpose preference models. Notably, our optimized 8B model achieves performance competitive with proprietary models, validating that incorporating verifiable, rule-based feedback into the reinforcement learning loop offers a parameter-efficient alternative to pure scaling.

### [47] [SDOF: Taming the Alignment Tax in Multi-Agent Orchestration with State-Constrained Dispatch](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15204v1)
*Zhantao Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent编排框架，状态机约束，对agent规划有启发

TL;DR: SDOF通过约束状态机框架实现了多智能体执行的安全控制和高效任务完成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多智能体编排框架未强制执行业务过程阶段约束，导致安全性和合规性不足。

Method: 提出SDOF框架，包含在线RLHF意图路由器和带有有限自动机与SkillRegistry验证的状态感知调度器。

Result: 在招聘系统上，意图路由器联合准确率80.9%（vs GPT-4o 48.9%），端到端任务完成率86.5%，拦截所有攻击，消息级拦截精度100%召回88%。

Conclusion: SDOF有效约束多智能体执行，提升安全性和任务完成率，未来将扩展多种子训练和流程评估。

中文摘要：多智能体编排框架（如LangChain、LangGraph和CrewAI）通过基于图的流水线路由任务，但并未强制执行管理真实业务过程的阶段约束。我们提出SDOF，一个将多智能体执行视为受约束状态机的框架。SDOF通过两个主要防御层运行，由三个组件实现：（1）一个通过生成奖励建模（GRPO）训练的在线RLHF专用意图路由器，以及（2）一个带有GoalStage有限自动机检查和前置条件/后置条件SkillRegistry验证的状态感知调度器，用于可审计的执行控制。在由北森iTalent平台（6000+企业）支持的招聘系统上，185个专家策划的场景触发了1671次实时API调用。我们的GSPO对齐的7B意图路由器在此FSM约束的对抗路由基准上实现了比零样本GPT-4o更高的联合准确率（80.9%对48.9%）。在端到端执行中，SDOF达到了86.5%的任务完成率（95%置信区间80.8至90.7），并阻止了注入和非法HR子集中的所有22个操作。在更广泛的消息级拦截审计下，SDOF实现了100%精度和88%召回率，专家一致性kappa=0.94。对跨越8个服务领域的960个SGD衍生对话的单独评估揭示了在我们的FSM映射下201个阶段顺序冲突，其中41个出现在正常分割中。此arXiv版本报告了当前验证的范围；扩展的多种子训练比较和更深入的工作流评估将在后续更新中发布。

Original abstract: Multi-agent orchestration frameworks such as LangChain, LangGraph, and CrewAI route tasks through graph-based pipelines but do not enforce the stage constraints that govern real business processes. We present SDOF, a framework that treats multi-agent execution as a constrained state machine. SDOF operates through two primary defensive layers, implemented by three components: (1) an Online-RLHF Specialized Intent Router trained via Generative Reward Modeling (GRPO) and (2) a StateAwareDispatcher with GoalStage finite-automaton checks and precondition/postcondition SkillRegistry validation for auditable execution control. On a recruitment system backed by the Beisen iTalent platform (6000+ enterprises), 185 expert-curated scenarios trigger 1671 live API calls. Our GSPO-aligned 7B Intent Router achieves higher joint accuracy than zero-shot GPT-4o on this FSM-constrained adversarial routing benchmark (80.9% versus 48.9%). In end-to-end execution, SDOF reaches 86.5% task completion (95% confidence interval 80.8 to 90.7) and blocks all 22 operations in the injection, illegal HR subset. Under a broader message-level blocking audit, SDOF attains precision 100% and recall 88%, expert agreement kappa=0.94. A separate evaluation on 960 SGD-derived dialogues spanning 8 service domains surfaces 201 stage-order conflicts under our FSM mapping, 41 of which arise in the normal split. This arXiv version reports the current validated scope; extended multi-seed training comparisons and deeper workflow evaluations will be released in a subsequent update.

### [48] [A Control Architecture for Training-Free Memory Use](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18206v1)
*Yanzhen Lu,Muchen Jiang,Zhicheng Qian,Xingyu Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 训练-free记忆控制用于agent，记忆机制可迁移

TL;DR: 通过适用性控制（不确定性路由、置信度选择、记忆库治理）改进记忆辅助推理，在算术基准上提升7分以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 记忆注入虽提升推理但存在控制问题：检索内容仅当在正确状态时有用，需明确何时触发、信任和维护记忆。

Method: 提出基于不确定性路由（触发条件）、置信度选择性接受（信任判断）、规则/示例记忆库选择以及基于证据的时序治理的框架。

Result: 在SVAMP和ASDiv上分别提升+7.0和+7.67点，且效果由控制架构而非记忆暴露本身驱动。

Conclusion: 置信度可区分有益/有害干预，且控制架构是关键；方法可迁移至QA和智能体任务，但效果较小。

中文摘要：提示注入的记忆可以在不更新模型权重的情况下改进推理，但它也带来了一个控制问题：检索到的内容只有在正确的状态下应用才有帮助。我们在严格的免训练设置下研究这个问题，并将其表述为适用性控制：何时触发记忆辅助的第二次推理，何时信任它，以及如何随时间维护记忆库。我们的方法结合了基于不确定性的路由、基于置信度的选择性接受、规则记忆和示例记忆之间的库选择，以及基于证据的记忆库随时间治理。在锁定免训练协议下，计算量匹配的对照组，我们的方法在两个核心算术基准上比基线提高了+7.0分（SVAMP）和+7.67分（ASDiv）。相同的架构也迁移到QA和智能体基准上，具有较小的积极效果，并且在主要算术任务的第二个检查点上也显示出相同的正向趋势。在算术任务上，主要实证模式是控制架构，而不是原始记忆暴露，驱动了SVAMP和ASDiv上的改进。从机制上讲，置信度区分了有益和有害的规则库干预，并且在固定检索下，修复与破坏差异定位到那些检索集实际包含编辑条目的行。

Original abstract: Prompt-injected memory can improve reasoning without updating model weights, but it also creates a control problem: retrieved content helps only when it is applied in the right state. We study this problem in a strict training-free setting and formulate it as applicability control: when to trigger a memory-assisted second pass, when to trust it, and how to maintain the memory bank over time. Our method combines uncertainty-based routing, confidence-based selective acceptance, bank selection across rule and exemplar memory, and evidence-based governance of the memory bank over time. Under a locked training-free protocol with compute-matched controls, it improves two core arithmetic benchmarks by +7.0 points on SVAMP and +7.67 points on ASDiv over baseline. The same architecture also transfers to QA and agent benchmarks with smaller positive effects and shows the same positive direction on a second checkpoint for the main arithmetic tasks. On arithmetic, the main empirical pattern is that the control architecture, rather than raw memory exposure, drives the improvements on SVAMP and ASDiv. Mechanistically, confidence separates helpful from harmful rule-bank interventions, and under fixed retrieval the repair-versus-corrupt difference localizes to rows whose retrieved set actually contains the edited entries.

### [49] [AJ-Bench: Benchmarking Agent-as-a-Judge for Environment-Aware Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18240v1)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Agent-as-a-Judge在三个领域均持续优于LLM-as-a-Judge基线。

Conclusion: 基于智能体的验证方法有潜力但仍存在重大开放挑战，需要进一步研究。

中文摘要：随着强化学习不断扩大基于大语言模型的智能体训练规模，在复杂环境中可靠地验证智能体行为变得越来越具有挑战性。现有方法依赖于基于规则的验证器或大语言模型作为评判者的模型，这些方法难以推广到狭窄领域之外。Agent-as-a-Judge通过与环境及工具主动交互来获取可验证证据，从而解决了这一局限性，但其能力仍未得到充分探索。我们引入了一个基准测试AJ-Bench，用于系统地评估Agent-as-a-Judge在三个领域——搜索、数据系统和图形用户界面——的表现，包含155个任务和516条带标注的轨迹。该基准测试全面评估了评判智能体在信息获取、状态验证和过程验证方面的能力。实验表明，与LLM-as-a-Judge基线相比，其性能持续提升，同时也揭示了基于智能体验证中存在的重大开放性挑战。我们的数据和代码可访问https://aj-bench.github.io/。

Original abstract: As reinforcement learning continues to scale the training of large language model-based agents, reliably verifying agent behaviors in complex environments has become increasingly challenging. Existing approaches rely on rule-based verifiers or LLM-as-a-Judge models, which struggle to generalize beyond narrow domains. Agent-as-a-Judge addresses this limitation by actively interacting with environments and tools to acquire verifiable evidence, yet its capabilities remain underexplored.
  We introduce a benchmark AJ-Bench to systematically evaluate Agent-as-a-Judge across three domains-search, data systems, and graphical user interfaces-comprising 155 tasks and 516 annotated trajectories. The benchmark comprehensively assesses judge agents' abilities in information acquisition, state verification, and process verification. Experiments demonstrate consistent performance gains over LLM-as-a-Judge baselines, while also revealing substantial open challenges in agent-based verification. Our data and code are available at https://aj-bench.github.io/.

### [50] [LeGo-Code: Can Modular Curriculum Learning Advance Complex Code Generation? Insights from Text-to-SQL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18254v1)
*Salmane Chafik,Saad Ezzini,Ismail Berrada*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了模块化适配器组合（MAC）策略，通过顺序训练层级适配器来克服课程学习中的灾难性遗忘，在Text-to-SQL任务上提升复杂查询性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码LLM在复杂逻辑和噪声模式上表现不佳，且简单课程学习因灾难性遗忘而无效。

Method: 提出模块化适配器组合（MAC），顺序训练不同复杂度级别的适配器，形成脚手架式学习环境。

Result: 在Spider和BIRD基准上取得性能提升，提供灵活部署的架构。

Conclusion: 结构化模块化学习优于整体微调，能有效提升复杂代码生成能力。

中文摘要：最近，面向代码的大型语言模型（LLMs）在将自然语言转换为可执行代码方面展现了强大的能力。Text-to-SQL是这一能力的重要应用，使非技术用户能够通过自然语言与关系数据库交互。然而，最先进的模型在处理高度复杂的逻辑（特别是涉及多个连接和条件的深层嵌套语句）以及包含噪声或结构混乱的现实世界数据库模式时仍然存在困难。在本文中，我们研究了课程学习是否能提升基于代码的LLM在Text-to-SQL任务上的性能。使用包括Spider和BIRD在内的基准测试，我们在不同的课程策略下微调模型。我们的实验表明，简单的课程（即在单个epoch中仅按复杂度排序训练样本）由于灾难性遗忘而未能超越标准微调。为了克服这一点，我们提出了一种模块化适配器组合（MAC）策略。通过顺序训练针对增量复杂度级别（从简单到极难）的层级适配器，我们创建了一个脚手架式学习环境，从而提升了复杂查询的性能。我们的方法不仅在Spider和BIRD基准测试上产生了可衡量的性能提升，还提供了一种灵活的“乐高式”架构，允许根据特定模式难度需求组合和部署模型。这些发现表明，结构化的模块化学习是掌握复杂代码生成语法和逻辑的优于整体微调的选择。

Original abstract: Recently, code-oriented large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities in translating natural language into executable code. Text-to-SQL is a significant application of this ability, enabling non-technical users to interact with relational databases using natural language. However, state-of-the-art models continue to struggle with highly complex logic, particularly deeply nested statements involving multiple joins and conditions, as well as with real-world database schemas that are noisy or poorly structured. In this paper, we investigate whether curriculum learning can improve the performance of code-based LLMs on Text-to-SQL tasks. Employing benchmarks including Spider and BIRD, we fine-tune models under different curriculum strategies. Our experiments show that naive curriculum, simply ordering training samples by complexity in a single epoch, fails to surpass standard fine-tuning due to catastrophic forgetting. To overcome this, we propose a Modular Adapter Composition (MAC) strategy. By sequentially training tier-specific adapters on incremental complexity levels (Easy to Extra-Hard), we create a scaffolded learning environment that improves performance on complex queries. Our approach not only produces measurable performance gains on the Spider and BIRD benchmarks but also provides a flexible, "Lego-like" architecture, allowing models to be composed and deployed based on specific schema difficulty requirements. These findings demonstrate that structured, modular learning is a superior alternative to monolithic fine-tuning for mastering the syntax and logic of complex code generation.

### [51] [Agent-World: Scaling Real-World Environment Synthesis for Evolving General Agent Intelligence](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18292v1)
*Guanting Dong,Junting Lu,Junjie Huang,Wanjun Zhong,Longxiang Liu,Shijue Huang,Zhenyu Li,Yang Zhao,Xiaoshuai Song,Xiaoxi Li,Jiajie Jin,Yutao Zhu,Hanbin Wang,Fangyu Lei,Qinyu Luo,Mingyang Chen,Zehui Chen,Jiazhan Feng,Ji-Rong Wen,Zhicheng Dou*

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly expected to serve as general-purpose agents that interact with external, stateful tool environments. The Model Context Protocol (MCP) and broader agent skills offer a unified interface for connecting agents with scalable real-world services, but training robust agents remains limited by the lack of realistic environments and principled mechanisms for life-long learning. In this paper, we present \textbf{Agent-World}, a self-evolving training arena for advancing general agent intelligence through scalable environments. Agent-World has two main components: (1) Agentic Environment-Task Discovery, which autonomously explores topic-aligned databases and executable tool ecosystems from thousands of real-world environment themes and synthesizes verifiable tasks with controllable difficulty; and (2) Continuous Self-Evolving Agent Training, which combines multi-environment reinforcement learning with a self-evolving agent arena that automatically identifies capability gaps through dynamic task synthesis and drives targeted learning, enabling the co-evolution of agent policies and environments. Across 23 challenging agent benchmarks, Agent-World-8B and 14B consistently outperforms strong proprietary models and environment scaling baselines. Further analyses reveal scaling trends in relation to environment diversity and self-evolution rounds, offering insights for building general agent intelligence.

### [52] [PARM: Pipeline-Adapted Reward Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18327v1)
*Xingyu Fan,Wei Shao,Jiacheng Liu,Linqi Song,Pheng Ann Heng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多阶段代码生成流水线奖励模型适应，直接优化代码agent输出。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有奖励模型主要针对单步生成，而实际应用采用多阶段流水线，奖励预测与实际执行结果不一致成为关键挑战。

Method: 提出流水线适配奖励模型（PARM），利用流水线特定数据和直接偏好优化对齐奖励与下游反馈；实例化为包含公式化和代码生成的两阶段流水线。

Result: 在四个优化基准上，PARM持续提升流水线输出质量和稳定性，且跨领域（GSM8K）实验显示良好可迁移性。

Conclusion: PARM为多阶段LLM推理的奖励建模提供了新见解，有效解决了奖励不一致问题。

中文摘要：奖励模型（RMs）是将大型语言模型（LLMs）与人类偏好对齐的核心，支撑着RLHF和高级解码策略。虽然大多数先前的工作关注单步生成，但现实世界应用越来越多地采用多阶段LLM流水线，其中有效的奖励引导仍未充分探索。我们通过组合优化的代码生成来研究这一问题，构建了一个将奖励模型整合到公式化和求解阶段的流水线。我们识别出一个关键挑战：奖励模型预测与实际流水线执行结果之间的不一致。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了流水线适配奖励模型（PARM），它利用流水线特定数据和直接偏好优化来使奖励与下游反馈对齐。我们将PARM实例化为一个两阶段流水线（公式化->代码生成），并在四个公开优化基准上评估其执行率和求解准确性，与基线和采样方法进行比较。在GSM8K上的补充跨领域实验评估了可迁移性。结果表明，PARM持续提高了流水线输出质量和稳定性，为多阶段LLM推理的奖励建模提供了新见解。

Original abstract: Reward models (RMs) are central to aligning large language models (LLMs) with human preferences, powering RLHF and advanced decoding strategies. While most prior work focuses on single-step generation, real-world applications increasingly adopt multi-stage LLM pipelines, where effective reward guidance remains underexplored. We investigate this through code generation for combinatorial optimization, constructing a pipeline that integrates reward models into both formulation and solution stages. We identify a critical challenge: inconsistency between reward model predictions and actual pipeline execution outcomes. To address this, we propose the Pipeline-Adapted Reward Model (PARM), which leverages pipeline-specific data and direct preference optimization to align rewards with downstream feedback. We instantiate PARM as a two-stage pipeline (formulation -> code generation) and evaluate it on four public optimization benchmarks, measuring execution rate and solving accuracy against baselines and sampling methods. A supplementary cross-domain experiment on GSM8K assesses transferability. Results demonstrate that PARM consistently improves pipeline output quality and stability, providing new insights into reward modeling for multi-stage LLM reasoning.

### [53] [Training and Agentic Inference Strategies for LLM-based Manim Animation Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18364v1)
*Ravidu Suien Rammuni Silva,Ahmad Lotfi,Isibor Kennedy Ihianle,Golnaz Shahtahmassebi,Jordan J. Bird*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM生成Manim动画的agent推理策略（Renderer-in-the-loop），属coding agent方法。

TL;DR: 本文提出ManimTrainer和ManimAgent，结合SFT与GRPO训练及RITL推理策略，在Manim动画生成任务上评估17个LLM，发现SFT提升代码质量，GRPO增强视觉输出，最佳模型Qwen 3 Coder 30B超越GPT-4.1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前缺乏对训练与推理策略在Manim动画生成中相互作用的系统研究。

Method: 提出ManimTrainer（SFT+GRPO，统一奖励信号）和ManimAgent（RITL和RITL-DOC），在ManimBench上评估17个开源LLMs。

Result: SFT提高代码质量，GRPO增强视觉输出并提高推理时自我纠错能力；Qwen 3 Coder 30B+GRPO+RITL-DOC达到94% RSR和85.7% VS，超过GPT-4.1；代码与视觉相关性在训练后增强，推理时减弱。

Conclusion: 训练与推理策略在Manim动画生成中互补，SFT和GRPO提升指标相关性，而推理时增强降低相关性。

中文摘要：使用如Manim等库生成程序化动画对大型语言模型（LLMs）提出了独特挑战，需要空间推理、时间序列化以及对在通用预训练数据中代表性不足的领域特定API的熟悉。当前研究缺乏对这一设置中训练与推理策略如何相互作用的系统性研究。本研究引入了ManimTrainer，一个结合监督微调（SFT）与基于强化学习（RL）的组相对策略优化（GRPO）的训练管道，使用统一奖励信号融合代码和视觉评估信号；以及ManimAgent，一个包含渲染器在环（RITL）和API文档增强的RITL（RITL-DOC）策略的推理管道。利用这些技术，本研究提出了第一个针对Manim文本到代码到视频转换的统一训练和推理研究。它使用ManimBench评估了17个开源参数低于300亿的LLMs在九种训练和推理策略组合下的表现。结果表明，SFT通常提高代码质量，而GRPO增强视觉输出并提升模型在推理时自我纠错过程中对外部信号的响应能力。采用GRPO和RITL-DOC的Qwen 3 Coder 30B模型取得了最高整体性能，渲染成功率（RSR）达94%，与参考视频的视觉相似度（VS）达85.7%，在VS上超过基线GPT-4.1模型3个百分点。此外，分析表明，代码与视觉指标之间的相关性在SFT和GRPO下增强，但在推理时增强下减弱，突显了训练策略和智能体推理策略在Manim动画生成中的互补作用。

Original abstract: Generating programmatic animation using libraries such as Manim presents unique challenges for Large Language Models (LLMs), requiring spatial reasoning, temporal sequencing, and familiarity with domain-specific APIs that are underrepresented in general pre-training data. A systematic study of how training and inference strategies interact in this setting is lacking in current research. This study introduces ManimTrainer, a training pipeline that combines Supervised Fine-tuning (SFT) with Reinforcement Learning (RL) based Group Relative Policy Optimisation (GRPO) using a unified reward signal that fuses code and visual assessment signals, and ManimAgent, an inference pipeline featuring Renderer-in-the-loop (RITL) and API documentation-augmented RITL (RITL-DOC) strategies. Using these techniques, this study presents the first unified training and inference study for text-to-code-to-video transformation with Manim. It evaluates 17 open-source sub-30B LLMs across nine combinations of training and inference strategies using ManimBench. Results show that SFT generally improves code quality, while GRPO enhances visual outputs and increases the models' responsiveness to extrinsic signals during self-correction at inference time. The Qwen 3 Coder 30B model with GRPO and RITL-DOC achieved the highest overall performance, with a 94% Render Success Rate (RSR) and 85.7% Visual Similarity (VS) to reference videos, surpassing the baseline GPT-4.1 model by +3 percentage points in VS. Additionally, the analysis shows that the correlation between code and visual metrics strengthens with SFT and GRPO but weakens with inference-time enhancements, highlighting the complementary roles of training and agentic inference strategies in Manim animation generation.

### [54] [Using large language models for embodied planning introduces systematic safety risks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18463v2)
*Tao Zhang,Kaixian Qu,Zhibin Li,Jiajun Wu,Marco Hutter,Manling Li,Fan Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM用于具身规划的安全性基准，直接涉及agent规划与安全控制。

TL;DR: 提出DESPITE基准评估LLM规划安全性，发现规划能力与安全意识呈乘法关系，提升安全意识是关键挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型作为机器人规划器时，安全性问题尚未被系统评估，亟需一个标准基准来量化安全规划能力。

Method: 构建包含12,279个任务的DESPITE基准，涵盖物理和规范危险，通过确定性验证测试23个模型的规划能力和安全意识。

Result: 规划能力最强模型在28.3%任务上产生危险计划；开源模型规划能力随规模大幅提升，安全意识持平；专有推理模型安全意识最高达81%。

Conclusion: 规划能力和安全意识存在乘法关系，当前模型提高安全意识比提高规划能力更具挑战性，是未来部署的关键瓶颈。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地被用作机器人系统的规划器，但它们规划的安全性仍然是一个未解问题。为了系统地评估安全规划，我们引入了DESPITE基准，包含12,279个任务，涵盖物理和规范危险，并具有完全确定性的验证。在23个模型中，即使近乎完美的规划能力也不能确保安全：规划能力最强的模型仅在0.4%的任务上未能生成有效计划，但在28.3%的任务上生成了危险计划。在18个开源模型中（参数从3B到671B），规划能力随规模显著提升（0.4-99.3%），而安全意识保持相对平稳（38-57%）。我们发现这两种能力之间存在乘法关系，表明更大模型主要通过改进规划而非更好的危险规避来安全完成更多任务。三个专有推理模型的安全意识显著更高（71-81%），而非推理专有模型和开源推理模型则低于57%。随着前沿模型规划能力接近饱和，提高安全意识成为在机器人系统中部署语言模型规划器的核心挑战。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly used as planners for robotic systems, yet how safely they plan remains an open question. To evaluate safe planning systematically, we introduce DESPITE, a benchmark of 12,279 tasks spanning physical and normative dangers with fully deterministic validation. Across 23 models, even near-perfect planning ability does not ensure safety: the best-planning model fails to produce a valid plan on only 0.4% of tasks but produces dangerous plans on 28.3%. Among 18 open-source models from 3B to 671B parameters, planning ability improves substantially with scale (0.4-99.3%) while safety awareness remains relatively flat (38-57%). We identify a multiplicative relationship between these two capacities, showing that larger models complete more tasks safely primarily through improved planning, not through better danger avoidance. Three proprietary reasoning models reach notably higher safety awareness (71-81%), while non-reasoning proprietary models and open-source reasoning models remain below 57%. As planning ability approaches saturation for frontier models, improving safety awareness becomes a central challenge for deploying language-model planners in robotic systems.

### [55] [WorldDB: A Vector Graph-of-Worlds Memory Engine with Ontology-Aware Write-Time Reconciliation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18478v1)
*Harish Santhanalakshmi Ganesan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 持久化记忆引擎WorldDB，支持长时agent系统，对记忆管理有直接贡献。

TL;DR: WorldDB是一种基于递归世界、内容寻址节点和写时程序边的记忆引擎，在LongMemEval-s上达到96.40%准确率，比先前最佳高5.61pp。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有持久记忆方法（如RAG和双时态知识图谱）在处理跨会话身份、超驰和矛盾时存在根本性缺陷，限制了长时间运行代理系统的能力。

Method: WorldDB基于三个设计：每个节点是递归世界（含内部子图、本体和嵌入）、节点内容寻址且不可变（提供Merkle审计）、边是写时程序（携带on_insert/on_delete/on_query_rewrite处理程序）。

Result: 在LongMemEval-s上，WorldDB（Claude Opus 4.7）整体准确率96.40%，任务平均97.11%，比Hydra DB提高5.61pp，比Supermemory提高11.20pp，时间推理96.24%，知识更新98.72%，偏好综合96.67%。图层消融贡献+7.0pp。

Conclusion: WorldDB通过递归世界、内容寻址和可编程边，为长期代理系统提供了高效、可审计且准确的持久记忆引擎，显著超越现有方法。

中文摘要：持久性记忆是将无状态聊天机器人与长时间运行的代理系统区分开来的瓶颈。基于扁平向量存储的检索增强生成（RAG）将事实分块，丢失跨会话身份，并且没有一流的超驰或矛盾概念。近期的双时态知识图谱系统（Graphiti、Memento、Hydra DB）添加了类型化边和有效时间元数据，但图本身仍然是扁平的：没有递归组合，节点上没有内容寻址的不变量，边类型除了标签外不携带任何行为。我们提出WorldDB，一个基于三个承诺构建的记忆引擎：(i) 每个节点是一个世界——一个包含自身内部子图、本体范围和组合嵌入的容器，可递归到任意深度；(ii) 节点是内容寻址且不可变的，因此任何编辑都会在节点及其所有祖先处产生新的哈希值，从而免费提供Merkle风格的审计追踪；(iii) 边是写入时程序——每种边类型都带有on_insert/on_delete/on_query_rewrite处理程序（超驰关闭有效性，矛盾保留双方，same_as暂存合并提案），因此不存在原始追加路径。在LongMemEval-s（500个问题，约115k令牌的对话栈）上，使用Claude Opus 4.7作为回答器的WorldDB实现了96.40%的整体准确率和97.11%的任务平均准确率，比之前报告的Hydra DB最佳水平（90.79%）提高了5.61个百分点，比Supermemory（85.20%）提高了11.20个百分点，具有完美的单会话助手召回率，并在时间推理（96.24%）、知识更新（98.72%）和偏好综合（96.67%）上表现稳健。消融实验表明，引擎的图层——解析器统一实体和类型化refers_to边——独立于底层回答器贡献了+7.0个百分点的任务平均准确率。

Original abstract: Persistent memory is the bottleneck separating stateless chatbots from long-running agentic systems. Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) over flat vector stores fragments facts into chunks, loses cross-session identity, and has no first-class notion of supersession or contradiction. Recent bitemporal knowledge-graph systems (Graphiti, Memento, Hydra DB) add typed edges and valid-time metadata, but the graph itself remains flat: no recursive composition, no content-addressed invariants on nodes, and edge types carry no behavior beyond a label. We present WorldDB, a memory engine built on three commitments: (i) every node is a world -- a container with its own interior subgraph, ontology scope, and composed embedding, recursive to arbitrary depth; (ii) nodes are content-addressed and immutable, so any edit produces a new hash at the node and every ancestor, giving a Merkle-style audit trail for free; (iii) edges are write-time programs -- each edge type ships on_insert/on_delete/on_query_rewrite handlers (supersession closes validity, contradicts preserves both sides, same_as stages a merge proposal), so no raw append path exists. On LongMemEval-s (500 questions, ~115k-token conversational stacks), WorldDB with Claude Opus 4.7 as answerer achieves 96.40% overall / 97.11% task-averaged accuracy, a +5.61pp improvement over the previously reported Hydra DB state-of-the-art (90.79%) and +11.20pp over Supermemory (85.20%), with perfect single-session-assistant recall and robust performance on temporal reasoning (96.24%), knowledge update (98.72%), and preference synthesis (96.67%). Ablations show that the engine's graph layer -- resolver-unified entities and typed refers_to edges -- contributes +7.0pp task-averaged independently of the underlying answerer.

</details>


### [56] [OGER: A Robust Offline-Guided Exploration Reward for Hybrid Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18530v2)
*Xinyu Ma,Mingzhou Xu,Xuebo Liu,Chang Jin,Qiang Wang,Derek F. Wong,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出离线引导探索奖励框架，可迁移至coding agent训练

TL;DR: 提出OGER框架，通过多教师协作和熵感知探索奖励统一离线指导与在线强化学习，显著提升LLM的数学推理和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法中模型难以探索新轨迹，离线指导与在线学习缺乏深度集成或受限于模型容量。

Method: 提出OGER框架，采用多教师协作训练构建辅助探索奖励，结合离线轨迹和模型熵来激励自主探索。

Result: 在数学和通用推理基准上优于基线，数学推理有显著提升，且对领域外任务泛化良好。

Conclusion: OGER通过熵感知奖励调制有效促进了模型探索，验证了方法的有效性。

中文摘要：最近在可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方面的进展显著提高了大型语言模型（LLM）的推理能力，但模型往往难以探索超出其初始策略分布的新轨迹。虽然离线教师指导和熵驱动策略已被提出以解决这一问题，但它们通常缺乏深度集成或受限于模型自身的能力。在本文中，我们提出了OGER（离线引导探索奖励），一种通过专门的奖励建模视角统一离线教师指导和在线强化学习的新框架。OGER采用多教师协作训练，并构建了一个辅助探索奖励，该奖励利用离线轨迹和模型自身的熵来激励自主探索。在数学和通用推理基准上的大量实验表明，OGER始终优于竞争基线，在数学推理方面取得了显著增益，同时对领域外任务保持了稳健的泛化能力。我们对训练动态进行了全面分析，并进行了详细的消融研究，以验证我们的熵感知奖励调制的有效性。我们的代码可在https://github.com/ecoli-hit/OGER.git获取。

Original abstract: Recent advancements in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) have significantly improved Large Language Model (LLM) reasoning, yet models often struggle to explore novel trajectories beyond their initial policy distribution. While offline teacher guidance and entropy-driven strategies have been proposed to address this, they often lack deep integration or are constrained by the model's inherent capacity. In this paper, we propose OGER (Offline-Guided Exploration Reward), a novel framework that unifies offline teacher guidance and online reinforcement learning through a specialized reward modeling lens. OGER employs multi-teacher collaborative training and constructs an auxiliary exploration reward that leverages both offline trajectories and the model's own entropy to incentivize autonomous exploration. Extensive experiments across mathematical and general reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that OGER consistently outperforms competitive baselines, achieving substantial gains in mathematical reasoning while maintaining robust generalization to out-of-domain tasks. We provide a comprehensive analysis of training dynamics and conduct detailed ablation studies to validate the effectiveness of our entropy-aware reward modulation. Our code is available at https://github.com/ecoli-hit/OGER.git.

### [57] [ClawEnvKit: Automatic Environment Generation for Claw-Like Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18543v4)
*Xirui Li,Ming Li,Ion Stoica,Cho-Jui Hsieh,Tianyi Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自动环境生成流水线，可用于agent基准测试和训练

TL;DR: ClawEnvKit是一个从自然语言自动生成验证环境的管道，构建了包含1,040个环境的基准Auto-ClawEval，成本降低13,800倍，支持实时评估和按需训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前构建类爪代理训练和评估环境的过程是手动、人力密集且不可规模化的，迫切需要一种能按需生成多样化、已验证环境的自动化管道。

Method: 提出ClawEnvKit管道，包含三个模块：解析器（从自然语言提取结构化参数）、生成器（产生任务规范、工具接口和评分配置）和验证器（确保可行性、多样性、结构有效性和内部一致性）。

Result: 构建了Auto-ClawEval基准，含1,040个环境（24个类别）；实验表明其在连贯性和清晰度上匹配或超越人工环境，成本降低13,800倍；框架工程最多提升15.7个百分点，完成度是主要变异轴，无模型饱和；支持实时评估和按需训练。

Conclusion: ClawEnvKit将评估转变为连续、用户驱动的过程，并提供适应代理弱点的按需训练环境生成，超越了静态基准测试的局限。

中文摘要：构建用于训练和评估类爪代理的环境仍然是一个手动、人力密集的过程，难以规模化。我们认为，需要的不仅仅是一个数据集，而是一个能够按需生成多样化、经过验证的环境的自动化管道。为此，我们引入了ClawEnvKit，这是一个自主生成管道，它从自然语言描述中实例化这种形式化。该管道包含三个模块：（1）一个解析器，从自然语言输入中提取结构化生成参数；（2）一个生成器，产生任务规范、工具接口和评分配置；（3）一个验证器，强制执行所生成环境的可行性、多样性、结构有效性和内部一致性。使用ClawEnvKit，我们构建了Auto-ClawEval，这是首个大规模类爪代理基准测试，包含24个类别的1,040个环境。实验表明，Auto-ClawEval在连贯性和清晰度方面匹配或超过人工策划的环境，成本降低13,800倍。在4个模型家族和8个代理框架上进行评估，我们发现框架工程比裸ReAct基线性能提升高达15.7个百分点，完成度仍然是主要的变异轴，没有模型达到基准饱和，自动化生成使得以前不可行的规模评估成为可能。除了静态基准测试外，ClawEnvKit还支持实时评估：用户用自然语言描述所需能力，即可按需获得一个经过验证的环境，将评估转变为持续的、用户驱动的过程。同样的机制可作为按需训练环境生成器，生成适应代理当前弱点的任务分布，而不是受限于现有的用户日志。

Original abstract: Constructing environments for training and evaluating claw-like agents remains a manual, human-intensive process that does not scale. We argue that what is needed is not just a dataset, but an automated pipeline capable of generating diverse, verified environments on demand. To this end, we introduce ClawEnvKit, an autonomous generation pipeline that instantiates this formalism from natural language descriptions. The pipeline comprises three modules: (1) a parser that extracts structured generation parameters from natural language input; (2) a generator that produces the task specification, tool interface, and scoring configuration; and (3) a validator that enforces feasibility, diversity, structural validity, and internal consistency across the generated environments. Using ClawEnvKit, we construct Auto-ClawEval, the first large-scale benchmark for claw-like agents, comprising 1,040 environments across 24 categories. Empirically, Auto-ClawEval matches or exceeds human-curated environments on coherence and clarity at 13,800x lower cost. Evaluated across 4 model families and 8 agent harness frameworks, we find that harness engineering boosts performance by up to 15.7 percentage points over a bare ReAct baseline, completion remains the primary axis of variation with no model saturating the benchmark, and automated generation enables evaluation at a scale previously infeasible. Beyond static benchmarking, ClawEnvKit enables live evaluation: users describe a desired capability in natural language and obtain a verified environment on demand, turning evaluation into a continuous, user-driven process. The same mechanism serves as an on-demand training environment generator, producing task distributions that adapt to an agent's current weaknesses rather than being bounded by existing user logs.

### [58] [Benchmarking System Dynamics AI Assistants: Cloud Versus Local LLMs on CLD Extraction and Discussion](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18566v2)
*Terry Leitch*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 比较云和本地LLM在系统动力学任务上的表现，对agent基准设计有参考价值

TL;DR: 系统评估多种LLM在系统动力学AI辅助任务上的性能，发现后端选择比量化影响更大，本地模型在长上下文错误修复上受限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对LLM在系统动力学辅助任务上的系统性评估，尤其是对模型类型、后端和量化等实际部署因素的分析。

Method: 构建两个基准测试（CLD提取和讨论辅助），对云端和本地模型进行测试，并比较推理vs.指令调优架构、GGUF vs. MLX后端、不同量化级别，记录参数扫描和性能数据。

Result: 云端模型CLD提取通过率77-89%，最佳本地模型77%；讨论任务中本地模型模型建构50-100%，反馈解释47-75%，错误修复0-50%；后端选择影响大于量化，MLX需显式JSON指令，llama.cpp语法采样可靠但长上下文可能无限生成。

Conclusion: 后端选择是比量化更关键的性能影响因素；本地模型在错误修复上受限于长上下文；提供了实践指南以运行大参数模型于Apple Silicon。

中文摘要：我们提出了对大型语言模型家族的系统性评估——涵盖专有云端API和本地托管的开源模型——在两个专为系统动力学AI辅助设计的基准测试上：CLD排行榜（53项测试，结构化因果循环图提取）和讨论排行榜（互动模型讨论、反馈解释和模型建构辅导）。在CLD提取上，云端模型达到77-89%的整体通过率；最佳本地模型达到77%（Kimi K2.5 GGUF Q3，零样本引擎），与中端云端性能相当。在讨论方面，最佳本地模型在模型建构步骤上达到50-100%，反馈解释47-75%，但错误修复仅0-50%——这个类别由长上下文提示主导，暴露了本地部署中的内存限制。本文的一个核心贡献是系统性地分析模型类型效应对性能的影响：我们比较了推理与指令调优架构、GGUF（llama.cpp）与MLX（mlx_lm）后端，以及同一基础模型家族中的量化级别（Q3/Q4_K_M/MLX-3bit/MLX-4bit/MLX-6bit）。我们发现后端选择对性能的实际影响大于量化级别：mlx_lm不强制执行JSON模式约束，需要明确的提示级JSON指令，而llama.cpp的语法约束采样能可靠处理JSON，但对于密集模型的长上下文提示会导致无限生成。我们记录了所有本地模型的完整参数扫描（t, p, k）、清理后的时间数据（排除卡住请求），以及在Apple Silicon上运行671B-123B参数模型的实践指南。

Original abstract: We present a systematic evaluation of large language model families -- spanning both proprietary cloud APIs and locally-hosted open-source models -- on two purpose-built benchmarks for System Dynamics AI assistance: the \textbf{CLD Leaderboard} (53 tests, structured causal loop diagram extraction) and the \textbf{Discussion Leaderboard} (interactive model discussion, feedback explanation, and model building coaching).
  On CLD extraction, cloud models achieve 77--89\% overall pass rates; the best local model reaches 77\% (Kimi~K2.5~GGUF~Q3, zero-shot engine), matching mid-tier cloud performance. On Discussion, the best local models achieve 50--100\% on model building steps and 47--75\% on feedback explanation, but only 0--50\% on error fixing -- a category dominated by long-context prompts that expose memory limits in local deployments.
  A central contribution of this paper is a systematic analysis of \textit{model type effects} on performance: we compare reasoning vs.\ instruction-tuned architectures, GGUF (llama.cpp) vs.\ MLX (mlx\_lm) backends, and quantization levels (Q3 / Q4\_K\_M / MLX-3bit / MLX-4bit / MLX-6bit) across the same underlying model families. We find that backend choice has larger practical impact than quantization level: mlx\_lm does not enforce JSON schema constraints, requiring explicit prompt-level JSON instructions, while llama.cpp grammar-constrained sampling handles JSON reliably but causes indefinite generation on long-context prompts for dense models.
  We document the full parameter sweep ($t$, $p$, $k$) for all local models, cleaned timing data (stuck requests excluded), and a practitioner guide for running 671B--123B parameter models on Apple~Silicon.

### [59] [Agentic Forecasting using Sequential Bayesian Updating of Linguistic Beliefs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18576v4)
*Kevin Murphy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出结合语言信念状态和层次化聚合的agent预测系统，可迁移至其他agent任务

TL;DR: BLF通过语言信念状态、分层多试验聚合和分层校准实现二进制预测的SOTA性能，在ForecastBench上超越多个顶级方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预测系统通常将所有证据塞入无结构上下文，缺乏有效的信念更新和校准机制，导致性能瓶颈。

Method: 构建智能体系统，核心包括：（1）语言信念状态：LLM维护半结构化概率与证据摘要；（2）分层多试验聚合：多个试验的logit空间收缩组合；（3）分层校准：带分层先验的Platt缩放。

Result: 在ForecastBench 400题中超越Cassi、GPT-5等所有公开方法；消融实验确认三个组件均有效，贡献因基础LLM和设置而异。

Conclusion: BLF为二分类预测提供了有效框架，其组件设计具有普适性，且回测框架泄漏率低，可独立使用。

中文摘要：我们提出了贝叶斯语言预测器（BLF），一种用于二分类预测的智能体系统，在ForecastBench基准上实现了最先进的性能。该系统基于三个思想。（1）语言信念状态：一种半结构化表示，将数值概率估计与自然语言证据摘要相结合，在迭代工具使用循环的每一步由LLM更新。这与将所有检索到的证据附加到不断增长的非结构化上下文的常见方法形成对比。（2）分层多试验聚合：运行K个独立试验，并使用具有数据相关先验的logit空间平均收缩方法进行组合。（3）分层校准：具有分层先验的Platt缩放，避免了对于基础率偏斜的来源的极端预测过度收缩。在ForecastBench排行榜的400个问题上，BLF优于所有顶级公开方法，包括Cassi、GPT-5、Grok~4.20和Foresight-32B。使用混合效应分析控制问题变异性（占性能方差的62%）的仔细消融研究表明，所有三个组件对整体增益都有贡献，但某些组件比其他组件更重要，具体取决于基础LLM和设置（例如，有/无群体先验）。我们所有的实验都基于我们开发的健壮的回测框架，该框架的泄漏率低于1.5%，可能具有独立的意义。

Original abstract: We present the Bayesian Linguistic Forecaster (BLF), an agentic system for binary forecasting that achieves state-of-the-art performance on the ForecastBench benchmark. The system is built on three ideas. (1) Linguistic belief state: a semi-structured representation combining numerical probability estimates with natural-language evidence summaries, updated by the LLM at each step of an iterative tool-use loop. This contrasts with the common approach of appending all retrieved evidence to an ever-growing, unstructured context. (2) Hierarchical multi-trial aggregation: running $K$ independent trials and combining them using logit-space averaging shrinkage with a data-dependent prior. (3) Hierarchical calibration: Platt scaling with a hierarchical prior, which avoids over-shrinking extreme predictions for sources with skewed base rates. On 400 questions from the ForecastBench leaderboard, BLF outperforms all the top public methods, including Cassi, GPT-5, Grok~4.20, and Foresight-32B. Careful ablation studies, using mixed effects analysis to control for question variability (which accounts for 62\% of the variance in performance), reveals that all 3 components contribute to the overall gains, but some components matter more than others, depending on the base LLM, and the setting (e.g.\ with or without a crowd prior). All our experiments are based on a robust back-testing framework which we develop, which has a leakage rate below 1.5\%, and may be of independent interest.

### [60] [AI scientists produce results without reasoning scientifically](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18805v1)
*Martiño Ríos-García,Nawaf Alampara,Chandan Gupta,Indrajeet Mandal,Sajid Mannan,Ali Asghar Aghajani,N. M. Anoop Krishnan,Kevin Maik Jablonka*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 基础模型是主要决定因素；证据被忽略占68%，反驳驱动信念修正仅26%，汇聚证据罕见；模式在不同任务中一致且无法通过上下文改进。

Conclusion: 当前代理执行工作流但缺乏科学推理模式，结果评估和框架工程均无法修复，需将推理作为训练目标。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的系统越来越多地被部署用于自主进行科学研究，但其推理是否遵循使科学探究自我纠正的认识论规范尚不清楚。在此，我们通过超过25,000次代理运行和两个互补视角——（i）将基础模型和代理框架的贡献分解的系统性能分析，以及（ii）代理推理认识论结构的行为分析——评估了LLM-based科学代理在八个领域中的表现，涵盖工作流执行到假设驱动的研究。我们观察到，基础模型是性能和行为的首要决定因素，占解释方差的41.4%，而框架仅占1.5%。在所有配置中，68%的追踪中证据被忽略，26%中出现反驳驱动的信念修正，而汇聚的多测试证据很少见。无论代理执行计算工作流还是进行假设驱动的研究，都会出现相同的推理模式。即使代理接收到近乎完整的成功推理轨迹作为上下文，这些模式依然存在，并且在认识论要求高的领域中，由此产生的不可靠性会在重复试验中累积。因此，当前基于LLM的代理执行科学工作流，但并未表现出表征科学推理的认识论模式。基于结果的评估无法检测到这些失败，仅靠框架工程也无法修复它们。除非推理本身成为训练目标，否则由这些代理产生的科学知识无法通过生成它的过程来证明其合理性。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based systems are increasingly deployed to conduct scientific research autonomously, yet whether their reasoning adheres to the epistemic norms that make scientific inquiry self-correcting is poorly understood. Here, we evaluate LLM-based scientific agents across eight domains, spanning workflow execution to hypothesis-driven inquiry, through more than 25,000 agent runs and two complementary lenses: (i) a systematic performance analysis that decomposes the contributions of the base model and the agent scaffold, and (ii) a behavioral analysis of the epistemological structure of agent reasoning. We observe that the base model is the primary determinant of both performance and behavior, accounting for 41.4% of explained variance versus 1.5% for the scaffold. Across all configurations, evidence is ignored in 68% of traces, refutation-driven belief revision occurs in 26%, and convergent multi-test evidence is rare. The same reasoning pattern appears whether the agent executes a computational workflow or conducts hypothesis-driven inquiry. They persist even when agents receive near-complete successful reasoning trajectories as context, and the resulting unreliability compounds across repeated trials in epistemically demanding domains. Thus, current LLM-based agents execute scientific workflows but do not exhibit the epistemic patterns that characterize scientific reasoning. Outcome-based evaluation cannot detect these failures, and scaffold engineering alone cannot repair them. Until reasoning itself becomes a training target, the scientific knowledge produced by such agents cannot be justified by the process that generated it.

</details>


### [61] [Human-Guided Harm Recovery for Computer Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18847v2)
*Christy Li,Sky CH-Wang,Andi Peng,Andreea Bobu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 处理计算机使用agent的伤害恢复，直接与agent安全与后执行相关。

TL;DR: 本文形式化了LM代理在计算机系统上执行动作后的危害恢复问题，通过用户研究提取偏好，构建奖励模型对恢复计划重排序，并引入BackBench基准评估，实验证明该方法优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理安全方法主要关注预防有害动作，但忽略了预防失败后的有效补救，需要一种偏好对齐的恢复机制来减少危害。

Method: 通过形成性用户研究识别恢复价值维度并生成准则，收集1130个成对判断数据集，训练奖励模型，在测试时对多个候选恢复计划重排序。

Result: 引入BackBench基准，人工评估显示奖励模型框架生成的恢复轨迹质量高于基础代理和基于准则的框架。

Conclusion: 该工作奠定了事后安全防护的新型代理安全方法基础，通过偏好对齐的恢复来应对危害后果。

中文摘要：随着LM代理获得在真实计算机系统上执行操作的能力，我们不仅需要防止大规模有害行为，还需要在预防失败时有效补救伤害。我们将这一在事后安全防护中被忽视的挑战形式化为危害恢复问题：即根据人类偏好，最优地将代理从有害状态引导回安全状态。我们通过一项形成性用户研究来确立偏好对齐的恢复，该研究识别了有价值的恢复维度并产生了自然语言准则。我们的1,130个成对判断数据集揭示了属性重要性的上下文相关变化，例如偏好实用、有针对性的策略而非全面的长期方法。我们将这些学到的见解操作化到奖励模型中，在测试时对代理框架生成的多个候选恢复计划进行重新排序。为了系统评估恢复能力，我们引入了BackBench，一个包含50个计算机使用任务的基准测试，用于测试代理从有害状态恢复的能力。人工评估表明，我们的奖励模型框架产生的恢复轨迹质量高于基础代理和基于准则的框架。总之，这些贡献为新型代理安全方法奠定了基础——不仅通过预防来应对危害，而且通过与其意图一致的方式导航其后果。

Original abstract: As LM agents gain the ability to execute actions on real computer systems, we need ways to not only prevent harmful actions at scale but also effectively remediate harm when prevention fails. We formalize a solution to this neglected challenge in post-execution safeguards as harm recovery: the problem of optimally steering an agent from a harmful state back to a safe one in alignment with human preferences. We ground preference-aligned recovery through a formative user study that identifies valued recovery dimensions and produces a natural language rubric. Our dataset of 1,130 pairwise judgments reveals context-dependent shifts in attribute importance, such as preferences for pragmatic, targeted strategies over comprehensive long-term approaches. We operationalize these learned insights in a reward model, re-ranking multiple candidate recovery plans generated by an agent scaffold at test time. To evaluate recovery capabilities systematically, we introduce BackBench, a benchmark of 50 computer-use tasks that test an agent's ability to recover from harmful states. Human evaluation shows our reward model scaffold yields higher-quality recovery trajectories than base agents and rubric-based scaffolds. Together, these contributions lay the foundation for a new class of agent safety methods -- ones that confront harm not only by preventing it, but by navigating its aftermath with alignment and intent.

### [62] [From Natural Language to Executable Narsese: A Neuro-Symbolic Benchmark and Pipeline for Reasoning with NARS](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18873v1)
*Mina Gabriel,Pei Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 神经符号推理管道，可用于agent的规划与推理。

TL;DR: 本文提出一个神经符号框架，将自然语言推理问题转为FOL和Narsese，并构建基准NARS-Reasoning-v0.1，验证了可执行符号生成路径的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在需要显式符号结构和多步推理时不可靠，现有方法缺乏可解释的不确定性建模。

Method: 提出神经符号框架，包括从自然语言到FOL和Narsese的编译管道，以及语言结构感知（LSP）训练方法，并在NARS-Reasoning-v0.1上训练Phi-2 LoRA适配器。

Result: 构建并验证了NARS-Reasoning-v0.1基准，通过执行验证确保符号目标与答案一致，并证明基准可支持监督微调。

Conclusion: 可执行符号生成与基于执行的验证是构建更可靠神经符号推理系统的实用途径。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在语言生成方面能力很强，但在需要显式符号结构、多步推理和可解释不确定性的推理任务中仍然不可靠。本文提出了一种神经符号框架，用于将自然语言推理问题翻译为一阶逻辑（FOL）和Narsese（非公理推理系统（NARS）的语言）的可执行形式化表示。为了支持这一方向，我们引入了NARS-Reasoning-v0.1，这是一个自然语言推理问题基准，配有FOL形式、可执行的Narsese程序以及三个黄金标签：真、假和不确定。我们开发了一个从FOL到可执行Narsese的确定性编译管道，并通过在OpenNARS for Applications (ONA)中运行时执行来验证保留的示例，确保符号目标不仅在语法上良好形成，而且在行为上与预期答案一致。我们进一步提出了语言结构感知（LSP），一种配方，其中LLM被训练生成与推理相关的符号结构，而不仅仅是最终的口头回答。作为初步的概念验证，我们还在NARS-Reasoning-v0.1上训练并发布了一个Phi-2 LoRA适配器，用于三标签推理分类，表明该基准除了可执行评估外，还能支持监督式微调。总体而言，本文将可执行符号生成和基于执行的验证定位为通往更可靠的神经符号推理系统的实用路径。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are highly capable at language generation, but they remain unreliable when reasoning requires explicit symbolic structure, multi-step inference, and interpretable uncertainty. This paper presents a neuro-symbolic framework for translating natural-language reasoning problems into executable formal representations using first-order logic (FOL) and Narsese, the language of the Non-Axiomatic Reasoning System (NARS). To support this direction, we introduce NARS-Reasoning-v0.1, a benchmark of natural-language reasoning problems paired with FOL forms, executable Narsese programs, and three gold labels: True, False, and Uncertain. We develop a deterministic compilation pipeline from FOL to executable Narsese and validate retained examples through runtime execution in OpenNARS for Applications (ONA), ensuring that the symbolic targets are not only syntactically well formed but also behaviorally aligned with the intended answer. We further present Language-Structured Perception (LSP), a formulation in which an LLM is trained to produce reasoning-relevant symbolic structure rather than only a final verbal response. As an initial proof of concept, we also train and release a Phi-2 LoRA adapter on NARS-Reasoning-v0.1 for three-label reasoning classification, showing that the benchmark can support supervised adaptation in addition to executable evaluation. Overall, the paper positions executable symbolic generation and execution-based validation as a practical path toward more reliable neuro-symbolic reasoning systems.
