### [63] [How Adversarial Environments Mislead Agentic AI?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18874v1)
*Zhonghao Zhan,Huichi Zhou,Zhenhao Li,Peiyuan Jing,Krinos Li,Hamed Haddadi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究工具集成agent在对手环境下的脆弱性，提出攻击与测试框架。

TL;DR: 提出对抗性环境注入（AEI）威胁模型，揭示工具集成代理的信任差距，并通过POTEMKIN框架发现认知与导航鲁棒性之间存在权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估仅关注代理在良性环境中的工具使用能力，忽略了工具被恶意操控时的风险，存在信任差距。

Method: 形式化AEI威胁模型，开发POTEMKIN测试工具，设计两种攻击（幻觉和迷宫）在11,000+次运行中测试五个前沿代理。

Result: 发现代理对一种攻击的抵抗常导致对另一种攻击更脆弱，表明认知与导航鲁棒性是独立且相互冲突的能力。

Conclusion: 需同时评估代理的怀疑能力与工具使用能力，应对AEI威胁需兼顾认知与导航鲁棒性。

中文摘要：工具集成代理的部署基于外部工具使其输出立足于现实的假设。然而，这一依赖恰恰创造了关键的攻击面。当前的评估在良性环境中基准测试能力，询问“代理能否正确使用工具”，但从未问“如果工具撒谎怎么办”。我们识别出这一信任差距：代理被评估性能，而非怀疑。我们将此漏洞形式化为对抗性环境注入（AEI），一种威胁模型，其中对手破坏工具输出以欺骗代理。AEI构成环境欺骗：在不知情的代理周围构建一个由被污染的搜索结果和捏造的参考网络构成的“虚假世界”。我们通过POTEMKIN实现这一操作，这是一个与模型上下文协议（MCP）兼容的即插即用鲁棒性测试工具。我们识别出两个正交攻击面：幻觉（广度攻击）污染检索以诱导认知漂移转向错误信念，而迷宫（深度攻击）利用结构陷阱导致策略崩溃进入无限循环。在超过11,000次运行中，对五个前沿代理，我们发现显著的鲁棒性差距：抵抗一种攻击往往增加对另一种攻击的脆弱性，表明认知和导航鲁棒性是不同能力。

Original abstract: Tool-integrated agents are deployed on the premise that external tools ground their outputs in reality. Yet this very reliance creates a critical attack surface. Current evaluations benchmark capability in benign settings, asking "can the agent use tools correctly" but never "what if the tools lie". We identify this Trust Gap: agents are evaluated for performance, not for skepticism. We formalize this vulnerability as Adversarial Environmental Injection (AEI), a threat model where adversaries compromise tool outputs to deceive agents. AEI constitutes environmental deception: constructing a "fake world" of poisoned search results and fabricated reference networks around unsuspecting agents. We operationalize this via POTEMKIN, a Model Context Protocol (MCP)-compatible harness for plug-and-play robustness testing. We identify two orthogonal attack surfaces: The Illusion (breadth attacks) poison retrieval to induce epistemic drift toward false beliefs, while The Maze (depth attacks) exploit structural traps to cause policy collapse into infinite loops. Across 11,000+ runs on five frontier agents, we find a stark robustness gap: resistance to one attack often increases vulnerability to the other, demonstrating that epistemic and navigational robustness are distinct capabilities.

</details>


### [64] [Formally Verified Patent Analysis via Dependent Type Theory: Machine-Checkable Certificates from a Hybrid AI + Lean 4 Pipeline](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18882v1)
*George Koomullil*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 形式化验证的AI+Lean4管道，可迁移到coding agent的验证。

TL;DR: 提出一个形式化验证的混合AI+Lean 4专利分析框架，实现多个IP用例的数学正确性保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有专利分析依赖手动专家分析（慢、不可扩展）或ML/NLP方法（概率性、不透明、非组合性），缺乏形式化保证。

Method: 将权利要求编码为DAG，使用Lean 4定理证明器形式化验证核心算法，通过不可信生成器+内核检查保证高层定理正确性。

Result: 实现了六个算法，验证了DAG覆盖核心和结构引理，案例研究展示了加权覆盖和构建敏感性分析。

Conclusion: 这是首个将交互式定理证明应用于专利分析的框架，保证条件取决于ML层准确性，未来将进行已裁决案例验证。

中文摘要：我们提出了一个形式化验证的专利分析框架，作为混合AI + Lean 4流水线。DAG覆盖核心（算法1b）在固定有界匹配分数后得到完全机器验证。自由实施、权利要求构建敏感性、跨权利要求一致性和等同原则分析在规范级别上形式化，并带有内核检查的候选证书。现有的专利分析方法依赖于手动专家分析（慢、不可扩展）或ML/NLP方法（概率性、不透明、非组合性）。据我们所知，这是第一个将基于依赖类型理论的交互式定理证明应用于知识产权分析的框架。权利要求被编码为Lean 4中的DAG，匹配强度作为已验证完全格的元素，置信度分数通过经过验证正确的单调函数在依赖关系中传播。我们通过六个算法形式化了五个IP用例（专利到产品映射、自由实施、权利要求构建敏感性、跨权利要求一致性、等同原则）。结构引理、覆盖核心生成器和闭路恒等式coverage = W_cov在Lean 4中得到机器验证。其他用例的高层定理仍然是非正式证明草图，其证明生成函数在架构上得到缓解（不可信生成器，其输出经过内核检查和无sorry公理审计）。保证条件取决于ML层：它们证明ML分数下游计算的数学正确性，而不是分数本身的准确性。一个关于合成内存模块权利要求的案例研究展示了加权覆盖和构建敏感性分析。对已裁决案例的验证是未来工作。

Original abstract: We present a formally verified framework for patent analysis as a hybrid AI + Lean 4 pipeline. The DAG-coverage core (Algorithm 1b) is fully machine-verified once bounded match scores are fixed. Freedom-to-operate, claim-construction sensitivity, cross-claim consistency, and doctrine-of-equivalents analyses are formalized at the specification level with kernel-checked candidate certificates. Existing patent-analysis approaches rely on manual expert analysis (slow, non-scalable) or ML/NLP methods (probabilistic, opaque, non-compositional). To our knowledge, this is the first framework that applies interactive theorem proving based on dependent type theory to intellectual property analysis. Claims are encoded as DAGs in Lean 4, match strengths as elements of a verified complete lattice, and confidence scores propagate through dependencies via proven-correct monotone functions. We formalize five IP use cases (patent-to-product mapping, freedom-to-operate, claim construction sensitivity, cross-claim consistency, doctrine of equivalents) via six algorithms. Structural lemmas, the coverage-core generator, and the closed-path identity coverage = W_cov are machine-verified in Lean 4. Higher-level theorems for the other use cases remain informal proof sketches, and their proof-generation functions are architecturally mitigated (untrusted generators whose outputs are kernel-checked and sorry-free axiom-audited). Guarantees are conditional on the ML layer: they certify mathematical correctness of computations downstream of ML scores, not the accuracy of the scores themselves. A case study on a synthetic memory-module claim demonstrates weighted coverage and construction-sensitivity analysis. Validation against adjudicated cases is future work.

</details>

# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [65] [EVE: Verifiable Self-Evolution of MLLMs via Executable Visual Transformations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18320v1)
*Yongrui Heng,Chaoya Jiang,Han Yang,Shikun Zhang,Wei Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: MLLM自我进化框架（Challenger-Solver），自进化机制可迁移至agent。

TL;DR: EVE是一个通过可执行视觉变换实现多模态大模型自我进化的框架，利用挑战者-求解者双策略架构和多维奖励系统持续生成多样化、难度递增的训练数据，无需伪标签。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我进化方法存在局限：伪标签方法因模型预测漂移导致质量下降，模板方法过于静态无法动态调整难度和多样性。需要一种独立于模型内部确定性、且能持续丰富训练分布的自我改进机制。

Method: 提出EVE框架，采用挑战者-求解者双策略架构。挑战者维护并扩展视觉变换代码队列，合成Python脚本执行动态变换，生成带有执行验证答案的VQA问题；多维奖励系统（语义多样性+动态难度校准）引导挑战者生成更复杂任务，防止模式崩溃并促进互惠共进化。

Result: 大量实验表明EVE在多个基准上持续超越现有自我进化方法，验证了其稳健性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: EVE为可验证的多模态大语言模型自我进化建立了有效范式，完全消除对伪标签的依赖，通过代码生成和执行实现可验证的持续自我改进。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型的自我进化仍然是一个关键挑战：基于伪标签的方法由于模型预测漂移而遭受渐进式质量下降，而基于模板的方法则局限于一组静态的变换，无法在难度或多样性上适应。我们认为，稳健、持续的自我改进不仅需要独立于模型内部确定性的确定性外部反馈，还需要一种机制来永久地多样化训练分布。为此，我们引入了EVE（可执行视觉变换驱动的自我进化），一个全新的框架，它完全绕过伪标签，利用可执行的视觉变换，并持续丰富其种类和复杂性。EVE采用挑战者-求解者双策略架构。挑战者维护并逐步扩展一个视觉变换代码示例队列，从中合成新的Python脚本以执行动态视觉变换。执行这些脚本产生具有绝对、执行验证的真实答案的VQA问题，消除了对模型生成监督的任何依赖。一个整合了语义多样性和动态难度校准的多维奖励系统引导挑战者丰富其代码示例队列，同时提出越来越具有挑战性的任务，防止模式崩溃，并促进两个策略之间的互惠共进化。大量实验表明，EVE持续优于现有的自我进化方法，为可验证的多模态大语言模型自我进化建立了一个稳健且可扩展的范式。代码可在https://github.com/0001Henry/EVE获取。

Original abstract: Self-evolution of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) remains a critical challenge: pseudo-label-based methods suffer from progressive quality degradation as model predictions drift, while template-based methods are confined to a static set of transformations that cannot adapt in difficulty or diversity. We contend that robust, continuous self-improvement requires not only deterministic external feedback independent of the model's internal certainty, but also a mechanism to perpetually diversify the training distribution. To this end, we introduce EVE (Executable Visual transformation-based self-Evolution), a novel framework that entirely bypasses pseudo-labels by harnessing executable visual transformations continuously enriched in both variety and complexity. EVE adopts a Challenger-Solver dual-policy architecture. The Challenger maintains and progressively expands a queue of visual transformation code examples, from which it synthesizes novel Python scripts to perform dynamic visual transformations. Executing these scripts yields VQA problems with absolute, execution-verified ground-truth answers, eliminating any reliance on model-generated supervision. A multi-dimensional reward system integrating semantic diversity and dynamic difficulty calibration steers the Challenger to enrich its code example queue while posing progressively more challenging tasks, preventing mode collapse and fostering reciprocal co-evolution between the two policies. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EVE consistently surpasses existing self-evolution methods, establishing a robust and scalable paradigm for verifiable MLLM self-evolution. The code is available at https://github.com/0001Henry/EVE .

</details>


### [66] [Progressive Online Video Understanding with Evidence-Aligned Timing and Transparent Decisions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18459v1)
*Kecheng Zhang,Zongxin Yang,Mingfei Han,Haihong Hao,Yunzhi Zhuge,Changlin Li,Junhan Zhao,Zhihui Li,Xiaojun Chang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 在线视频理解中的推理控制器（ATDM），对agent透明决策有启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出一种解耦推理控制与记忆整合的在线视频理解框架，通过进度和置信度指标实现证据对齐的透明决策，并在基准上取得领先性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统视频LLM在在线流式场景中忽略了响应时机对齐和决策透明度的关键能力，导致决策不透明、对齐困难以及计算预算限制下的全局理解难题。

Method: 提出包含主动思考决策器（ATDM）和分层渐进语义整合（HPSI）的框架：ATDM通过进度ρ和置信度c外化决策过程以对齐响应时间；HPSI利用可学习多级聚合令牌跨片段传播以构建高效全局认知状态。

Result: 在StreamingBench和OVOBench上分别达到71.6%和46.9%的准确率，其中Thinking-QwenVL将StreamingBench的SOTA从67.63%提升至71.60%。

Conclusion: 该方法为证据对齐和透明的在线视频分析提供了稳健解决方案，并通过实验验证了其有效性。

中文摘要：视觉智能体在野外运行时，必须能够在视频流中恰好出现足够证据的第一时间精确响应查询，这是传统视频大语言模型在离线设置下所忽略的关键能力。向在线、流式范式的转变带来了重大挑战：决策透明度不足、响应时机与视觉证据对齐困难，以及在严格计算预算下维护全局因果一致理解的需求。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一种将推理控制与记忆整合解耦的新型框架。我们介绍了我们的模型，该框架的一个实例，包含两个核心组件。首先，主动思考决策器（ATDM）是一个透明的推理控制器，它使用可观察的进度（ρ）和置信度（c）指标来外化其决策过程。这使其能够精确地将响应时间t_r与第一个足够证据的时间戳t^*对齐，同时向用户流式传输其推理过程。其次，分层渐进语义整合（HPSI）模块充当高效记忆系统。它采用一组可学习的多级聚合标记，这些标记在片段之间传播，以构建丰富的全局认知状态而不超过标记预算。我们的方法在关键在线视频理解基准上树立了新标准，在StreamingBench上实现了71.6%的强性能，在OVOBench上实现了46.9%，展示了证据对齐和透明的在线视频分析的稳健解决方案。大量实验证明了ATDM和HPSI的有效性，例如，Thinking-QwenVL将StreamingBench基准上先前最先进方法的准确率从67.63%提高到71.60%。

Original abstract: Visual agents operating in the wild must respond to queries precisely when sufficient evidence first appears in a video stream, a critical capability that is overlooked by conventional video LLMs evaluated in offline settings. The shift to an online, streaming paradigm introduces significant challenges: a lack of decision transparency, the difficulty of aligning response timing with visual evidence, and the need to maintain a global, causally consistent understanding under tight computational budgets. To address these issues, we propose a novel framework that decouples reasoning control from memory integration. We introduce \textbf{\model{}}, an instantiation of this framework with two core components. First, the \emph{Active Thinking Decision Maker (ATDM)} is a transparent reasoning controller that externalizes its decision process using observable progress ($\boldsymbolρ$) and confidence ($\boldsymbol{c}$) metrics. This allows it to precisely time its response $t_r$ to match the first-sufficient-evidence timestamp $t^\star$ while streaming its reasoning to the user. Second, the \emph{Hierarchical Progressive Semantic Integration (HPSI)} module acts as an efficient memory system. It employs a set of learnable, multi-level aggregation tokens that are propagated across clips to build a rich, global cognitive state without exceeding token budgets. %Our approach sets a new standard on key online video understanding benchmarks, achieving strong performance of \textbf{71.6\%} on StreamingBench and \textbf{46.9\%} on OVOBench, demonstrating a robust solution for evidence-aligned and transparent online video analysis. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of ATDM and HPSI, e.g., Thinking-QwenVL improves the accuracy of the previous state-of-the-art from 67.63\% to 71.60\% on the StreamingBench benchmark.

### [67] [Diversity Collapse in Multi-Agent LLM Systems: Structural Coupling and Collective Failure in Open-Ended Idea Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18005v2)
*Nuo Chen,Yicheng Tong,Yuzhe Yang,Yufei He,Xueyi Zhang,Qingyun Zou,Qian Wang,Bingsheng He*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 研究多agent系统的多样性崩溃，提出结构耦合理论，对agent协作设计有启发。

TL;DR: 多智能体系统中协作创意生成的多样性存在三个层面的瓶颈，主要源于交互结构而非模型能力，需保持独立性和分歧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管多智能体系统被期望通过集体互动拓宽创意生成的多样性，但何时以及为何这种协作能真正扩展解决方案空间尚不明确，需要系统性地研究多样性变化的底层机制。

Method: 从三个自下而上的层面（模型智能、智能体认知、系统动态）进行系统的实证研究，通过实验观察不同因子对多样性指标的影响。

Result: 发现了三个层面的多样性塌缩现象：模型层面强对齐模型导致边际多样性递减；认知层面权威主导抑制语义多样性；系统层面规模扩展回报递减且密集通信加速收敛。这些塌缩源于结构性耦合。

Conclusion: 多样性崩溃主要源于交互结构而非模型不足，因此设计创意MAS时应注重维护智能体的独立性和分歧，以避免集体失败。

中文摘要：多智能体系统（MAS）越来越多地被用于开放式创意生成，其驱动力是期望集体互动能拓宽探索的多样性。然而，这种合作何时以及为何真正扩展了解决方案空间仍不清楚。我们提出了一个系统的实证研究，从三个自下而上的层面研究基于MAS的创意生成中的多样性：模型智能、智能体认知和系统动态。在模型层面，我们发现了一个计算效率悖论：更强、高度对齐的模型尽管每样本质量更高，但边际多样性递减。在认知层面，权威驱动的动态与初级主导的群体相比，抑制了语义多样性。在系统层面，群体规模扩展产生递减回报，而密集的通信拓扑加速了过早收敛。我们将这些结果描述为结构性耦合导致的集体失败，这是一种交互无意中收缩智能体探索并引发多样性崩溃的过程。我们的分析表明，这种崩溃主要源于交互结构而非模型本身的不足，强调了在设计用于创意任务的MAS时保持独立性和分歧的重要性。我们的代码可在 https://github.com/Xtra-Computing/MAS_Diversity 获取。

Original abstract: Multi-agent systems (MAS) are increasingly used for open-ended idea generation, driven by the expectation that collective interaction will broaden the exploration diversity. However, when and why such collaboration truly expands the solution space remains unclear. We present a systematic empirical study of diversity in MAS-based ideation across three bottom-up levels: model intelligence, agent cognition, and system dynamics. At the model level, we identify a compute efficiency paradox, where stronger, highly aligned models yield diminishing marginal diversity despite higher per-sample quality. At the cognition level, authority-driven dynamics suppress semantic diversity compared to junior-dominated groups. At the system level, group-size scaling yields diminishing returns and dense communication topologies accelerate premature convergence. We characterize these outcomes as collective failures emerging from structural coupling, a process where interaction inadvertently contracts agent exploration and triggers diversity collapse. Our analysis shows that this collapse arises primarily from the interaction structure rather than inherent model insufficiency, highlighting the importance of preserving independence and disagreement when designing MAS for creative tasks. Our code is available at https://github.com/Xtra-Computing/MAS_Diversity.

### [68] [Aether: Network Validation Using Agentic AI and Digital Twin](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18233v1)
*Jordan Auge,Sam Betts,Giovanna Carofiglio,Giulio Grassi,Martin Gysi,John Kenneth d'Souza*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 提出五智能体协作的网络验证系统，agent架构与数字孪生可迁移至软件工程验证。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 网络变更验证主要依赖人工，耗时且易错；现有形式化验证仅适用于离线预部署，难以适应持续变化和真实生产环境；当前工具分散，覆盖不全，错误在部署后才暴露。

Method: 提出Aether框架，集成生成式代理AI与多功能网络数字孪生；采用五个专门的网络运营AI代理协同处理变更验证生命周期，包括意图分析、网络验证和测试；统一数字孪生整合建模、仿真和模拟以保持一致的最新网络视图。

Result: 在合成网络变更场景和主要ISP的过往事件上评估：错误检测率100%，诊断覆盖率92-96%，完成时间6-7分钟，优于传统方法。

Conclusion: Aether实现了自动化、快速的网络变更验证，显著减少人工工作量、降低错误率，并提高运营敏捷性和成本效益。

中文摘要：网络变更验证仍然是现代网络运营中一个关键但主要依靠人工、耗时且容易出错的过程。尽管形式化网络验证在证明正确性属性方面取得了实质性进展，但它通常应用于离线、预部署环境，并且在适应持续变更和验证真实生产行为方面面临挑战。当前的运营方法通常涉及分散的测试工具，导致覆盖不全，错误仅在部署后才会暴露。在本文中，我们提出Aether，一种新颖的方法，将生成式代理人工智能与多功能网络数字孪生相结合，以自动化和简化网络变更验证工作流程。它采用代理架构，包含五个专门的网络运营AI代理，协同处理从意图分析到网络验证和测试的变更验证生命周期。Aether代理使用统一的网络数字孪生，集成建模、仿真和模拟，以维护一致且最新的网络视图用于验证和测试。通过在此数字孪生之上编排代理协作，Aether实现了自动化、快速的网络变更验证，同时减少了人工工作量、最小化错误，并提高了运营敏捷性和成本效益。我们在涵盖主要网络变更类别的合成网络变更场景以及来自一家主要ISP运营网络的过往事件上评估了Aether，展示了在错误检测（100%）、诊断覆盖（92-96%）和速度（6-7分钟）方面相比传统方法的良好结果。

Original abstract: Network change validation remains a critical yet predominantly manual, time-consuming, and error-prone process in modern network operations. While formal network verification has made substantial progress in proving correctness properties, it is typically applied in offline, pre-deployment settings and faces challenges in accommodating continuous changes and validating live production behavior. Current operational approaches typically involve scattered testing tools, resulting in partial coverage and errors that surface only after deployment. In this paper, we present Aether, a novel approach that integrates Generative Agentic AI with a multi-functional Network Digital Twin to automate and streamline network change validation workflows. It features an agentic architecture with five specialized Network Operations AI agents that collaboratively handle the change validation lifecycle from intent analysis to network verification and testing. Aether agents use a unified Network Digital Twin integrating modeling, simulation, and emulation to maintain a consistent, up-to-date network view for verification and testing. By orchestrating agent collaboration atop this digital twin, Aether enables automated, rapid network change validation while reducing manual effort, minimizing errors, and improving operational agility and cost-effectiveness. We evaluate Aether over synthetic network change scenarios covering main classes of network changes and on past incidents from a major ISP operational network, demonstrating promising results in error detection (100%), diagnostic coverage (92-96%), and speed (6-7 minutes) over traditional methods.

### [69] [From Craft to Kernel: A Governance-First Execution Architecture and Semantic ISA for Agentic Computers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18652v2)
*Xiangyu Wen,Yuang Zhao,Xiaoyu Xu,Lingjun Chen,Changran Xu,Shu Chi,Jianrong Ding,Zeju Li,Haomin Li,Li Jiang,Fangxin Liu,Qiang Xu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出治理优先的执行架构与语义ISA，强化agent安全与可靠性，可迁移至代码agent安全控制。

TL;DR: Arbiter-K是一种治理优先的智能体执行架构，通过确定性核封装概率模型，利用语义指令架构和污染传播实现精确的安全拦截。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体AI依赖大语言模型控制循环，脆弱且不安全，需要更稳健的架构。

Method: 提出Arbiter-K架构，包含概率处理单元、确定性神经符号内核、语义ISA、安全上下文注册表、指令依赖图及主动污染传播机制，在确定性汇点拦截不安全轨迹，支持执行纠正和回滚。

Result: 在OpenClaw和NanoBot上实现76%-95%不安全拦截，绝对增益92.79%。

Conclusion: Arbiter-K将安全作为微架构属性，有效提升了智能体系统的安全性。

中文摘要：智能体AI从脆弱的原型向生产系统的过渡因普遍存在的工艺危机而停滞。我们认为，当前主流编排范式——将系统控制循环委托给大型语言模型，并仅用启发式护栏进行修补——是这种脆弱性的根本原因。取而代之，我们提出Arbiter-K，一种治理优先的执行架构，它将底层模型重新概念化为一个概率处理单元，并由一个确定性的神经符号内核封装。Arbiter-K实现了语义指令集架构（ISA），将概率消息具象化为离散指令。这使得内核能够维护安全上下文注册表，并在运行时构建指令依赖图，从而基于每个推理节点的数据流谱系实现主动污染传播。通过利用这一机制，Arbiter-K在确定性汇点（例如高风险工具调用或未经授权的网络出口）精确拦截不安全轨迹，并在安全策略触发时实现自主执行纠正和架构回滚。在OpenClaw和NanoBot上的评估表明，Arbiter-K将安全作为微架构属性强制执行，实现了76%到95%的不安全拦截，相对于原生策略获得92.79%的绝对增益。代码已在https://github.com/cure-lab/ArbiterOS公开。

Original abstract: The transition of agentic AI from brittle prototypes to production systems is stalled by a pervasive crisis of craft. We suggest that the prevailing orchestration paradigm-delegating the system control loop to large language models and merely patching with heuristic guardrails-is the root cause of this fragility. Instead, we propose Arbiter-K, a Governance-First execution architecture that reconceptualizes the underlying model as a Probabilistic Processing Unit encapsulated by a deterministic, neuro-symbolic kernel. Arbiter-K implements a Semantic Instruction Set Architecture (ISA) to reify probabilistic messages into discrete instructions. This allows the kernel to maintain a Security Context Registry and construct an Instruction Dependency Graph at runtime, enabling active taint propagation based on the data-flow pedigree of each reasoning node. By leveraging this mechanism, Arbiter-K precisely interdicts unsafe trajectories at deterministic sinks (e.g., high-risk tool calls or unauthorized network egress) and enables autonomous execution correction and architectural rollback when security policies are triggered. Evaluations on OpenClaw and NanoBot demonstrate that Arbiter-K enforces security as a microarchitectural property, achieving 76% to 95% unsafe interception for a 92.79% absolute gain over native policies. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/cure-lab/ArbiterOS.

</details>


### [70] [RAVEN: Retrieval-Augmented Vulnerability Exploration Network for Memory Corruption Analysis in User Code and Binary Programs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17948v2)
*Parteek Jamwal,Minghao Shao,Boyuan Chen,Achyuta Muthuvelan,Asini Subanya,Boubacar Ballo,Kashish Satija,Mariam Shafey,Mohamed Mahmoud,Moncif Dahaji Bouffi,Pasindu Wickramasinghe,Siyona Goel,Yaakulya Sabbani,Hakim Hacid,Mthandazo Ndhlovu,Eleanna Kafeza,Sanjay Rawat,Muhammad Shafique*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 基于LLM agent和RAG的漏洞分析，属于代码安全agent。

TL;DR: 提出RAVEN框架，结合LLM代理与检索增强生成技术，自动生成符合谷歌Project Zero模板的漏洞分析报告，在105个样本上达到54.21%的平均质量分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在漏洞分类、检测等任务中表现优异，但在自动化漏洞报告文档化方面研究不足

Method: 构建四个LLM代理（Explorer、RAG引擎、Analyst、Reporter）及一个LLM Judge评估器，利用检索增强生成生成结构化漏洞报告

Result: 在105个涵盖15种CWE类型的代码样本上平均质量得分54.21%

Conclusion: RAVEN方法在自动化漏洞文档编制方面有效，但仍需改进以提升报告质量。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在各种网络安全任务中展示了卓越的能力，包括漏洞分类、检测和修补。然而，它们在自动化漏洞报告文档编制和分析方面的潜力仍未得到充分探索。我们提出了RAVEN（检索增强型漏洞探索网络），这是一个利用LLM代理和检索增强生成（RAG）来综合生成全面漏洞分析报告的框架。给定易受攻击的源代码，RAVEN根据谷歌Project Zero根因分析模板生成报告。该框架使用四个模块：一个用于漏洞识别的Explorer代理、一个从精选数据库（包括谷歌Project Zero报告和CWE条目）检索相关知识的RAG引擎、一个用于影响和利用评估的Analyst代理，以及一个用于结构化报告生成的Reporter代理。为确保质量，RAVEN包含一个特定任务的LLM法官，用于评估报告的结构完整性、地面真实性对齐、代码推理质量和修复质量。我们在来自NIST-SARD数据集的105个涵盖15种CWE类型的易受攻击代码样本上评估了RAVEN。结果显示平均质量得分为54.21%，支持了我们的方法在自动化漏洞文档编制方面的有效性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities across various cybersecurity tasks, including vulnerability classification, detection, and patching. However, their potential in automated vulnerability report documentation and analysis remains underexplored. We present RAVEN (Retrieval Augmented Vulnerability Exploration Network), a framework leveraging LLM agents and Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) to synthesize comprehensive vulnerability analysis reports. Given vulnerable source code, RAVEN generates reports following the Google Project Zero Root Cause Analysis template. The framework uses four modules: an Explorer agent for vulnerability identification, a RAG engine retrieving relevant knowledge from curated databases including Google Project Zero reports and CWE entries, an Analyst agent for impact and exploitation assessment, and a Reporter agent for structured report generation. To ensure quality, RAVEN includes a task specific LLM Judge evaluating reports across structural integrity, ground truth alignment, code reasoning quality, and remediation quality. We evaluate RAVEN on 105 vulnerable code samples covering 15 CWE types from the NIST-SARD dataset. Results show an average quality score of 54.21%, supporting the effectiveness of our approach for automated vulnerability documentation.

</details>


### [71] [Owner-Harm: A Missing Threat Model for AI Agent Safety](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18658v1)
*Dongcheng Zhang,Yiqing Jiang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出agent安全威胁模型，对coding agent安全设计有直接借鉴。

TL;DR: 提出Owner-Harm威胁模型，发现现有防御在所有者危害上存在重大漏洞，并引入SSDG框架进行泛化分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准只关注通用犯罪危害，忽略了智能体伤害部署者这一具有商业后果的威胁类别，且现实事件已表明其严重性。

Method: 提出包含八类行为的Owner-Harm威胁模型，在AgentHarm和AgentDojo基准上量化防御差距，构建300场景基准，并提出符号-语义防御泛化（SSDG）框架，通过上下文剥夺和注入实验验证。

Result: 组合安全系统在AgentHarm上达100% TPR/0% FPR，但在AgentDojo注入任务上仅14.8% TPR；门控机制在300场景上达75.3% TPR/3.3% FPR，添加后审计验证器后TPR升至85.3%，劫持检测从43.3%升至93.3%。

Conclusion: 所有者危害是独特威胁，环境绑定的符号规则导致防御漏洞，有效检测需结构化的目标-动作对齐而非简单文本拼接；SSDG框架有助于指导防御泛化。

中文摘要：现有的AI智能体安全基准主要关注通用的犯罪危害（网络犯罪、骚扰、武器合成），对一个独特且具有商业后果的威胁类别——智能体伤害其自身部署者——存在系统性的盲区。现实世界的事件说明了这一差距：Slack AI凭证外泄（2024年8月）、Microsoft 365 Copilot日历注入泄露（2024年1月）、以及Meta智能体未经授权的论坛帖子暴露运营数据（2026年3月）。我们提出了Owner-Harm，一个包含八类损害部署者的智能体行为的正式威胁模型。我们在两个基准上量化了防御差距：一个组合安全系统在AgentHarm（通用犯罪危害）上实现了100%的真阳性率（TPR）/0%的假阳性率（FPR），但在AgentDojo注入任务（提示注入介导的所有者危害）上仅达到14.8%（4/27；95%置信区间：5.9%-32.5%）。一个受控的通用LLM基线表明，这一差距并非所有者危害所固有（62.7% vs. 59.3%，差异3.4个百分点），而是源于环境绑定的符号规则无法在工具词汇表之间泛化。在一个事后构建的300场景所有者危害基准上，仅门控机制就实现了75.3%的TPR/3.3%的FPR；添加一个确定性的后审计验证器将总体TPR提高到85.3%（+10.0个百分点），并将劫持检测从43.3%提高到93.3%，展示了强大的层次互补性。我们引入了符号-语义防御泛化（SSDG）框架，将信息覆盖率与检测率相关联。两个SSDG实验部分验证了该框架：上下文剥夺将检测差距放大了3.4倍（R=3.60 vs. R=1.06）；上下文注入揭示了结构化的目标-动作对齐（而非文本拼接）对于有效的所有者危害检测是必需的。

Original abstract: Existing AI agent safety benchmarks focus on generic criminal harm (cybercrime, harassment, weapon synthesis), leaving a systematic blind spot for a distinct and commercially consequential threat category: agents harming their own deployers. Real-world incidents illustrate the gap: Slack AI credential exfiltration (Aug 2024), Microsoft 365 Copilot calendar-injection leaks (Jan 2024), and a Meta agent unauthorized forum post exposing operational data (Mar 2026). We propose Owner-Harm, a formal threat model with eight categories of agent behavior damaging the deployer. We quantify the defense gap on two benchmarks: a compositional safety system achieves 100% TPR / 0% FPR on AgentHarm (generic criminal harm) yet only 14.8% (4/27; 95% CI: 5.9%-32.5%) on AgentDojo injection tasks (prompt-injection-mediated owner harm). A controlled generic-LLM baseline shows the gap is not inherent to owner-harm (62.7% vs. 59.3%, delta 3.4 pp) but arises from environment-bound symbolic rules that fail to generalize across tool vocabularies. On a post-hoc 300-scenario owner-harm benchmark, the gate alone achieves 75.3% TPR / 3.3% FPR; adding a deterministic post-audit verifier raises overall TPR to 85.3% (+10.0 pp) and Hijacking detection from 43.3% to 93.3%, demonstrating strong layer complementarity. We introduce the Symbolic-Semantic Defense Generalization (SSDG) framework relating information coverage to detection rate. Two SSDG experiments partially validate it: context deprivation amplifies the detection gap 3.4x (R = 3.60 vs. R = 1.06); context injection reveals structured goal-action alignment, not text concatenation, is required for effective owner-harm detection.

</details>


### [72] [Evaluating Answer Leakage Robustness of LLM Tutors against Adversarial Student Attacks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18660v1)
*Jin Zhao,Marta Knežević,Tanja Käser*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究LLM tutor的对抗攻击鲁棒性，可迁移到coding agent安全防护。

TL;DR: 本文研究学生对抗行为下LLM助教的答案泄露问题，提出了越狱攻击的标准化基准和简单有效的防御策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作未考虑学生滥用情况，需要评估LLM助教在对抗攻击下的鲁棒性。

Method: 将六组对抗和说服技术适应到教育场景，引入经过微调的对抗学生代理作为基准，并提出防御策略。

Result: 发现现有上下文对抗代理常无法有效攻击，而微调代理能成功越狱；提出的防御策略能减少答案泄露。

Conclusion: 需要标准化基准来评估LLM助教的鲁棒性，简单防御策略有效。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地应用于教育领域，但其默认的乐于助人特性常常与教学原则相冲突。先前的工作通过答案泄露（即直接给出完整解决方案而非脚手架式引导）来评估教学质量，但通常假设学习者出于善意，这使得助教在学生滥用情况下的鲁棒性基本未被探索。在本文中，我们研究了学生表现出对抗行为并旨在从助教那里获取正确答案的场景。我们评估了一系列基于LLM的助教模型，包括不同模型家族、教学对齐模型以及多智能体设计，在多种对抗性学生攻击下。我们将六组对抗和说服技术适应到教育场景，并用它们来探测助教泄露最终答案的可能性。我们使用不同类型的上下文对抗学生代理来评估答案泄露鲁棒性，发现它们通常无法实施有效攻击。因此，我们引入了一个经过微调以越狱基于LLM的助教的对抗学生代理，我们将其作为评估助教鲁棒性的标准化基准的核心。最后，我们提出了简单但有效的防御策略，可以减少答案泄露并增强基于LLM的助教在对抗场景下的鲁棒性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in education, yet their default helpfulness often conflicts with pedagogical principles. Prior work evaluates pedagogical quality via answer leakage-the disclosure of complete solutions instead of scaffolding-but typically assumes well-intentioned learners, leaving tutor robustness under student misuse largely unexplored. In this paper, we study scenarios where students behave adversarially and aim to obtain the correct answer from the tutor. We evaluate a broad set of LLM-based tutor models, including different model families, pedagogically aligned models, and a multi-agent design, under a range of adversarial student attacks. We adapt six groups of adversarial and persuasive techniques to the educational setting and use them to probe how likely a tutor is to reveal the final answer. We evaluate answer leakage robustness using different types of in-context adversarial student agents, finding that they often fail to carry out effective attacks. We therefore introduce an adversarial student agent that we fine-tune to jailbreak LLM-based tutors, which we propose as the core of a standardized benchmark for evaluating tutor robustness. Finally, we present simple but effective defense strategies that reduce answer leakage and strengthen the robustness of LLM-based tutors in adversarial scenarios.

### [73] [Do Privacy Policies Match with the Logs? An Empirical Study of Privacy Disclosure in Android Application Logs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18552v2)
*Zhiyuan Chen,Love Jayesh Ahir,Ahmad Suleiman,Kundi Yao,Yiming Tang,Weiyi Shang,Daqing Hou*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对1000个Android应用的隐私政策和日志进行实证研究发现，大多数应用有隐私政策但很少提及日志实践，且大量日志泄露未声明信息，政策与实际行为严重不一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 隐私政策往往含糊不清或不完整，需要评估它们与真实数据收集行为的一致性。

Method: 分析1000个Android应用的隐私政策和生成的86,836,964条日志条目，比较政策声明与实际日志数据。

Result: 88%有隐私政策，仅28.5%提及日志；27.7%日志相关陈述模糊；67.6%应用泄露政策未提及的敏感信息；仅0.4%政策与日志一致。

Conclusion: 当前隐私政策对日志实践描述不完整或模糊，经常与实际日志行为不一致。

中文摘要：隐私政策旨在告知用户软件系统如何收集和处理数据，但它们往往含糊不清或不完整。本文对隐私政策中与日志相关的陈述模式及其与Android应用程序日志中观察到的隐私披露的一致性进行了实证研究。我们分析了跨多个类别的1000个Android应用程序，生成了86,836,964条日志条目。我们的发现表明，虽然大多数应用程序（88.0%）提供了隐私政策，但只有28.5%明确提到了日志记录实践。在那些提及日志记录的隐私政策中，大多数清楚地描述了记录了什么信息；然而，27.7%的与日志相关的陈述仍然过于简单或模糊，对实际数据收集提供的见解有限。我们进一步观察到应用程序日志中普遍存在隐私泄露，67.6%的应用程序泄露了其政策中未提及的敏感信息。令人担忧的是，只有0.4%的应用程序在声明的政策内容和实际记录的数据之间表现出一致性。这些发现突显了当前隐私政策对日志记录实践提供了不完整或模糊的描述，这些描述往往与实际日志记录行为不一致。

Original abstract: Privacy policies are intended to inform users about how software systems collect and handle data, yet they often remain vague or incomplete. This paper presents an empirical study of patterns in log-related statements within privacy policies and their alignment with privacy disclosures observed in Android application logs. We analyzed 1,000 Android apps across multiple categories, generating 86,836,964 log entries. Our findings reveal that while most applications (88.0%) provide privacy policies, only 28.5% explicitly mention logging practices. Among those that reference logging, most clearly describe what information is logged; however, 27.7% of log-related statements remain overly simplistic or vague, offering limited insight into actual data collection. We further observed widespread privacy leakages in application logs, with 67.6% of apps leaking sensitive information not mentioned in their policies. Alarmingly, only 0.4% of applications demonstrated consistent alignment between declared policy contents and actual logged data. These findings highlight that current privacy policies provide incomplete or ambiguous descriptions of logging practices, which frequently do not align with actual logging behaviors.

</details>


### [74] [Towards Optimal Agentic Architectures for Offensive Security Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18718v1)
*Isaac David,Arthur Gervais*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究agent架构拓扑对安全任务的影响，有通用agent设计结论

TL;DR: 本文通过构建包含20个交互目标的受控基准，系统评估了不同多智能体协调拓扑的渗透测试效果，发现可观察性和领域是主要因素，且存在非单调的成本-质量前沿。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于主体的安全系统固定单一协调拓扑，不清楚额外主体何时有帮助或增加成本，因此需要经验性研究拓扑选择的影响。

Method: 构建了包含20个交互目标（10个Web/API和10个二进制）的受控基准，每个目标有一个端点可达的真实漏洞。在白盒和黑盒模式下，对五种架构族、三种模型族进行600次运行实验，并分析了Bootstrap置信区间和配对目标级别差异。

Result: 检测任何漏洞达到58.0%，有效检测达到49.8%。MAS-Indep取得最高有效检测率64.2%，SAS效率最高（0.058美元/有效发现）。白盒优于黑盒（67.0% vs 32.7%），Web优于二进制（74.3% vs 25.3%）。主要影响是可观察性和领域，存在非单调成本-质量前沿。

Conclusion: 更广泛的协调可提高覆盖率，但考虑延迟、令牌成本和利用验证难度后，并不占主导地位，即存在非单调的成本-质量前沿。

中文摘要：基于主体的安全系统越来越多地使用使用工具的LLM审计实时目标，但先前的系统固定单一协调拓扑，使得不清楚何时额外的主体有帮助以及何时只会增加成本。我们将拓扑选择视为一个经验性的系统问题。我们引入了一个受控基准，包含20个交互式目标（10个Web/API和10个二进制），每个目标暴露一个端点可达的真实漏洞，在白盒和黑盒模式下进行评估。核心研究在五种架构族、三种模型族和两种访问模式下执行了600次运行，另有60次运行的长上下文试点仅在附录中报告。在完成的核心基准上，检测任何漏洞达到58.0%，有效检测达到49.8%。MAS-Indep实现了最高的有效检测率（64.2%），而SAS是最强的效率基线，每个有效发现0.058美元。白盒显著优于黑盒（有效检测67.0% vs 32.7%），Web显著优于二进制（74.3% vs 25.3%）。Bootstrap置信区间和配对目标级别差异表明，主要影响是可观察性和领域，而一些领先的白盒拓扑在统计上接近。主要结果是一个非单调的成本-质量前沿：更广泛的协调可以提高覆盖范围，但一旦考虑延迟、令牌成本和利用验证难度，它就不占主导地位。

Original abstract: Agentic security systems increasingly audit live targets with tool-using LLMs, but prior systems fix a single coordination topology, leaving unclear when additional agents help and when they only add cost. We treat topology choice as an empirical systems question. We introduce a controlled benchmark of 20 interactive targets (10 web/API and 10 binary), each exposing one endpoint-reachable ground-truth vulnerability, evaluated in whitebox and blackbox modes. The core study executes 600 runs over five architecture families, three model families, and both access modes, with a separate 60-run long-context pilot reported only in the appendix. On the completed core benchmark, detection-any reaches 58.0% and validated detection reaches 49.8%. MAS-Indep attains the highest validated detection rate (64.2%), while SAS is the strongest efficiency baseline at $0.058 per validated finding. Whitebox materially outperforms blackbox (67.0% vs. 32.7% validated detection), and web materially outperforms binary (74.3% vs. 25.3%). Bootstrap confidence intervals and paired target-level deltas show that the dominant effects are observability and domain, while some leading whitebox topologies remain statistically close. The main result is a non-monotonic cost-quality frontier: broader coordination can improve coverage, but it does not dominate once latency, token cost, and exploit-validation difficulty are taken into account.

</details>


### [75] [Temporal UI State Inconsistency in Desktop GUI Agents: Formalizing and Defending Against TOCTOU Attacks on Computer-Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18860v1)
*Wenpeng Xu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 针对桌面GUI agent的TOCTOU攻击与防御，直接涉及agent安全。

TL;DR: 提出视觉原子性违反漏洞，三种攻击原语及PUSV三层防御，实验证明对前两种攻击100%拦截，对DOM注入无效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GUI代理存在观察-行动间隙导致的TOCTOU漏洞，攻击者可在用户操作前篡改UI状态，亟需防御方案。

Method: 形式化视觉原子性违反，设计Notification Overlay Hijack、Window Focus Manipulation、Web DOM Injection三种攻击原语，并提出PUSV三层防御：L1掩码像素SSIM、L2a全局截图差异、L2b X窗口快照差异。

Result: PUSV对原语A和B实现100%拦截率（180次试验），零误报，开销<0.1秒；但对原语C（DOM注入）拦截率约0%，揭示盲点。

Conclusion: 不同攻击原语需要不同检测信号，单层防御不够，需分层设计；未来应结合OS和DOM层面的深度防御。

中文摘要：通过截图-点击循环控制桌面计算机的GUI代理引入了一类新的漏洞：观察-行动间隙（在真实OSWorld工作负载上平均6.51秒）创建了一个检查时间、使用时间（TOCTOU）窗口，在此期间，非特权攻击者可以操纵UI状态。我们将此形式化为视觉原子性违反，并描述了三种具体的攻击原语：（A）通知覆盖劫持，（B）窗口焦点操纵，以及（C）Web DOM注入。原语B是Android动作重新绑定的最接近桌面模拟，在观察时零视觉证据的情况下实现了100%的动作重定向成功率。我们提出了执行前UI状态验证（PUSV），一种轻量级的三层防御，在每个动作调度前立即重新验证UI状态：点击目标处的掩码像素SSIM（L1）、全局截图差异（L2a）和X窗口快照差异（L2b）。PUSV在180次对抗性试验（135次原语A + 45次原语B）中实现了100%的动作拦截率，零误报且开销小于0.1秒。针对原语C（零视觉足迹DOM注入），PUSV揭示了一个结构性盲点（约0% AIR），这推动了未来操作系统+DOM深度防御架构的发展。没有单一的PUSV层能够单独实现全面覆盖；不同的原语需要不同的检测信号，验证了分层设计。

Original abstract: GUI agents that control desktop computers via screenshot-and-click loops introduce a new class of vulnerability: the observation-to-action gap (mean 6.51 s on real OSWorld workloads) creates a Time-Of-Check, Time-Of-Use (TOCTOU) window during which an unprivileged attacker can manipulate the UI state. We formalize this as a Visual Atomicity Violation and characterize three concrete attack primitives: (A) Notification Overlay Hijack, (B) Window Focus Manipulation, and (C) Web DOM Injection. Primitive B, the closest desktop analog to Android Action Rebinding, achieves 100% action-redirection success rate with zero visual evidence at the observation time. We propose Pre-execution UI State Verification (PUSV), a lightweight three-layer defense that re-verifies the UI state immediately before each action dispatch: masked pixel SSIM at the click target (L1), global screenshot diff (L2a), and X Window snapshot diff (L2b). PUSV achieves 100% Action Interception Rate across 180 adversarial trials (135 Primitive A + 45 Primitive B) with zero false positives and < 0.1 s overhead. Against Primitive C (zero-visual-footprint DOM injection), PUSV reveals a structural blind spot (~0% AIR), motivating future OS+DOM defense-in-depth architectures. No single PUSV layer alone achieves full coverage; different primitives require different detection signals, validating the layered design.

</details>

### [76] [Proxics: an efficient programming model for far memory accelerators](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18120v1)
*Zikai Liu,Niels Pressel,Jasmin Schult,Roman Meier,Pengcheng Xu,Timothy Roscoe*

Main category: cs.OS

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 针对近数据处理加速器，提出基于进程和管道等OS抽象的高效轻量编程模型，并通过实际硬件验证其对批量内存、内存数据库和图应用的性能优势，强调CPU与NDP间低延迟通信的关键性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有近数据处理加速器缺乏清晰可移植的操作系统抽象来编程，而直接套用经典进程和IPC机制因其重量级和不匹配带宽优化目标而不适用。

Method: 通过编译和互连协议优化，在NDP设备上轻量高效地实现虚拟处理器（进程）和进程间通信通道（类似Unix管道）抽象。

Result: 在真实硬件平台上，该模型在批量内存操作、内存数据库和图应用中相比仅CPU实现展现出性能优势，并证明CPU与NDP间高效低延迟通信的重要性。

Conclusion: 所提编程模型有效提升了NDP加速器的可编程性和性能，且高效通信通道是NDP系统设计中不可忽视的关键特征。

中文摘要：使用分解或远内存系统（如CXL内存池）重新引起了对近数据处理（NDP）的兴趣：将核心置于靠近内存的位置以减少与CPU之间的带宽需求。此类加速器的硬件设计正在涌现，但缺乏清晰、可移植的OS抽象来对其进行编程。我们提出了一种基于熟悉OS抽象的NDP设备编程模型：虚拟处理器（进程）和进程间通信通道（如Unix管道）。虽然从用户角度来看很有吸引力，但这种抽象的天真实现不适合NDP加速器：某些硬件设计中处理能力的缺乏使得经典进程过于重量级，而基于共享缓冲区的IPC在旨在减少内存带宽的系统中毫无意义。因此，我们展示了如何通过利用编译和互连协议以轻量且高效的方式实现这些抽象。我们通过一个真实的硬件平台演示了它们，该平台运行具有多种内存访问模式的应用，包括批量内存操作、内存数据库和图应用。至关重要的是，我们不仅展示了相对于仅CPU实现的优势，还展示了CPU与NDP加速器之间高效低延迟通信通道的关键重要性，这一特征在现有提议中基本被忽视。

Original abstract: The use of disaggregated or far memory systems such as CXL memory pools has renewed interest in Near-Data Processing (NDP): situating cores close to memory to reduce bandwidth requirements to and from the CPU. Hardware designs for such accelerators are appearing, but there lack clean, portable OS abstractions for programming them.
  We propose a programming model for NDP devices based on familiar OS abstractions: virtual processors (processes) and inter-process communication channels (like Unix pipes).
  While appealing from a user perspective, a naive implementation of such abstractions is inappropriate for NDP accelerators: the paucity of processing power in some hardware designs makes classical processes overly heavyweight, and IPC based on shared buffers makes no sense in a system designed to reduce memory bandwidth.
  Accordingly, we show how to implement these abstractions in a lightweight and efficient manner by exploiting compilation and interconnect protocols. We demonstrate them with a real hardware platform runing applications with a range of memory access patterns, including bulk memory operations, in-memory databases and graph applications.
  Crucially, we show not only the benefits over CPU-only implementations, but also the critical importance of efficient, low-latency communication channels between CPU and NDP accelerators, a feature largely neglected in existing proposals.

</details>

### [77] [Before You Interpret the Profile: Validity Scaling for LLM Metacognitive Self-Report](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17707v1)
*Jon-Paul Cacioli*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM置信度有效性评估，可辅助agent决策可靠性分析。

TL;DR: 将临床人格评估的效度筛选框架应用于LLM，操作化六个效度指标，识别出无效模型，并揭示有效与无效模型在置信度模式上的显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM评估缺乏像临床人格评估那样的反应效度筛选，可能使得基于LLM的评估结果不可靠，因此需要引入类似方法。

Method: 采用PAI和MMPI-3中的效度量表框架，对20个前沿模型在524个条目上的元认知探测数据进行分析，操作化L、K、F、Fp、RBS和TRIN六个效度指标，并通过分层分类系统进行模型分类。

Result: 四个模型被识别为构念无效，两个为升高；有效剖面模型的置信度与项目敏感性相关（平均r=0.18，14/16显著），无效剖面模型则无（平均r=-0.20，d=2.17，p=0.001）；思维链训练导致两种相反的反应扭曲；两个潜在维度解释了94.6%的指标方差。

Conclusion: 临床效度框架可成功迁移至LLM评估，并提取出便携式筛选协议，为LLM评估的可靠性提供了新工具。

中文摘要：临床人格评估在解释实质性量表之前会筛选反应效度。LLM评估则没有。我们将PAI和MMPI-3中的效度量表框架应用于来自20个前沿模型在524个条目上的元认知探测数据。操作化了六个效度指标：L（在错误上保持信心）、K（在错误上下注）、F（撤回共识认可的条目）、Fp（撤回正确答案）、RBS（反向监控）和TRIN（固定回答）。一个分层分类系统将四个模型识别为构念无效，两个为升高。有效剖面的模型产生项目敏感性置信度（平均r = .18，16个中的14个显著）。无效剖面的模型则不然（平均r = -.20，d = 2.17，p = .001）。思维链训练产生了两种相反的反应扭曲。两个潜在维度解释了94.6%的指标方差。配套论文提取了一个可移植的筛选协议（Cacioli, 2026e）并针对选择性预测进行了验证（Cacioli, 2026f）。所有数据和代码：https://github.com/synthiumjp/validity-scaling-llm

Original abstract: Clinical personality assessment screens response validity before interpreting substantive scales. LLM evaluation does not. We apply the validity scaling framework from the PAI and MMPI-3 to metacognitive probe data from 20 frontier models across 524 items. Six validity indices are operationalised: L (maintaining confidence on errors), K (betting on errors), F (withdrawing consensus-endorsed items), Fp (withdrawing correct answers), RBS (inverted monitoring), and TRIN (fixed responding). A tiered classification system identifies four models as construct-level invalid and two as elevated. Valid-profile models produce item-sensitive confidence (mean r = .18, 14 of 16 significant). Invalid-profile models do not (mean r = -.20, d = 2.17, p = .001). Chain-of-thought training produces two opposite response distortions. Two latent dimensions account for 94.6% of index variance. Companion papers extract a portable screening protocol (Cacioli, 2026e) and validate it against selective prediction (Cacioli, 2026f). All data and code: https://github.com/synthiumjp/validity-scaling-llm

</details>


### [78] [Screen Before You Interpret: A Portable Validity Protocol for Benchmark-Based LLM Confidence Signals](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17714v1)
*Jon-Paul Cacioli*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM置信度信号便携式有效性协议，适用于agent决策质量监控。

TL;DR: 将临床人格评估中的有效性筛查原则转移至LLM置信度数据，提出新协议，在20个模型上验证，有效与无效模型置信度与准确性相关性差异显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前缺乏标准方法来验证LLM置信度信号是否携带项目级信息，导致基于置信度的决策可能不可靠。

Method: 借鉴临床人格评估中的有效性筛查原则，设计包含三个核心指标（L, Fp, RBS）、一个结构指标（TRIN）和项目敏感性统计量的协议，基于2×2列联表计算，并采用三级分类系统。

Result: 在20个前沿LLM上，4个模型被分类为无效，2个为不确定；有效剖面模型置信度与准确性平均相关系数r=0.18，无效剖面模型r=-0.20（d=2.48），跨基准验证显示方法可迁移。

Conclusion: 该协议可有效筛选LLM置信度信号的有效性，且跨基准和探针格式可转移，为可靠使用置信度信号提供了新工具。

中文摘要：LLM置信度信号用于弃权、路由和安全关键决策。目前尚无标准做法来检查置信度信号在构建于其之上之前是否携带项目级信息。我们将临床人格评估（PAI, MMPI-3）中的有效性筛查原则转移为一种基于基准的LLM置信度数据的便携协议。该协议指定了三个核心指标（L, Fp, RBS）、一个结构指标（TRIN）和一个项目敏感性统计量，均基于单个2×2列联表计算。三级分类系统（无效、不确定、有效）借鉴了四种临床传统。在524个项目上的20个前沿LLM上验证，四个模型被分类为无效，两个为不确定。有效剖面模型的平均r值为0.18（15/16显著）。无效剖面模型的平均r值为-0.20（d=2.48）。使用MMLU与言语化置信度的18个模型的跨基准验证以及Yang等人（2024）的外部数据证实了该筛查方法可跨基准和探针格式转移。所有数据和代码：https://github.com/synthiumjp/validity-scaling-llm

Original abstract: LLM confidence signals are used for abstention, routing, and safety-critical decisions. No standard practice exists for checking whether a confidence signal carries item-level information before building on it. We transfer the validity screening principle from clinical personality assessment (PAI, MMPI-3) as a portable protocol for benchmark-based LLM confidence data. The protocol specifies three core indices (L, Fp, RBS), a structural indicator (TRIN), and an item-sensitivity statistic, computed from a single 2x2 contingency table. A three-tier classification system (Invalid, Indeterminate, Valid) draws on four clinical traditions. Validated on 20 frontier LLMs across 524 items, four models are classified Invalid, two Indeterminate. Valid-profile models show mean r = .18 (15/16 significant). Invalid-profile models show mean r = -.20 (d = 2.48). Cross-benchmark validation on 18 models using MMLU with verbalized confidence and on external data from Yang et al. (2024) confirms the screen transfers across benchmarks and probe formats. All data and code: https://github.com/synthiumjp/validity-scaling-llm

</details>


### [79] [Concurrent Criterion Validation of a Validity Screen for LLM Confidence Signals via Selective Prediction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17716v1)
*Jon-Paul Cacioli*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 置信度有效性筛选与选择性预测验证，可迁移至agent的可靠执行评估。

TL;DR: 效度筛查的三层分类（有效、不确定、无效）能显著预测LLM的选择性预测性能，且分类解释了大量AUROC方差，其中有效模型表现最好，无效模型最差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证效度筛查是否能够预测LLM的选择性预测性能，从而为置信度校准提供有效工具。

Method: 对来自7个家族的20个前沿LLM进行6个认知轨道共524个项目的评估，使用效度筛查将置信度信号分为三类，并计算类型2 AUROC等指标，进行统计检验和交叉验证。

Result: 有效模型AUROC均值0.624，无效模型0.357，Cohen's d=2.81；三级分类解释47%方差；DeepSeek-R1在低覆盖率下性能急剧下降。

Conclusion: 效度筛查能有效预测LLM的选择性预测性能，对实际应用中的置信度评估具有重要价值。

中文摘要：效度筛查（Cacioli, 2026d, 2026e）将LLM置信度信号分类为有效、不确定或无效。我们测试这些分类是否预测选择性预测性能。对七个家族的20个前沿LLM在六个认知轨道的524个项目上进行了评估。有效模型显示平均类型2 AUROC = .624（SD = .048）。无效模型显示平均AUROC = .357（SD = .231）。Cohen's d = 2.81，p = .002。层级顺序单调：无效（.357）< 不确定（.554）< 有效（.624）。分半交叉验证在1000次分割中产生中位数d = 1.77，P(d > 0) = 1.0。三层分类解释了AUROC中47%的方差。DeepSeek-R1从全覆盖时的85.3%准确率下降到10%覆盖时的11.3%。该筛查预测了标准。对于选择性预测，筛查很重要。

Original abstract: The validity screen (Cacioli, 2026d, 2026e) classifies LLM confidence signals as Valid, Indeterminate, or Invalid. We test whether these classifications predict selective prediction performance. Twenty frontier LLMs from seven families were evaluated on 524 items across six cognitive tracks. Valid models show mean Type 2 AUROC = .624 (SD = .048). Invalid models show mean AUROC = .357 (SD = .231). Cohen's d = 2.81, p = .002. The tiers order monotonically: Invalid (.357) < Indeterminate (.554) < Valid (.624). Split-half cross-validation yields median d = 1.77, P(d > 0) = 1.0 across 1,000 splits. The three-tier classification accounts for 47% of the variance in AUROC. DeepSeek-R1 drops from 85.3% accuracy at full coverage to 11.3% at 10% coverage. The screen predicts the criterion. For selective prediction, the screen matters.

</details>


### [80] [PoQ-Judge: A Multi-Architecture Evaluation Framework for Cost-Aware Proof-of-Quality in Decentralized LLM Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11196v1)
*Arther Tian,Alex Ding,Frank Chen,Simon Wu,Aaron Chan*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: PoQ-Judge评估框架用于LLM推理质量，可迁移至agent输出评估。

TL;DR: PoQ-Judge是一个轻量级无参考的LLM输出质量评估框架，通过训练专用裁判模型实现高效评分，在QA任务上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 去中心化LLM推理网络需要一种轻量级、无参考的质量评估方法，用于质量证明（PoQ），以代替需要参考答案的现有评估器。

Method: 提出PoQ-Judge框架，训练三种架构（TextCNN、MiniLM、DeBERTa）作为裁判模型，采用两阶段训练（UltraFeedback+GPT标注数据），结合在线校准和级联评估策略。

Result: 最佳模型（DeBERTa）在保留测试集上达到0.747 Pearson相关系数，作为无参考组件在复合评分中达到0.645，匹配最佳参考评估器；级联评估降低72.7%成本且质量损失小；QA任务结果远优于摘要。

Conclusion: PoQ-Judge有效实现无参考质量评估，但代理质量仍是主要限制，尤其在摘要任务上，需进一步提升代理质量。

中文摘要：去中心化的LLM推理网络需要轻量级、无参考的质量评估用于质量证明（PoQ）。我们提出了PoQ-Judge，一个训练专用裁判模型来对查询-输出对进行评分而无须真实参考的框架。我们研究了三种架构在质量-成本权衡上的表现：TextCNN裁判、MiniLM交叉编码器和DeBERTa裁判。使用在UltraFeedback加上GPT标记的领域内数据上的两阶段训练，最佳模型在保留测试集上与真实代理的皮尔逊相关系数达到0.747，优于先前工作中基于参考的评估器。作为复合评分中的无参考组件，它达到了0.645的皮尔逊相关系数，与最佳单一基于参考的评估器相匹配，同时消除了对参考答案的需求。我们还展示了在线校准将语义质量识别为主导维度，并且级联评估将成本降低了72.7%，而质量损失很小。在问答上的结果远优于摘要，指出代理质量是主要剩余限制。

Original abstract: Decentralized LLM inference networks need lightweight, reference-free quality evaluation for Proof of Quality (PoQ). We present PoQ-Judge, a framework that trains dedicated judge models to score query-output pairs without ground-truth references. We study three architectures across the quality-cost tradeoff: a TextCNN judge, a MiniLM cross-encoder, and a DeBERTa judge. Using two-stage training on UltraFeedback plus GPT-labeled in-domain data, the best model reaches 0.747 Pearson correlation with the ground-truth proxy on a held-out test set, outperforming reference-based evaluators from prior work. As a reference-free component in composite scoring, it achieves 0.645 Pearson correlation, matching the best single reference-based evaluator while removing the need for reference answers. We also show that online calibration identifies semantic quality as the dominant dimension and that cascade evaluation reduces cost by 72.7 percent with only modest quality loss. Results are much stronger on QA than summarization, pointing to proxy quality as the main remaining limitation.

</details>


### [81] [MHSafeEval: Role-Aware Interaction-Level Evaluation of Mental Health Safety in Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17730v1)
*Suhyun Lee,Palakorn Achananuparp,Neemesh Yadav,Ee-Peng Lim,Yang Deng*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: MHSafeEval基于agent的多轮对话安全评估，可借鉴agent安全评估方法论。

TL;DR: 提出了角色感知的心理健康安全分类法R-MHSafe和闭环评估框架MHSafeEval，通过对抗性多轮交互发现LLM在咨询中的角色依赖和累积性安全失败，显著提升诊断粒度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM心理健康咨询安全评估框架仅评估孤立回应，无法诊断多轮交互中危害的积累和角色依赖。

Method: 提出R-MHSafe角色感知分类法（肇事者、煽动者、促进者、纵容者）和MHSafeEval闭环对抗性多轮交互评估框架。

Result: 大规模评估显示现有静态基准遗漏大量角色依赖和累积性安全失败，新框架显著提升失败模式覆盖率和诊断粒度。

Conclusion: R-MHSafe和MHSafeEval能更有效地发现LLM在心理健康咨询中的临床安全风险。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）正被越来越多地探索作为心理健康的可扩展工具，但由于临床危害的交互性和情境依赖性，评估其安全性仍然具有挑战性。现有的评估框架主要使用粗粒度的分类法或静态数据集评估孤立的回应，限制了其诊断危害如何在多轮咨询互动中出现和积累的能力。在这项工作中，我们引入了R-MHSafe，一个角色感知的心理健康安全分类法，根据AI咨询师采纳的交互角色（包括肇事者、煽动者、促进者或纵容者）结合临床基础的危害类别来表征临床显著的危害。然后，我们提出了MHSafeEval，一个闭环的、基于智能体的评估框架，将安全评估制定为通过对抗性多轮交互发现危害的轨迹级发现，由角色感知建模引导。使用R-MHSafe和MHSafeEval，我们对最先进的LLM进行了大规模评估。我们的结果揭示了现有静态基准系统性地遗漏的显著的角色依赖和累积性安全失败，并表明我们的框架显著提高了失败模式覆盖率和诊断粒度。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly explored as scalable tools for mental health counseling, yet evaluating their safety remains challenging due to the interactional and context-dependent nature of clinical harm. Existing evaluation frameworks predominantly assess isolated responses using coarse-grained taxonomies or static datasets, limiting their ability to diagnose how harms emerge and accumulate over multi-turn counseling interactions. In this work, we introduce R-MHSafe, a role-aware mental health safety taxonomy that characterizes clinically significant harm in terms of the interactional roles an AI counselor adopts, including perpetrator, instigator, facilitator, or enabler, combined with clinically grounded harm categories. Then, we propose MHSafeEval, a closed-loop, agent-based evaluation framework that formulates safety assessment as trajectory-level discovery of harm through adversarial multi-turn interactions, guided by role-aware modeling. Using R-MHSafe and MHSafeEval, we conduct a large-scale evaluation across state-of-the-art LLMs. Our results reveal substantial role-dependent and cumulative safety failures that are systematically missed by existing static benchmarks, and show that our framework significantly improves failure-mode coverage and diagnostic granularity.

</details>


### [82] [PDDL-Mind: Large Language Models are Capable on Belief Reasoning with Reliable State Tracking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17819v1)
*Wang Bill Zhu,Qiutong Tony Yi,Robin Jia,Jesse Thomason*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 神经符号框架用于信念推理，通过PDDL状态跟踪增强LLM规划，对agent规划有启发

TL;DR: 提出PDDL-Mind神经符号框架，通过显式翻译叙事为PDDL状态和动作，提升LLM在心理理论任务上的准确率，优于现有方法5%以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在心理理论基准上表现不佳，主要原因是隐式状态跟踪不可靠，而非推理能力不足。

Method: PDDL-Mind框架将叙事描述翻译为PDDL形式的状态和动作，并验证动作引发的状态转换，为LLM提供逻辑一致的世界状态表示。

Result: 在MMToM-QA、MuMA和FanToM基准上，PDDL-Mind相比现有最佳方法获得超过5%的绝对准确率提升。

Conclusion: 显式状态跟踪比隐式推理更有效，神经符号方法能显著提升LLM的心理理论能力。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在现有心理理论（ToM）基准上的表现远低于人类水平，即使通过链式思维提示或概率信念更新进行增强也是如此。我们认为这些失败主要源于不可靠的隐式状态跟踪，而非高层推理的限制。我们引入了PDDL-Mind，一个神经符号框架，将环境状态演化与信念推断解耦。通过将叙事描述翻译为以规划领域定义语言（PDDL）表达的显式状态和动作，并验证动作引发的状态转换是否满足预定义领域，PDDL-Mind为LLMs提供了逻辑一致且显式的世界状态表示以用于ToM任务。在MMToM-QA、MuMA和FanToM上的实验表明，PDDL-Mind在ToM基准问题上相比现有最佳方法取得了超过5%的绝对准确率提升。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) perform substantially below human level on existing theory-of-mind (ToM) benchmarks, even when augmented with chain-of-thought prompting or probabilistic belief updates. We argue that these failures primarily arise from unreliable implicit state tracking rather than limitations in high-level reasoning. We introduce PDDL-Mind, a neuro-symbolic framework that decouples environment state evolution from belief inference. By translating narrative descriptions into explicit states and actions expressed in Planning Domain Definition Language (PDDL), and by verifying action-induced state transitions against a predefined domain, PDDL-Mind provides LLMs with a logically consistent and explicit representation of world states for ToM tasks. Experiments on MMToM-QA, MuMA and FanToM show that PDDL-Mind achieves over 5% absolute accuracy gain over the best existing state-of-the-art method on ToM benchmark questions.

</details>


### [83] [Latent Abstraction for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17866v2)
*Ha Lan N. T,Minh-Anh Nguyen,Dung D. Le*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出隐空间检索框架LAnR，统一向量检索与生成，可潜在地用于agent内存检索与工具调用。

TL;DR: LAnR是一个统一框架，让单个LLM在其潜在空间内联合进行编码、检索和生成，通过隐藏状态向量检索并自适应停止，提升RAG效率和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG方法依赖自然语言查询和分离的检索器-生成器架构，限制了LLM表示能力的利用，导致检索调用多、效率低。

Method: LAnR使用LLM的[PRED]标记隐藏状态生成稠密检索向量，与文档编码匹配，并通过MLP控制头基于隐藏状态自适应决定检索停止，无需文本查询和独立检索器。

Result: 在六个QA基准（单跳和多跳）上，LAnR优于现有RAG方法，同时减少检索调用次数，提升推理效率。

Conclusion: LAnR通过统一潜在空间操作，实现了更高效的检索增强生成，验证了答案标记熵作为检索充分性指标的可靠性。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）已成为一种标准方法，用于通过外部知识增强大型语言模型（LLM），减轻幻觉并提高事实性。然而，现有系统依赖于在每一步生成自然语言查询，并保持检索器和生成器之间的严格架构分离，从而无法充分利用LLM的全部表示能力。我们提出LAnR（用于RAG的潜在抽象），一个统一的框架，其中单个LLM在其自身的潜在空间内联合执行编码、检索和生成。LAnR不生成文本查询，而是从指定[PRED]标记的隐藏状态生成稠密检索向量，并使用它们与来自同一模型的编码文档表示进行匹配。此外，LAnR通过一个轻量级MLP控制头，基于相同的隐藏状态自适应地决定何时已检索到足够的证据，从而消除了独立的检索器和显式的词级停止推理。这一设计源于我们的经验观察：答案标记熵能够可靠地指示检索的充分性。在涵盖单跳和多跳设置的六个QA基准上的广泛实验表明，LAnR优于现有的RAG方法，同时通过减少检索调用次数和更紧密的模型集成实现了更高的推理效率。

Original abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has become a standard approach for enhancing large language models (LLMs) with external knowledge, mitigating hallucinations, and improving factuality. However, existing systems rely on generating natural language queries at each hop and maintaining a strict architectural separation between retriever and generator, preventing them from leveraging the full representational capacity of the LLM. We propose \textbf{LAnR} (Latent Abstraction for RAG), a unified framework in which a single LLM jointly performs encoding, retrieval, and generation entirely within its own latent space. Rather than generating textual queries, LAnR produces dense retrieval vectors from the hidden states of a designated \texttt{[PRED]} token and uses them to match against encoded document representations from the same model. Furthermore, LAnR adaptively decides when sufficient evidence has been retrieved using a lightweight MLP control head over those same hidden states, eliminating both the separate retriever and explicit token-level stopping reasoning. This design is motivated by our empirical observation that answer token entropy reliably signals retrieval sufficiency. Extensive experiments on six QA benchmarks spanning single-hop and multi-hop settings demonstrate that LAnR outperforms existing RAG methods, while achieving improved inference efficiency through reduced number of retrieval calls and tighter model integration.

</details>


### [84] [Latent Preference Modeling for Cross-Session Personalized Tool Calling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17886v1)
*Yejin Yoon,Minseo Kim,Taeuk Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 引入跨会话个性化工具调用与记忆偏好建模，直接提升agent工具使用的适应性。

TL;DR: 我们提出了MPT基准和PRefine方法，通过记忆增强的个性化来解决LLM代理中用户请求不充分导致的工具使用问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 用户经常在请求中遗漏关键细节，导致工具使用输入不充分，凸显了个性化工具调用的必要性。

Method: 我们提出PRefine，一种测试时记忆增强方法，将用户偏好表示为不断演化的假设，并通过生成-验证-优化循环从历史中提取可复用的约束。

Result: PRefine提高了工具调用准确性，同时仅使用全历史提示所需标记的1.24%。

Conclusion: 代理系统中的鲁棒个性化依赖于捕获用户选择背后原因的记忆，而不仅仅是选择本身。

中文摘要：用户经常在向基于LLM的代理提出请求时遗漏关键细节，导致工具使用的输入不充分。这对工具增强型代理构成了根本性挑战，因为API执行通常需要完整的参数，凸显了个性化工具调用的必要性。为了研究这个问题，我们引入了MPT，一个包含265个多会话对话的基准，涵盖三个挑战：偏好回忆、偏好归纳和偏好转移。我们还提出了PRefine，一种测试时记忆增强方法，将用户偏好表示为不断演化的假设。通过“生成-验证-优化”循环，它从历史中提取可复用的约束，并提高工具调用准确性，同时仅使用全历史提示所需标记的1.24%。这些结果表明，代理系统中的鲁棒个性化依赖于捕获用户选择背后原因的记忆，而不仅仅是选择本身。

Original abstract: Users often omit essential details in their requests to LLM-based agents, resulting in under-specified inputs for tool use. This poses a fundamental challenge for tool-augmented agents, as API execution typically requires complete arguments, highlighting the need for personalized tool calling. To study this problem, we introduce MPT, a benchmark comprising 265 multi-session dialogues that cover three challenges: Preference Recall, Preference Induction, and Preference Transfer. We also propose PRefine, a test-time memory-augmented method that represents user preferences as evolving hypotheses. Through a generate--verify--refine loop, it extracts reusable constraints from history and improves tool-calling accuracy while using only 1.24% of the tokens required by full-history prompting. These results indicate that robust personalization in agentic systems depends on memory that captures the reasons behind user choices, not just the choices themselves.

</details>


### [85] [STaD: Scaffolded Task Design for Identifying Compositional Skill Gaps in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18177v2)
*Sungeun An,Swanand Ravindra Kadhe,Shailja Thakur,Chad DeLuca,Hima Patel*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 识别LLM组合技能差距框架，可评估agent能力

TL;DR: 提出STaD框架，通过结构化任务变体系统性地探测LLM在推理任务中的技能组合缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合的基准测试分数无法揭示LLM在组合技能方面的具体缺陷，需要更精细的方法来识别和改进这些弱点。

Method: 基于脚手架概念，生成基准任务的可控变体，引入结构化、渐进的支持，以逐步方式系统性地探测模型行为。

Result: 在六个不同大小的模型上的实验揭示了三个推理基准中的多个失败点，并突出了每个模型独特且不同的技能差距。

Conclusion: STaD框架能够有效暴露LLM在推理任务中的技能组合缺陷，有助于针对性地改进模型能力。

中文摘要：基准测试通常被用作理解LLM在不同领域能力的一个标准。然而，聚合的基准测试分数对于揭示LLM在组合技能方面的缺陷以及如何改进它们提供的洞察有限。为了使这些弱点可见，我们提出了脚手架式任务设计（STaD）框架。STaD基于脚手架的概念生成基准任务的可控变体，脚手架以逐步的方式引入结构化、渐进的支持。这种方法不是单独检查失败，而是通过识别模型缺乏的特定推理技能组合，实现对模型行为的系统性和可扩展性探测。将LLM视为黑箱，我们在六个不同大小的模型上的实验揭示了三个推理基准中的多个失败点，并突出了每个模型独特且不同的技能差距。

Original abstract: Benchmarks are often used as a standard to understand LLM capabilities in different domains. However, aggregate benchmark scores provide limited insight into compositional skill gaps of LLMs and how to improve them. To make these weaknesses visible, we propose Scaffolded Task Design (STaD) framework. STaD generates controlled variations of benchmark tasks based on the concept of scaffolding, which introduces structured, incremental support in a step-by-step manner. Rather than inspecting failures individually, this approach enables systematic and scalable probing of model behavior by identifying the specific reasoning skill compositions they lack. Treating the LLM as a black box, our experiments on six models of varying sizes reveal multiple failure points in three reasoning benchmarks and highlight each model's unique and distinct skill gaps.

</details>


### [86] [Negative Advantages Is a Double-Edged Sword: Calibrating advantages in GRPO for Search Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18235v2)
*Jiayi Wu,Ruobing Xie,Zeqian Huang,Lei Jiang,Can Xu,Kangyang Luo,Bochen Lin,Ming Gao,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 针对搜索agent的GRPO优势校准方法，可迁移至coding agent训练。

TL;DR: 提出CalibAdv优势校准方法，解决GRPO在多跳搜索中因粗粒度优势分配和正负优势不平衡导致的训练不稳定和中间步骤惩罚问题，提升了模型性能和训练稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO算法在多跳搜索中存在正确中间步骤被惩罚、训练不稳定甚至崩溃的问题，原因是粗粒度优势分配和正负优势不平衡。

Method: CalibAdv利用中间步骤的正确性在细粒度上降低过大的负优势，然后重新平衡正负优势，采用轻量级设计从标准rollout信号校准优势。

Result: 在三个模型和七个基准上的实验表明，CalibAdv提高了模型性能和训练稳定性。

Conclusion: CalibAdv有效改进了搜索代理的GRPO训练，实现了更准确稳定的优势校准。

中文摘要：搜索代理通过与搜索引擎的多轮交互实现了强大的问答性能，其中群体相对策略优化（GRPO）是一种广泛使用的训练算法。然而，GRPO风格的算法在多跳搜索设置中仍然面临若干挑战。首先，当最终答案错误时，正确的中间步骤常常受到惩罚。其次，训练高度不稳定，常常导致自然语言能力下降甚至灾难性的训练崩溃。我们的分析将这些归因于粗粒度的优势分配以及正负优势之间的不平衡。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了CalibAdv，一种专门为搜索代理设计的优势校准方法，能够更准确、更稳定地对惩罚和奖励进行建模。具体来说，CalibAdv利用中间步骤的正确性在细粒度上降低过大的负优势。然后进一步重新平衡正负优势以提高训练稳定性。重要的是，CalibAdv采用轻量级设计，从标准的rollout信号中校准优势，使其简单易部署。跨三个模型和七个基准的大量实验表明，CalibAdv提高了模型性能和训练稳定性。我们的代码可在https://github.com/wujwyi/CalibAdv获取。

Original abstract: Search agents achieve strong question-answering performance through multi-turn interactions with search engines, with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) being a widely used training algorithm. However, GRPO-style algorithms still face several challenges in multi-hop search settings. First, correct intermediate steps are often penalized when the final answer is wrong. Second, training is highly unstable, often causing degradation of natural language ability or even catastrophic training collapse. Our analysis attributes these issues to coarse-grained advantage assignment and an imbalance between positive and negative advantages. To address these problems, we propose CalibAdv, an advantage calibration method specifically designed for search agents that enables more accurate and more stable modeling of penalties and rewards. Specifically, CalibAdv leverages the correctness of intermediate steps to downscale excessive negative advantages at a fine-grained level. It then further rebalances positive and negative advantages to improve training stability. Importantly, CalibAdv adopts a lightweight design that calibrates advantages from standard rollout signals, making it simple and easy to deploy. Extensive experiments across three models and seven benchmarks demonstrate that CalibAdv improves both model performance and training stability. Our code is available at https://github.com/wujwyi/CalibAdv.

</details>


### [87] [Characterizing AlphaEarth Embedding Geometry for Agentic Environmental Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18715v1)
*Mashrekur Rahman,Samuel J. Barrett,Christina Last*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出环境推理agent系统，含工具和推理链，但领域垂直，通用性有限

TL;DR: 通过分析地球观测嵌入的非欧几里得流形几何，构建了基于检索的智能体系统，验证了几何理解对复杂环境推理的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地球观测基础模型的嵌入几何结构未被充分探索，但可能影响下游推理性能，因此需要表征流形并利用几何知识改进推理。

Method: 基于1200万样本分析AlphaEarth的64维嵌入流形（有效维数、切空间旋转等），开发含九种工具的智能体系统，通过FAISS索引进行检索增强推理，并进行消融实验和跨模型基准测试。

Result: 流形非欧几里得，检索优于向量算术；智能体系统中检索主导响应质量，多步比较最优；几何工具对强模型（Opus）有益，对弱模型（Sonnet）略有损害。

Conclusion: 理解嵌入几何能够提升环境推理性能，但收益依赖于模型本身的推理能力，强模型更能利用几何特征进行有效推理。

中文摘要：地球观测基础模型将地表信息编码为密集的嵌入向量，然而这些表示的几何结构及其对下游推理的影响仍未得到充分探索。我们通过1200万美国大陆样本（2017-2023年）描述了Google AlphaEarth的64维嵌入的流形几何结构，并开发了一个利用这种几何理解进行环境推理的智能体系统。该流形是非欧几里得的：有效维数为13.3（参与率），来自64个原始维度，局部固有维数约为10。切空间大幅旋转，84%的位置超过60°，局部-全局对齐（平均|cosθ| = 0.17）接近随机基线0.125。监督线性探测表明，概念方向在流形上旋转，使用PCA推导和探测推导方向的组合向量算术产生较差的精度。相反，检索产生物理上一致的结果，局部几何预测检索一致性（R² = 0.32）。基于这一特征，我们引入了一个具有九个专门工具的智能体系统，它将环境查询分解为基于FAISS索引的嵌入数据库的推理链。五条件消融实验（120个查询，三个复杂度层级）表明，嵌入检索主导响应质量（μ= 3.79 ± 0.90 vs. 仅参数化μ= 3.03 ± 0.77；尺度1-5），在多步骤比较中达到峰值性能（μ= 4.28 ± 0.43）。跨模型基准测试表明，几何工具使Sonnet 4.5的分数降低0.12分，但使Opus 4.6的分数提高0.07分，Opus获得更高的几何基础（3.38 vs. 2.64），这表明几何特征的价值随着消费模型的推理能力而扩展。

Original abstract: Earth observation foundation models encode land surface information into dense embedding vectors, yet the geometric structure of these representations and its implications for downstream reasoning remain underexplored. We characterize the manifold geometry of Google AlphaEarth's 64-dimensional embeddings across 12.1 million Continental United States samples (2017--2023) and develop an agentic system that leverages this geometric understanding for environmental reasoning. The manifold is non-Euclidean: effective dimensionality is 13.3 (participation ratio) from 64 raw dimensions, with local intrinsic dimensionality of approximately 10. Tangent spaces rotate substantially, with 84\% of locations exceeding 60\textdegree{} and local-global alignment (mean$|\cosθ| = 0.17$) approaching the random baseline of 0.125. Supervised linear probes indicate that concept directions rotate across the manifold, and compositional vector arithmetic using both PCA-derived and probe-derived directions yields poor precision. Retrieval instead produces physically coherent results, with local geometry predicting retrieval coherence ($R^2 = 0.32$). Building on this characterization, we introduce an agentic system with nine specialized tools that decomposes environmental queries into reasoning chains over a FAISS-indexed embedding database. A five-condition ablation (120 queries, three complexity tiers) shows that embedding retrieval dominates response quality ($μ= 3.79 \pm 0.90$ vs.\ $3.03 \pm 0.77$ parametric-only; scale 1--5), with peak performance on multi-step comparisons ($μ= 4.28 \pm 0.43$). A cross-model benchmark show that geometric tools reduce Sonnet 4.5's score by 0.12 points but improve Opus 4.6's by 0.07, with Opus achieving higher geometric grounding (3.38 vs.\ 2.64), suggesting that the value of geometric characterization scales with the reasoning capability of the consuming model.

</details>


### [88] [Mango: Multi-Agent Web Navigation via Global-View Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18779v1)
*Weixi Tong,Yifeng Di,Tianyi Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent网络导航，含优化起点、bandit分配、情景记忆，对coding agent有直接参考

TL;DR: Mango是一种多代理网络导航方法，通过将URL选择建模为多臂老虎机问题并利用情景记忆，动态确定最佳起始点，显著提高了在深度层次网站上的导航成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网络代理从根URL开始探索，在复杂层次结构中效率低下，容易陷入导航陷阱或无法在预算内到达目标。

Method: 将URL选择建模为多臂老虎机问题，采用汤普森采样分配导航预算；引入情景记忆组件存储导航历史以实现学习。

Result: 在WebVoyager上成功率达63.6%（比基线高7.3%），在WebWalkerQA上达52.5%（比基线高26.8%）。

Conclusion: Mango通过动态确定起始点和学习历史，显著提升了网络导航的性能和泛化能力。

中文摘要：现有的网络代理通常从根URL开始探索，这对于具有深度层次结构的复杂网站来说效率低下。在没有网站结构全局视图的情况下，代理经常陷入导航陷阱，探索不相关的分支，或者无法在有限的预算内达到目标信息。我们提出了Mango，一种利用网站结构动态确定最佳起始点的多代理网络导航方法。我们将URL选择建模为多臂老虎机问题，并采用汤普森采样在候选URL间自适应分配导航预算。此外，我们引入了一个情景记忆组件来存储导航历史，使代理能够从先前的尝试中学习。在WebVoyager上的实验表明，使用GPT-5-mini时，Mango达到了63.6%的成功率，比最佳基线高出7.3%。此外，在WebWalkerQA上，Mango达到了52.5%的成功率，比最佳基线高出26.8%。我们还展示了Mango在使用开源和闭源模型作为骨干时的泛化能力。我们的数据和代码是开源的，可在https://github.com/VichyTong/Mango获取。

Original abstract: Existing web agents typically initiate exploration from the root URL, which is inefficient for complex websites with deep hierarchical structures. Without a global view of the website's structure, agents frequently fall into navigation traps, explore irrelevant branches, or fail to reach target information within a limited budget. We propose Mango, a multi-agent web navigation method that leverages the website structure to dynamically determine optimal starting points. We formulate URL selection as a multi-armed bandit problem and employ Thompson Sampling to adaptively allocate the navigation budget across candidate URLs. Furthermore, we introduce an episodic memory component to store navigation history, enabling the agent to learn from previous attempts. Experiments on WebVoyager demonstrate that Mango achieves a success rate of 63.6% when using GPT-5-mini, outperforming the best baseline by 7.3%. Furthermore, on WebWalkerQA, Mango attains a 52.5% success rate, surpassing the best baseline by 26.8%. We also demonstrate the generalizability of Mango using both open-source and closed-source models as backbones. Our data and code are open-source and available at https://github.com/VichyTong/Mango.

</details>

### [89] [CollabSkill: Evaluating Human-Agent Collaboration On Real-World Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09833v1)
*Yijia Shao,Zora Zhiruo Wang,Neel Ahuja,Yicheng Wang,Bowen Liu,Diyi Yang*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 人机协作评估框架CollabSkill，可用于agent协作能力基准测试。

TL;DR: CollabSkill通过真实人机协作实验和贝叶斯技能评级，揭示了与现有基准不同的代理排名，并发现实践经验是协作技能的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估缺乏真实人机协作数据且难以处理人际差异，导致人机协作潜力未被充分挖掘。

Method: 构建CollabSkill框架，配对真实工作者与AI代理执行职业任务，收集1500余条提示，使用贝叶斯技能评级系统分离量化技能贡献。

Result: Claude Code在CollabSkill排名第一，不同于Codex领先的自主基准；实践经验是协作技能主要驱动因素，显著提升AI素养。

Conclusion: CollabSkill可推动系统化人机协作评估，促进增强人类工作者的AI开发。

中文摘要：AI代理正在重塑工作场所，导致人类工作方式的急剧变化。尽管人机协作在维护人类主体性和创造经济价值方面具有巨大潜力，但这种范式在职业任务评估中仍然基本缺失，原因在于收集真实人类数据以及考虑人与人之间差异性的困难。我们提出了CollabSkill，一个用于评估真实世界职业任务中人机协作的框架。CollabSkill将真实人类工作者与AI代理配对，执行与其职业背景相匹配的任务，收集能够捕捉具有经济价值任务的复杂性和真实工作者使用模式的数据。为了考虑人与人之间的差异性，CollabSkill采用贝叶斯技能评级系统来分离并量化人类和AI代理的技能贡献。基于来自93名人类工作者的386个工作会话中的1500多个提示，我们的分析在两个方面提供了见解：在代理方面，CollabSkill上的排名与现有的完全自主基准（其中Codex领先）存在显著差异，而Claude Code排名第一；在人类方面，CollabSkill揭示实践经验是协作技能的主要驱动因素，实践协作显著改变了工作者的AI素养。我们共同希望CollabSkill能使社区投资于系统化的人机协作评估，并激发旨在构建真正增强人类工作者的AI代理的开发努力。

Original abstract: AI agents are reshaping the workspace, leading to drastic change of how humans work. Despite the considerable potential of human-agent collaboration both in preserving human agency and generating economic value, this paradigm remains largely absent from occupational task evaluation, hindered by the difficulty of gathering real human data and accounting for inter-human variability. We introduce CollabSkill, a framework for evaluating human-agent collaboration on real-world occupational tasks. CollabSkill pairs real human workers with AI agents on tasks matched to their occupational background, collecting data that capture the complexity of economically valuable tasks and the usage patterns of real workers. To account for inter-human variability, CollabSkill employs a Bayesian skill rating system to disentangle and quantify the skill contributions of both humans and AI agents. Drawing on over 1,500 prompts from 386 working sessions contributed by 93 human workers, our analysis yields insights on two fronts: on the agent side, rankings on CollabSkill diverge meaningfully from those of existing fully autonomous benchmarks where Codex leads, with Claude Code ranking first; on the human side, CollabSkill reveals that practical experience emerges as the primary driver of collaboration skill, with hands-on collaboration meaningfully shifting workers' AI literacy. Together, we hope CollabSkill enables the community to invest in systematic evaluation of human-agent collaboration and spurs development efforts aimed at building AI agents that genuinely augment human workers.

</details>


### [90] [Do LLMs Need to See Everything? A Benchmark and Study of Failures in LLM-driven Smartphone Automation using Screentext vs. Screenshots](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17817v1)
*Shiquan Zhang,Tianyi Zhang,Le Fang,Simon D'Alfonso,Hong Jia,Vassilis Kostakos*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 提出移动agent基准DailyDroid并分析失败模式，对编码agent评测有参考价值

TL;DR: 提出了DailyDroid基准测试，评估了LLM驱动的移动智能体在75个任务上的表现，发现多模态输入略优，并通过失败分析揭示了UI可访问性、输入模态和设计上的关键问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有移动智能体准确率低、常误解指令、难以处理复杂任务，但缺乏对其失败原因的深入分析。

Method: 构建DailyDroid基准，包含75个任务（5个场景、25个Android应用、3个难度级别），使用GPT-4o和o4-mini在300次试验中进行文本输入和多模态输入（文本+截图）评估，并进行失败分析。

Result: 文本输入和多模态输入性能相当，多模态输入成功率略高；通过失败分析编撰了常见失败手册，揭示了UI可访问性、输入模态和LLM/应用设计中的问题。

Conclusion: 研究成果为未来移动智能体、应用和UI开发提供了重要启示，指出了需要改进的关键领域。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLM）的快速发展，移动智能体已成为手机自动化的有前途工具，通过模拟屏幕上的用户交互来完成复杂任务。然而，这些智能体常常面临准确率低、用户指令理解错误以及困难任务失败的问题，而先前的研究很少深入探讨它们为何失败及在何处失败。为解决这一问题，我们引入了DailyDroid，这是一个包含75个任务、涵盖25个Android应用中五个场景、跨越三个难度级别的基准测试，旨在模拟日常智能手机使用。我们使用纯文本和多模态（文本+截图）输入在GPT-4o和o4-mini上进行了300次试验评估，结果显示两者性能相当，多模态输入的成功率略高。通过深入的失败分析，我们编制了一份常见失败手册。我们的发现揭示了UI可访问性、输入模态以及LLM/应用设计中的关键问题，为未来移动智能体、应用和UI开发提供了启示。

Original abstract: With the rapid advancement of large language models (LLMs), mobile agents have emerged as promising tools for phone automation, simulating human interactions on screens to accomplish complex tasks. However, these agents often suffer from low accuracy, misinterpretation of user instructions, and failure on challenging tasks, with limited prior work examining why and where they fail. To address this, we introduce DailyDroid, a benchmark of 75 tasks in five scenarios across 25 Android apps, spanning three difficulty levels to mimic everyday smartphone use. We evaluate it using text-only and multimodal (text + screenshot) inputs on GPT-4o and o4-mini across 300 trials, revealing comparable performance with multimodal inputs yielding marginally higher success rates. Through in-depth failure analysis, we compile a handbook of common failures. Our findings reveal critical issues in UI accessibility, input modalities, and LLM/app design, offering implications for future mobile agents, applications, and UI development.

### [91] [The Collaboration Gap in Human-AI Work](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18096v1)
*Varad Vishwarupe,Marina Jirotka,Nigel Shadbolt,Ivan Flechais*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 人机协作框架，讨论LLM协作的落地挑战，对agent交互设计有启发。

TL;DR: 本文通过访谈和文献分析，提出一个概念框架，解释为何人类与LLM的合作常常脆弱，并区分了三种工作结构（一次性帮助、不对称修复的弱合作、接地合作），强调接地条件的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM作为合作者的实际体验往往不如承诺，用户需要频繁诊断误解、重建假设和修复响应，因此需要理解合作脆弱性的根本原因。

Method: 对16位从事LLM驱动系统的设计师、开发者和应用AI从业者进行建构主义扎根理论分析，并结合人类-AI合作文献。

Result: 识别出三种反复出现的人类-LLM工作结构：一次性帮助、具有不对称修复的弱合作、接地合作；提出合作崩溃发生在伙伴关系外观超过互动接地能力时。

Conclusion: 稳定合作依赖于互动中的接地条件，而不仅仅是模型能力；贡献了一个讨论接地、修复和互动结构的框架，以改善LLM驱动工作中的协作。

中文摘要：LLMs are increasingly presented as collaborators in programming, design, writing, and analysis. Yet the practical experience of working with them often falls short of this promise. In many settings, users must diagnose misunderstandings, reconstruct missing assumptions, and repeatedly repair misaligned responses. This poster introduces a conceptual framework for understanding why such collaboration remains fragile. Drawing on a constructivist grounded theory analysis of 16 interviews with designers, developers, and applied AI practitioners working on LLM-enabled systems, and informed by literature on human-AI collaboration, we argue that stable collaboration depends not only on model capability but on the interaction's grounding conditions. We distinguish three recurrent structures of human-AI work: one-shot assistance, weak collaboration with asymmetric repair, and grounded collaboration. We propose that collaboration breaks down when the appearance of partnership outpaces the grounding capacity of the interaction and contribute a framework for discussing grounding, repair, and interaction structure in LLM-enabled work.

Original abstract: LLMs are increasingly presented as collaborators in programming, design, writing, and analysis. Yet the practical experience of working with them often falls short of this promise. In many settings, users must diagnose misunderstandings, reconstruct missing assumptions, and repeatedly repair misaligned responses. This poster introduces a conceptual framework for understanding why such collaboration remains fragile. Drawing on a constructivist grounded theory analysis of 16 interviews with designers, developers, and applied AI practitioners working on LLM-enabled systems, and informed by literature on human-AI collaboration, we argue that stable collaboration depends not only on model capability but on the interaction's grounding conditions. We distinguish three recurrent structures of human-AI work: one-shot assistance, weak collaboration with asymmetric repair, and grounded collaboration. We propose that collaboration breaks down when the appearance of partnership outpaces the grounding capacity of the interaction and contribute a framework for discussing grounding, repair, and interaction structure in LLM-enabled work.

</details>


### [92] [The Triadic Loop: A Framework for Negotiating Alignment in AI Co-hosted Livestreaming](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18850v1)
*Katherine Wang,Nadia Berthouze,Aneesha Singh*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 提出多actor对齐框架，可迁移到多agent协作设计。

TL;DR: 提出三元循环框架，将AI在直播中的对齐重新概念化为三方双向适应过程，并引入战略性失调等概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐框架局限于二元关系，无法应对直播中多用户动态交互，因此需要新框架。

Method: 基于文献综述和概念分析，提出三元循环框架、战略性失调机制及关系评估构念。

Result: 得到动态多方可对齐模型、跨循环强化机制及设计启示。

Conclusion: 框架有助于理解AI在直播中的社会角色，为设计维持社会一致性的AI联合主持提供指导。

中文摘要：AI系统越来越多地被嵌入到多用户社交环境中，然而大多数对齐框架将交互概念化为单个用户与AI系统之间的二元关系。直播平台挑战了这一假设：交互在主播和观众之间实时展开，产生动态的情感和社交反馈循环。在本文中，我们引入了三元循环（Triadic Loop）这一概念框架，将AI联合主持的直播中的对齐重新概念化为一个时间强化的双向适应过程，涉及三个参与者：主播↔AI联合主持、AI联合主持↔观众、以及主播↔观众。与指令遵循范式不同，双向对齐要求每个参与者持续重塑其他参与者，这意味着任何子循环中的失调都可能破坏整个系统的稳定性。借鉴多方可交互、协作AI和关系型代理的文献，我们阐述了AI联合主持如何不仅作为中介者，而且作为表演性参与者和社区成员，塑造集体意义形成。我们进一步提出“战略性失调”作为维持社区参与度的机制，并引入了三个基于已有工具的关系评估构念。该框架贡献了一个动态多方可对齐模型、跨循环强化机制，以及维持参与式媒体环境中社会一致性的AI联合主持的设计启示。

Original abstract: AI systems are increasingly embedded in multi-user social environments, yet most alignment frameworks conceptualize interaction as a dyadic relationship between a single user and an AI system. Livestreaming platforms challenge this assumption: interaction unfolds among streamers and audiences in real time, producing dynamic affective and social feedback loops. In this paper, we introduce the Triadic Loop, a conceptual framework that reconceptualizes alignment in AI co-hosted livestreaming as a temporally reinforced process of bidirectional adaptation among three actors: streamer $\leftrightarrow$ AI co-host, AI co-host $\leftrightarrow$ audience, and streamer $\leftrightarrow$ audience. Unlike instruction-following paradigms, bidirectional alignment requires each actor to continuously reshape the others, meaning misalignment in any sub-loop can destabilize the broader system. Drawing on literature from multi-party interaction, collaborative AI, and relational agents, we articulate how AI co-hosts function not only as mediators but as performative participants and community members shaping collective meaning-making. We further propose "strategic misalignment" as a mechanism for sustaining community engagement and introduce three relational evaluation constructs grounded in established instruments. The framework contributes a model of dynamic multi-party alignment, an account of cross-loop reinforcement, and design implications for AI co-hosts that sustain social coherence in participatory media environments.

</details>


### [93] [Choose Your Own Adventure: Non-Linear AI-Assisted Programming with EvoGraph](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18883v1)
*Vassilios Exarhakos,Jinghui Cheng,Jin L. C. Guo*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: EvoGraph通过交互式开发图解决AI编程中探索和管理的问题，降低认知负荷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI编程工具线性聊天式不符合编程迭代分支特性，导致开发者难以探索、管理和追踪。

Method: 创建EvoGraph IDE插件，自动记录分支AI编程历史，支持图形比较、合并和回退。

Result: 用户研究表明EvoGraph解决初步研究中的挑战，认知负荷低，支持安全探索和高效迭代。

Conclusion: 工作强调设计机会，帮助开发者理解AI编程中的问题解决进展。

中文摘要：当前的AI辅助编程工具主要是线性和基于聊天的，这与编程本身的迭代和分支性质相悖。我们对使用AI助手的开发者进行的初步研究表明，他们经常在探索替代方案、管理提示序列和追踪变更方面遇到困难。基于这些洞察，我们创建了EvoGraph，一个集成了AI交互和代码变更的轻量级交互式开发图的IDE插件。EvoGraph自动记录分支式的AI辅助编程历史，并允许开发者操作图形以比较、合并和重新访问先前的协作AI编程状态。我们与20名参与者的用户研究表明，EvoGraph解决了我们在初步研究中识别的开发者挑战，同时施加了较低的认知负荷。参与者还发现基于图形的表示支持安全探索、高效迭代和对AI生成变更的反思。我们的工作突出了工具设计的机会，以帮助开发者在新兴的AI中介编程背景下理解并应对他们的问题解决进展。

Original abstract: Current AI-assisted programming tools are predominantly linear and chat-based, which deviates from the iterative and branching nature of programming itself. Our preliminary study with developers using AI assistants suggested that they often struggle to explore alternatives, manage prompting sequences, and trace changes. Informed by these insights, we created EvoGraph, an IDE plugin that integrates AI interactions and code changes as a lightweight and interactive development graph. EvoGraph automatically records a branching AI-assisted coding history and allows developers to manipulate the graph to compare, merge, and revisit prior collaborative AI programming states. Our user study with 20 participants revealed that EvoGraph addressed developers' challenges identified in our preliminary study while imposing lower cognitive load. Participants also found the graph-based representation supported safe exploration, efficient iteration, and reflection on AI-generated changes. Our work highlights design opportunities for tools to help developers make sense of and act on their problem-solving progress in the emerging AI-mediated programming context.

</details>
