### [94] [First, Do No Harm (With LLMs): Mitigating Racial Bias via Agentic Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18038v1)
*Sihao Xing,Zaur Gouliev*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: 使用agentic workflow减轻偏见，方法可迁移到其他agent系统。

TL;DR: 本研究以欧盟AI法案为治理视角，评估五个LLMs在患者案例生成和鉴别诊断任务中的种族偏见，发现所有模型均存在偏差，但GPT-4.1偏差最小，DeepSeek V3在诊断任务中表现最佳，且代理工作流可减少部分显性偏见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在临床中的应用引发种族偏见担忧，现有研究多关注单一模型且缺乏缓解措施，需要以治理视角系统评估和缓解偏见。

Method: 以美国种族分层流行病学分布和专家诊断列表为基准，使用结构化提示模板和两部分评估设计，测试五个LLMs在合成患者案例生成和鉴别诊断排序任务中的隐性和显性种族偏见。

Result: 所有模型在案例生成中偏离真实分布，GPT-4.1偏差最小；鉴别诊断中DeepSeek V3表现最佳；代理工作流使DeepSeek V3的p值等指标提升，但非均匀改善。

Conclusion: 医疗AI系统需多指标偏见评估，基于检索的代理工作流可能减少诊断任务中的显性偏见。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在临床中的应用日益增多，引发了对其生成的医学文本和临床推理中种族偏见的担忧。现有研究已识别出医学LLMs中的偏见，但许多研究侧重于单一模型，对缓解偏见的关注较少。本研究以欧盟AI法案作为治理视角，评估了五个广泛使用的LLMs在两个任务上的表现，即合成患者案例生成和鉴别诊断排序。以美国按种族分层的流行病学分布和专家鉴别诊断列表为基准，我们应用结构化提示模板和两部分的评估设计来研究隐性和显性的种族偏见。所有模型在合成案例生成任务中都偏离了观察到的种族分布，其中GPT-4.1的整体偏差最小。在鉴别诊断任务中，DeepSeek V3在报告的各项指标上总体表现最强。当嵌入代理工作流时，DeepSeek V3的平均p值提高了0.0348，中位p值提高了0.1166，平均差异比独立模型提高了0.0949，尽管并非所有指标都一致改善。这些发现支持在医疗环境中使用的AI系统进行多指标偏见评估，并表明基于检索的代理工作流可能减少基准诊断任务中某些形式的显性偏见。详细的提示模板、实验数据集和代码管道可在我们的GitHub上获取。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in clinical settings, raising concerns about racial bias in both generated medical text and clinical reasoning. Existing studies have identified bias in medical LLMs, but many focus on single models and give less attention to mitigation. This study uses the EU AI Act as a governance lens to evaluate five widely used LLMs across two tasks, namely synthetic patient-case generation and differential diagnosis ranking. Using race-stratified epidemiological distributions in the United States and expert differential diagnosis lists as benchmarks, we apply structured prompt templates and a two-part evaluation design to examine implicit and explicit racial bias. All models deviated from observed racial distributions in the synthetic case generation task, with GPT-4.1 showing the smallest overall deviation. In the differential diagnosis task, DeepSeek V3 produced the strongest overall results across the reported metrics. When embedded in an agentic workflow, DeepSeek V3 showed an improvement of 0.0348 in mean p-value, 0.1166 in median p-value, and 0.0949 in mean difference relative to the standalone model, although improvement was not uniform across every metric. These findings support multi-metric bias evaluation for AI systems used in medical settings and suggest that retrieval-based agentic workflows may reduce some forms of explicit bias in benchmarked diagnostic tasks. Detailed prompt templates, experimental datasets, and code pipelines are available on our GitHub.

</details>

### [95] [AI-Native Network Controller: A Modular Framework for Safe Agentic Control of Multi-Domain Network Infrastructure](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20565v1)
*Merim Dzaferagic*

Main category: cs.NI

Selection reason: AI原生网络控制器的模块化框架，对agent安全与模块化设计有启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个AI原生网络控制器（AI-NNC），这是一个开源模块化框架，通过协议无关架构和轻量级适配器实现跨多域网络的智能AI控制，支持数据集收集、AI实验和协调测试台操作，从而实现更安全的自治网络管理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网络控制器多为域特定或缺乏对AI驱动自动化的原生支持，导致多域网络的安全协调智能控制仍是开放挑战。

Method: 设计了一个开源模块化框架AI-NNC，采用协议无关架构，通过轻量级Python适配器集成物理设备，控制逻辑由域特定应用程序实现，支持闭环控制、数据集收集、AI实验和协调测试台操作。

Result: AI-NNC能够跨不同网络域实现智能AI控制，且AI代理通过验证的应用程序操作，而非直接命令设备，从而实现更安全的自治网络管理。

Conclusion: AI-NNC提供了一种更安全的多域网络自治管理范式，通过验证的应用程序使AI代理安全地控制网络，这是迈向6G统一智能控制的关键一步。

中文摘要：多个网络域（包括无线接入、光传输和核心网络）在统一智能控制下的融合是未来6G系统的基本要求。这一点很重要，因为现有的网络控制器在很大程度上仍然局限于特定领域（例如用于无线电的O-RAN RIC），或者缺乏对跨异构基础设施的AI驱动自动化的原生支持。因此，多域网络的安全协调智能控制仍然是一个开放的挑战。在本文中，我们提出了AI原生网络控制器（AI-NNC），这是一个开源模块化框架，能够跨不同网络域实现智能AI控制。该框架围绕协议无关架构设计，其中每个物理设备通过轻量级Python适配器集成，而控制逻辑通过特定领域的控制应用程序实现。除了闭环控制，该框架还支持数据集收集、智能AI实验以及使用相同经过验证的控制和测量接口进行协调测试台操作。这种设计实现了一种更安全的自治网络管理范式，其中AI代理通过经过验证的应用程序运行，而不是直接向网络设备发出命令。

Original abstract: The convergence of multiple network domains, including radio access, optical transport, and core networks, under unified intelligent control is a fundamental requirement for future 6G systems. This is important because existing network controllers remain largely domain-specific, such as the O-RAN RIC for radio, or they lack native support for AI-driven automation across heterogeneous infrastructure. As a result, safe and coordinated agentic control of multi-domain networks is still an open challenge. In this paper, we present the AI-Native Network Controller (AI-NNC), an open-source and modular framework that enables agentic AI control across diverse network domains. The framework is designed around a protocol-agnostic architecture in which each physical device is integrated through a lightweight Python adapter, while control logic is implemented through domain-specific control applications. Beyond closed-loop control, the framework also supports dataset collection, agentic AI experimentation, and coordinated testbed operation using the same validated control and measurement interfaces. This design enables a safer paradigm for autonomous network management, where AI agents operate through validated applications rather than issuing commands directly to network equipment.

</details>

### [96] [Bayesian Active Learning with Gaussian Processes Guided by LLM Relevance Scoring for Dense Passage Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17906v1)
*Junyoung Kim,Anton Korikov,Jiazhou Liang,Justin Cui,Yifan Simon Liu,Qianfeng Wen,Mark Zhao,Scott Sanner*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 贝叶斯主动学习结合LLM评分用于检索，可启发agent高效利用LLM进行相关性判断。

TL;DR: 提出BAGEL框架，利用高斯过程和贝叶斯主动学习在预算约束下高效探索段落相关性分布，优于LLM重排序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM重排序计算成本高，且依赖稠密检索器导致无法检索语义簇和传播相关性信号。

Method: 使用高斯过程建模嵌入空间的相关性分布，通过平衡探索与利用迭代选择段落进行LLM评分。

Result: 在四个数据集上，BAGEL在相同LLM预算下均优于LLM重排序方法。

Conclusion: BAGEL能有效探索复杂相关性分布，提高检索效率。

中文摘要：尽管大型语言模型（LLM）展现出卓越的零样本相关性建模能力，但其高计算成本使得段落检索必须被构建为预算受限的全局优化问题。现有方法被动地依赖第一阶段稠密检索器，这导致了两个局限：（1）无法检索语义上不同的簇中的相关段落，（2）无法将相关性信号传播到更广泛的语料库。为了解决这些局限，我们提出了一种基于高斯过程的贝叶斯主动学习框架，由LLM相关性评分引导（BAGEL），该框架将稀疏的LLM相关性信号传播到整个嵌入空间以指导全局探索。BAGEL利用基于LLM相关性评分的查询特定高斯过程（GP），对整个嵌入空间中的多模态相关性分布进行建模。随后，它通过策略性地平衡高置信度区域的利用与不确定区域的探索，迭代选择待评分的段落。在四个基准数据集和两个LLM骨干网络上的大量实验表明，BAGEL有效地探索并捕获了复杂的相关性分布，并且在相同的LLM预算下，在所有四个数据集上均优于LLM重排序方法。

Original abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) exhibit exceptional zero-shot relevance modeling, their high computational cost necessitates framing passage retrieval as a budget-constrained global optimization problem. Existing approaches passively rely on first-stage dense retrievers, which leads to two limitations: (1) failing to retrieve relevant passages in semantically distinct clusters, and (2) failing to propagate relevance signals to the broader corpus. To address these limitations, we propose Bayesian Active Learning with Gaussian Processes guided by LLM relevance scoring (BAGEL), a novel framework that propagates sparse LLM relevance signals across the embedding space to guide global exploration. BAGEL models the multimodal relevance distribution across the entire embedding space with a query-specific Gaussian Process (GP) based on LLM relevance scores. Subsequently, it iteratively selects passages for scoring by strategically balancing the exploitation of high-confidence regions with the exploration of uncertain areas. Extensive experiments across four benchmark datasets and two LLM backbones demonstrate that BAGEL effectively explores and captures complex relevance distributions and outperforms LLM reranking methods under the same LLM budget on all four datasets.

</details>


### [97] [Evaluating Multi-Hop Reasoning in RAG Systems: A Comparison of LLM-Based Retriever Evaluation Strategies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18234v1)
*Lorenz Brehme,Thomas Ströhle,Ruth Breu*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 提出上下文感知检索评估方法CARE，可用于agent评估。

TL;DR: 提出上下文感知检索器评估（CARE）用于多跳查询RAG系统评估，实验表明其优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG评估集中于单上下文检索，缺乏对多跳查询中上下文组合重要性的考虑。

Method: 使用HotPotQA、MuSiQue、SQuAD数据集模拟RAG系统，比较三种LLM-as-judge评估策略（包括CARE）。

Result: CARE在评估多跳推理方面一致优于现有方法，尤其在更大模型和更长上下文窗口中效果更显著；单跳查询对上下文感知评估不敏感。

Conclusion: 上下文感知评估对提高RAG系统在复杂查询下的可靠性和准确性至关重要。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）通过外部知识增强大型语言模型（LLM），以更准确地回答问题。然而，关于评估RAG系统——特别是检索器组件——的研究仍然有限，因为现有大多数工作集中于单上下文检索而非多跳查询，在这些查询中，单个上下文可能看似无关，但组合起来却至关重要。在本研究中，我们使用HotPotQA、MuSiQue和SQuAD数据集模拟RAG系统，并比较了三种LLM作为评判的评估策略，包括我们提出的上下文感知检索器评估（CARE）。我们的目标是更好地理解如何在RAG系统中最有效地评估多跳推理。使用来自OpenAI、Meta和Google的LLM进行的实验表明，CARE在评估RAG系统中的多跳推理方面始终优于现有方法。性能提升在参数量更大和上下文窗口更长的模型中最为显著，而单跳查询对上下文感知评估的敏感性很小。总体而言，结果突显了上下文感知评估在提高检索增强生成系统的可靠性和准确性方面的关键作用，特别是在复杂查询场景中。为了确保可重复性，我们在https://github.com/lorenzbrehme/CARE提供了我们实验的完整数据。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) enhances large language models (LLMs) with external knowledge to answer questions more accurately.
  However, research on evaluating RAG systems-particularly the retriever component-remains limited, as most existing work focuses on single-context retrieval rather than multi-hop queries, where individual contexts may appear irrelevant in isolation but are essential when combined. In this research, we use the HotPotQA, MuSiQue, and SQuAD datasets to simulate a RAG system and compare three LLM-as-judge evaluation strategies, including our proposed Context-Aware Retriever Evaluation (CARE). Our goal is to better understand how multi-hop reasoning can be most effectively evaluated in RAG systems.
  Experiments with LLMs from OpenAI, Meta, and Google demonstrate that CARE consistently outperforms existing methods for evaluating multi-hop reasoning in RAG systems. The performance gains are most pronounced in models with larger parameter counts and longer context windows, while single-hop queries show minimal sensitivity to context-aware evaluation. Overall, the results highlight the critical role of context-aware evaluation in improving the reliability and accuracy of retrieval-augmented generation systems, particularly in complex query scenarios. To ensure reproducibility, we provide the complete data of our experiments at https://github.com/lorenzbrehme/CARE.

### [98] [COSAC: Counterfactual Credit Assignment in Sequential Cooperative Teams](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17693v2)
*Shripad Deshmukh,Jayakumar Subramanian,Raghavendra Addanki,Nikos Vlassis*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出多agent信用分配方法COSAC，可迁移至多coding agent协作场景。

TL;DR: COSAC是一种针对顺序合作团队的无评论家每个智能体策略梯度方法，通过岭回归和虚拟延续实现高效信用分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有顺序合作团队中的信用分配方法存在扩展性差、方差高或需要额外环境调用等问题，亟需一种无评论家且能解耦智能体信号的方法。

Method: COSAC利用岭回归分解团队奖励为每个智能体的加性贡献，通过当前策略的虚拟前向传播计算反事实优势，避免了重要性采样和环境重放，扩展了贵族效用到顺序团队。

Result: 在顺序赌博机任务中，COSAC在团队规模达16时取得最低优势MSE和低遗憾；在ARC任务中，收敛速度快于基线方法。

Conclusion: COSAC为顺序合作团队提供了高效、可扩展的信用分配方案。

中文摘要：在智能体以固定顺序行动并共享单一团队奖励的合作团队（多智能体语言系统、顺序机器人任务）中，每个智能体的信用分配是欠定的。基于评论家的方法随着智能体数量增加而扩展性差，因为需要维护联合/分解评论家成本高昂，而现有的无评论家替代方案存在其他问题：跨智能体的共同信用使得每个智能体的信号与队友噪声耦合；用于上游更新过时的重要性采样修正会导致方差随团队规模呈指数增长；或者每个智能体的反事实重放虽然隔离了每个智能体的影响，但以额外的环境或奖励调用为代价。我们提出了COSAC，一种针对顺序合作团队的无评论家每个智能体策略梯度。COSAC通过对批次轨迹进行单次岭回归来拟合团队奖励的加性每个智能体分解（为每个智能体提供与队友噪声解耦的学习信号），并通过当前策略的虚拟延续（策略前向传播）计算每个智能体的反事实优势，这替代了重要性采样重新加权和每个智能体的环境重放，且没有额外的环境或奖励成本。该估计器实现了顺序贵族效用（SeqAU），这是我们扩展Wolpert和Tumer（2001）的贵族效用到顺序团队的结果。我们证明了SeqAU信用的偏差和方差界限随团队规模增长而保持可控。我们在顺序赌博机上的受控研究表明，COSAC在团队规模高达K=16时获得了最低的优势MSE和持续低的学习遗憾。在AI2推理挑战（ARC）任务中，四个Qwen3-0.6B智能体轮流推理一个初中科学问题，COSAC比其它无评论家基线获得了更快的收敛速度。

Original abstract: In cooperative teams where agents act in a fixed order and share a single team-level reward (multi-agent language systems, sequential robotic tasks), per-agent credit assignment is under-determined. Critic-based approaches scale poorly as the number of agents grows owing to the costly maintenance of joint/factored critic(s), whereas the existing critic-free alternatives have other issues: common credit across agents that couples every agent's signal to teammate noise, importance-sampling corrections for upstream-update staleness that incur variance exponential in team size, or per-agent counterfactual replay that isolates each agent's effect at the price of extra environment or reward calls.
  We propose COSAC, a critic-free per-agent policy gradient for sequential cooperative teams. COSAC fits an additive per-agent decomposition of the team reward by a single ridge regression on the rollout batch (giving each agent a learning signal decoupled from teammate noise), and computes each agent's counterfactual advantage from fictitious continuations of the current policy (policy forward passes that replace both importance-sampling reweighting and per-agent environment replay, at no extra environment or reward cost). The estimator instantiates the Sequential Aristocrat Utility (SeqAU), our extension of Wolpert and Tumer's (2001) aristocrat utility to sequential teams. We prove bias and variance bounds on SeqAU credits that stay controlled as the team grows. Our controlled study on sequential bandits demonstrates that COSAC attains the lowest advantage MSE and consistently low learning regret across team sizes up to $K = 16$. On the AI2 Reasoning Challenge (ARC) task, where four Qwen3-0.6B agents reason in turn about a grade-school science question, COSAC attains faster convergence than the other critic-free baselines.

</details>


### [99] [LEPO: Latent Reasoning Policy Optimization for Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17892v4)
*Yuyan Zhou,Jiarui Yu,Hande Dong,Zhezheng Hao,Hong Wang,Jianqing Zhang,Qiang Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 将强化学习应用于隐空间推理，虽非严格agent，但RL训练机制对agent自我改进有启发。

TL;DR: 提出LEPO框架，通过Gumbel-Softmax向潜在推理注入随机性，并直接对连续潜在表示应用强化学习，显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有潜在推理方法缺乏随机采样，导致确定性推理，无法探索多样化的推理路径，且与强化学习不兼容。

Method: LEPO框架在展开阶段利用Gumbel-Softmax保持随机性进行多样轨迹采样，在优化阶段对潜在表示和离散标记构建统一梯度估计。

Result: 实验表明LEPO显著优于现有的离散和潜在推理的强化学习方法。

Conclusion: LEPO通过注入可控随机性并直接对连续潜在表示应用强化学习，有效提升了LLMs的推理探索能力和性能。

中文摘要：最近，潜在推理被引入大型语言模型（LLMs）中，以利用连续空间内的丰富信息。然而，如果没有随机采样，这些方法不可避免地退化为确定性推理，无法发现多样化的推理路径。为弥补这一差距，我们通过Gumbel-Softmax将可控的随机性注入到潜在推理中，恢复LLMs的探索能力，并增强其与强化学习（RL）的兼容性。在此基础上，我们提出了潜在推理策略优化（LEPO），一种将RL直接应用于连续潜在表示的新框架。具体来说，在展开阶段，LEPO保持随机性以实现多样化的轨迹采样，而在优化阶段，LEPO为潜在表示和离散标记构建统一的梯度估计。大量实验表明，LEPO显著优于现有的离散和潜在推理的RL方法。

Original abstract: Recently, latent reasoning has been introduced into large language models (LLMs) to leverage rich information within a continuous space. However, without stochastic sampling, these methods inevitably collapse to deterministic inference, failing to discover diverse reasoning paths. To bridge the gap, we inject controllable stochasticity into latent reasoning via Gumbel-Softmax, restoring LLMs' exploratory capacity and enhancing their compatibility with Reinforcement Learning (RL). Building on this, we propose \textbf{\underline{L}}atent R\textbf{\underline{e}}asoning \textbf{\underline{P}}olicy \textbf{\underline{O}}ptimization~(\textbf{LEPO}), a novel framework that applies RL directly to continuous latent representations. Specifically, in rollout stage, LEPO maintains stochasticity to enable diverse trajectory sampling, while in optimization stage, LEPO constructs a unified gradient estimation for both latent representations and discrete tokens. Extensive experiments show that LEPO significantly outperforms existing RL methods for discrete and latent reasoning.

</details>


### [100] [Can Explicit Physical Feasibility Benefit VLA Learning? An Empirical Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17896v2)
*Yubai Wei,Chen Wu,Hashem Haghbayan*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 显式物理可行性监督提升VLA策略，对agent执行中约束建模有参考意义。

TL;DR: 通过引入显式几何可行性监督，提升了VLA模型的物理可靠性和任务性能，尤其在低数据场景下效果显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA训练未显式监督物理约束（如避障），导致模型仅从示范隐式推断几何结构，可能产生不可行动作。

Method: 构建基于几何的可行性目标，集成到扩散VLA策略的训练中，并以避障任务作为受控测试环境。

Result: 显式可行性监督提高了物理可靠性和任务性能，同时增强了低数据场景下的学习效率。

Conclusion: 显式可行性信号可有效补充模仿学习，为开发更可靠的VLA策略提供新方向。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型将多模态输入直接映射到机器人动作，通常通过大规模模仿学习进行训练。虽然这种范式已展现出强大性能，但当前的VLA训练流程并未明确监督诸如避障或运动学可行性等硬性物理约束。因此，物理可行行为背后的几何结构只能从示范中隐式推断。本文研究引入显式可行性监督是否能对VLA策略提供有效的结构化指导。我们构建了一个简单的基于几何的可行性目标，并将其集成到基于扩散的VLA策略的训练阶段。为系统评估这一想法，我们使用避障操作作为几何依赖物理可行性的受控探针。实证结果表明，将可行性监督增强到VLA训练中可提高物理可靠性和整体任务性能，同时在低数据场景下提升学习效率。这些发现表明，显式可行性信号能有效补充基于模仿的VLA学习，凸显了其开发更可靠VLA策略的潜力。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models map multimodal inputs directly to robot actions and are typically trained through large-scale imitation learning. While this paradigm has shown strong performance, prevailing VLA training procedures do not explicitly supervise hard physical constraints such as obstacle avoidance or kinematic feasibility. As a result, the geometric structure underlying physically feasible behavior must be inferred only implicitly from demonstrations. In this paper, we study whether introducing explicit feasibility supervision can provide effective structured guidance for VLA policies. We formulate a simple geometry-grounded feasibility objective and integrate it into the training stage of a diffusion-based VLA policy. To evaluate this idea systematically, we use obstacle-aware manipulation as a controlled probe of geometry-dependent physical feasibility. Empirical results show that augmenting VLA training with feasibility supervision improves both physical reliability and overall task performance, while also enhancing learning efficiency in the low-data regime. These findings indicate that explicit feasibility signals can effectively complement imitation-based VLA learning, highlighting their potential for developing more reliable VLA policies.

</details>


### [101] [Learning to Correct: Calibrated Reinforcement Learning for Multi-Attempt Chain-of-Thought](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17912v1)
*Muhammed Emrullah Ildiz,Halil Alperen Gozeten,Ege Onur Taga,Samet Oymak*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出多尝试CoT的校准RL方法，属于通用LLM agent自我改进与验证。

TL;DR: 提出校准的尝试级别GRPO（CAL-GRPO），通过无偏加权策略优化多尝试推理中的Verification@K奖励，理论证明并实验验证其优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长CoT多尝试设置中，基于通过/失败的天真加权导致有偏梯度，需要一种能获得无偏梯度且方差小的强化学习方法。

Method: 引入CAL-GRPO，设计尝试级别的加权策略，对每个尝试的奖励进行校准，使得梯度无偏并保持较小方差。

Result: 在合成和真实数据上的实验表明，CAL-GRPO在Verification@K性能上优于普通GRPO和天真加权方法，消融研究支持理论分析。

Conclusion: CAL-GRPO能够有效利用多次尝试的奖励信号，实现无偏梯度优化，提升模型在长CoT推理中的最终成功率。

中文摘要：最先进的推理模型利用长链思维（CoT）通过更多的测试时计算来解决日益复杂的问题。在这项工作中，我们探索了一种长CoT设置，其中模型在收到硬验证器反馈后，可以依次进行多达K次尝试来解决问题，每次尝试都可以基于之前的尝试。这激发了强化学习方法，通过仔细加权各个尝试来利用每次尝试的奖励。我们研究了优化Verification@K奖励（模型在第K次尝试时成功），并表明天真地根据尝试的通过/失败结果进行加权会产生有偏梯度。我们引入了校准的尝试级别（Calibrated Attempt-Level, CAL）GRPO，通过设计一种加权策略来获得无偏梯度，同时保持较小的方差。我们的理论揭示了合并每次尝试奖励如何影响训练和最终的Verification@K性能。在合成和真实数据上的实验、基线和消融研究证实了我们的理论以及CAL-GRPO相对于普通GRPO和天真加权的优势。

Original abstract: State-of-the-art reasoning models utilize long chain-of-thought (CoT) to solve increasingly complex problems using more test-time computation. In this work, we explore a long CoT setting where the model makes up to K successive attempts at solving a problem, in which each attempt is allowed to build on earlier ones after the model receives a hard verifier feedback. This motivates RL methods that can harness per-attempt rewards by carefully weighting individual attempts. We study optimizing the Verification@K reward (the model succeeds by the K-th attempt) and show that naively weighing the attempts by their pass/fail results in biased gradients. We introduce Calibrated Attempt-Level (CAL) GRPO by devising a weighing strategy to obtain unbiased gradients while maintaining small variance. Our theory reveals how incorporating per-attempt rewards influence the training and the eventual Verification@K performance. Experiments, baselines, and ablations on synthetic and real data corroborate our theory and the benefits of CAL-GRPO over vanilla GRPO as well as naive weighting.

</details>


### [102] [RASP-Tuner: Retrieval-Augmented Soft Prompts for Context-Aware Black-Box Optimization in Non-Stationary Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18026v1)
*Enze Pan*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出上下文感知黑箱优化方法，检索增强和低维适应对agent上下文处理有参考。

TL;DR: RASP-Tuner通过上下文条件化遗憾最小化，利用基于检索的机制识别、混合专家代理和低维提示子空间适应，实现了高效的在线调优，在合成和真实任务上优于或匹配基线方法，且计算开销更低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线调优方法在面对重复出现的上下文机制时，因丢弃历史而付出重复适应成本，且全高斯过程更新在高观测次数下计算昂贵，难以满足低成本每步需求。

Method: RASP-Tuner： (i) 检索相似历史上下文识别机制代理； (ii) 用混合专家代理预测短期损失，输入为参数、上下文和检索的软提示； (iii) 主要在低维提示子空间适应，仅当误差或分歧激增时更新全代理； RealErrorComposer将异质指标映射到[0,1]作为可微训练目标。

Result: 在9个合成非平稳基准、1个对抗上下文检查和3个真实世界数据流上，RASP-Tuner在7/9合成任务上提升或匹配累积遗憾（T=100），每步壁钟时间比滑动窗口GP-UCB低8-12倍。

Conclusion: 理想化分析给出有界动态遗憾的充分条件，但实际系统违反部分假设，需进一步研究开放缺口。

中文摘要：许多部署的系统暴露了黑箱目标，其最小化配置随外部观察到的上下文而变化。当上下文重复访问一小组潜在机制时，丢弃历史记录的优化器会付出重复的适应成本；当每一步必须保持低成本时，在高观测次数下完全重新拟合高斯过程（GP）难以持续。我们将在线调优视为上下文条件化的遗憾最小化，并提出RASP-Tuner，它实例化了一个基于第一性原理的分解：（i）通过检索相似的历史上下文来识别机制代理；（ii）使用混合专家代理预测短期损失，其输入连接了参数、上下文和检索到的软提示；（iii）主要在低维提示子空间中进行适应，仅在标量化误差或分歧激增时调用完整的代理更新。RealErrorComposer通过EMA稳定的逻辑评分将异质流式指标映射到[0,1]，提供一个可微分的训练目标。在九个合成非平稳基准、一个对抗上下文完整性检查以及三个表格化真实世界流（见真实世界实验部分）上，RASP-Tuner在T=100的水平下与我们的GP-UCB和CMA-ES实现相比，在九个合成任务中的七个上提升或匹配了累积遗憾，同时在相同硬件上记录到每步壁钟时间比滑动窗口GP-UCB低8-12倍。在聚类分离、强凸机制模型（RA-GD）中的理想化分析提供了有界动态遗憾的充分条件；实际部署的流水线违反了其中几个前提，我们阐明了哪些缺口仍然开放。

Original abstract: Many deployed systems expose black-box objectives whose minimizing configuration shifts with an externally observed context. When contexts revisit a small set of latent regimes, an optimizer that discards history pays repeated adaptation cost; when each step must remain inexpensive, full Gaussian-process (GP) refits at high observation counts are difficult to sustain. We cast online tuning as context-conditioned regret minimization and present RASP-Tuner, which instantiates a decomposition motivated by first principles: (i) identify a regime proxy by retrieving similar past contexts; (ii) predict short-horizon loss with a mixture-of-experts surrogate whose input concatenates parameters, context, and a retrieved soft prompt; (iii) adapt chiefly in a low-dimensional prompt subspace, invoking full surrogate updates only when scalarized error or disagreement spikes. A RealErrorComposer maps heterogeneous streaming metrics to [0,1] via EMA-stabilized logistic scores, supplying a single differentiable training target. On nine synthetic non-stationary benchmarks, an adversarial-context sanity check, and three tabular real-world streams (Section on real-world experiments), RASP-Tuner improves or matches cumulative regret relative to our GP-UCB and CMA-ES implementations on seven of nine synthetic tasks under paired tests at horizon T=100, while recording 8-12 times lower wall-clock per step than sliding-window GP-UCB on identical hardware. Idealized analysis in a cluster-separated, strongly convex regime model (RA-GD) supplies sufficient conditions for bounded dynamic regret; the deployed pipeline violates several of these premises, and we articulate which gaps remain open.

</details>


### [103] [Scalable Neighborhood-Based Multi-Agent Actor-Critic](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18190v1)
*Tim Goppelsroeder,Rasmus Jensen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多agent可扩展actor-critic，协作方法可迁移

TL;DR: MADDPG-K通过限制评论家到最近的k个智能体，降低了计算成本，并在多智能体环境中实现了可扩展性和良好性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决MADDPG中集中式评论家输入随智能体数量线性增长导致训练成本高的问题。

Method: 每个智能体的评论家只考虑距离最近的k个智能体，使用欧几里得距离度量，保持输入大小恒定。

Result: 在合作和对抗环境中，MADDPG-K性能与MADDPG相当或更优，合作环境下收敛更快，运行时间扩展性更好。

Conclusion: MADDPG-K是一种可扩展的多智能体强化学习方法，有效解决了集中式评论家的计算瓶颈。

中文摘要：我们提出了MADDPG-K，这是对多智能体深度确定性策略梯度（MADDPG）的可扩展扩展，解决了集中式评论家方法的计算限制。集中式评论家以所有智能体的观测和动作为条件，在合作和竞争的多智能体环境中已显示出显著的性能提升。然而，它们的评论家网络输入大小随智能体数量线性增长，使得在大规模训练时成本越来越高。MADDPG-K通过将每个智能体的评论家限制在所选度量（在我们的案例中是欧几里得距离）下最近的k个智能体来缓解这一问题。这确保了无论智能体总数如何，评论家输入大小都是恒定的。我们分析了这种方法的复杂性，表明其保留的二次成本来自于廉价的距离标量计算，而不是阻碍标准MADDPG的昂贵神经网络矩阵乘法。我们通过多粒子环境套件中的合作和对抗环境对方法进行了实证验证，展示了与MADDPG相比具有竞争性或更优越的性能、在合作环境中更快的收敛性，以及随着智能体数量增长更好的运行时间扩展性。我们的代码可在https://github.com/TimGop/MADDPG-K获取。

Original abstract: We propose MADDPG-K, a scalable extension to Multi-Agent Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (MADDPG) that addresses the computational limitations of centralized critic approaches. Centralized critics, which condition on the observations and actions of all agents, have demonstrated significant performance gains in cooperative and competitive multi-agent settings. However, their critic networks grow linearly in input size with the number of agents, making them increasingly expensive to train at scale. MADDPG-K mitigates this by restricting each agent's critic to the $k$ closest agents under a chosen metric which in our case is Euclidean distance. This ensures a constant-size critic input regardless of the total agent count. We analyze the complexity of this approach, showing that the quadratic cost it retains arises from cheap scalar distance computations rather than the expensive neural network matrix multiplications that bottleneck standard MADDPG. We validate our method empirically across cooperative and adversarial environments from the Multi-Particle Environment suite, demonstrating competitive or superior performance compared to MADDPG, faster convergence in cooperative settings, and better runtime scaling as the number of agents grows. Our code is available at https://github.com/TimGop/MADDPG-K .

</details>


### [104] [Towards Disentangled Preference Optimization Dynamics: Suppress the Loser, Preserve the Winner](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18239v3)
*Wei Chen,Yubing Wu,Junmei Yang,Delu Zeng,Qibin Zhao,John Paisley,Min Chen,Zhou Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 偏好优化动力学分析及奖励校准方法，对agent对齐有通用启发。

TL;DR: 提出统一激励分数分解和“解缠带”条件，基于此设计奖励校准方法，实现偏好优化中抑制拒绝响应而不损害选择响应，实验证明性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于边距的偏好优化方法在抑制拒绝响应时往往会同时抑制选择响应，且缺乏通用方法避免此问题，因此需要一种统一的框架来分析和解决这一困境。

Method: 通过统一激励分数分解揭示不同优化目标的共同结构，并基于选择/拒绝似然动态分析提出“解缠带”（DB）条件；然后设计奖励校准（RC）方法，自适应调整更新权重以满足DB条件。

Result: RC方法实现了更解缠的动态，在多个下游任务中取得更好的性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的统一分解和DB条件为偏好优化提供了理论洞察，RC方法是一种有效且即插即用的解决方案，实现了抑制失败者同时保留胜利者的目标。

中文摘要：偏好优化被广泛用于使大型语言模型（LLMs）与人类偏好对齐。然而，许多基于边距的方法在试图抑制被拒绝响应时，也会抑制被选择响应，而且目前没有通用的方法能在不同目标中防止这种情况。我们通过偏好优化的统一激励分数分解来解决这个问题，揭示了不同目标共享相同的局部更新方向，仅在标量权重上有所不同。这种分解为以前在单独设置中研究的目标提供了一个通用框架。基于此分解，通过分析选择/拒绝似然的动态，我们确定了“解缠带”（DB），这是一个简单且可测试的条件，它告诉我们训练何时可以遵循期望的路径：在可能的早期阶段之后，抑制失败者同时保护胜利者。利用DB，我们提出了奖励校准（RC），这是一种即插即用的方法，它自适应地重新平衡选择响应和被拒绝响应的更新以满足DB，而无需重新设计基础目标。实验结果表明，RC导致更解缠的动态，在多个设置中观察到更好的下游性能。我们的代码可在https://github.com/IceyWuu/DisentangledPreferenceOptimization获取。

Original abstract: Preference optimization is widely used to align large language models (LLMs) with human preferences. However, many margin-based methods also suppress the chosen response when they try to suppress the rejected one, and there is no general way to prevent this across different objectives.
  We address this issue with a unified incentive-score decomposition of preference optimization, revealing that different objectives share the same local update directions and differ only in their scalar weights.
  This decomposition provides a common framework for analyzing objectives that were previously studied in separate settings.
  Building on this decomposition, by analyzing the dynamics of the chosen/rejected likelihoods, we identify the disentanglement band (DB), a simple, testable condition that tells us when training can follow the desired path: suppress the loser while preserving the winner, possibly after an early stage.
  Using the DB, we propose reward calibration (RC), a plug-and-play method that adaptively rebalances the updates for chosen and rejected responses to satisfy the DB, without redesigning the base objective.
  Empirical results show that RC leads to more disentangled dynamics, with better downstream performance observed across several settings. Our code is available at https://github.com/IceyWuu/DisentangledPreferenceOptimization.

</details>


### [105] [Reducing Credit Assignment Variance via Counterfactual Reasoning Paths](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16302v2)
*Fei Ding,Yongkang Zhang,Youwei Wang,Zijian Zeng*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 反事实推理路径降低强化学习方差，直接涉及代码推理agent训练。

TL;DR: 提出反事实比较框架进行信用分配，并基于此提出隐式行为策略优化（IBPO），显著提升了LLM多步推理的训练稳定性和性能上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏终端奖励导致信用分配问题，造成高梯度方差、训练不稳定和无效更新，限制了模型持续改进。

Method: 提出反事实比较框架，通过采样多个推理轨迹并利用差异作为隐式过程级优势估计，将稀疏终端奖励转换为步骤敏感信号；并基于此提出隐式行为策略优化（IBPO）。

Result: 显著提高训练稳定性和在数学与代码推理基准上的性能上限。

Conclusion: 该工作指出了释放LLM推理潜力的有前景方向。

中文摘要：使用大型语言模型进行多步推理的强化学习通常依赖于稀疏的终端奖励，这会产生一个条件不佳的信用分配问题：最终反馈被均匀地传播到所有中间决策。这导致高梯度方差、不稳定的训练和许多无效的更新，最终限制了模型的持续改进。我们提出了一种用于信用分配的反事实比较框架。对于每个输入，该框架采样多个推理轨迹，并将它们的差异视为对替代决策的隐式近似。这产生了一个隐式的过程级优势估计器，将稀疏的终端奖励转换为步骤敏感的学习信号。基于这一框架，我们引入了隐式行为策略优化（IBPO），它显著提高了训练稳定性和在数学与代码推理基准上的性能上限。我们的结果指出了释放大型语言模型推理潜力的一个有前景的方向。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning for multi-step reasoning with large language models (LLMs) typically relies on sparse terminal rewards, which creates a poorly conditioned credit-assignment problem: the final feedback is propagated uniformly across all intermediate decisions. This leads to high gradient variance, unstable training, and many ineffective updates, ultimately limiting sustained model improvement. We propose a counterfactual-comparison framework for credit assignment. For each input, the framework samples multiple reasoning trajectories and treats their differences as implicit approximations to alternative decisions. This yields an implicit process-level advantage estimator that converts sparse terminal rewards into step-sensitive learning signals. Building on this framework, we introduce Implicit Behavior Policy Optimization (IBPO), which substantially improves training stability and the performance ceiling on mathematical and code-reasoning benchmarks. Our results point to a promising direction for unlocking the reasoning potential of LLMs.

</details>


### [106] [Latent Phase-Shift Rollback: Inference-Time Error Correction via Residual Stream Monitoring and KV-Cache Steering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18567v1)
*Manan Gupta,Dhruv Kumar*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 推理时错误检测和回滚方法，可潜在应用于coding agent自我纠正

TL;DR: LPSR 通过监控残差流的相位偏移并回滚 KV 缓存来纠正大模型的推理错误，在 MATH-500 上显著提升性能，无需微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在生成过程中一旦出现错误步骤，后续标记会加剧错误，而非纠正，而现有方法如自我纠正或 Best-of-N 效果有限或成本高。

Method: 在生成时监控关键层残差流的余弦相似度和熵以检测相位偏移，检测到错误时回滚 KV 缓存并注入预计算引导向量，无需微调或额外前向传播。

Result: 在 MATH-500 上，8B 模型 LPSR 达 44.0%，远超标准自回归（28.8%）、自我纠正（19.8%）和 Best-of-16（36.2%），且以更少参数超过 70B 模型（35.2%）。

Conclusion: LPSR 是一种高效无需训练的推理时错误纠正方法，且揭示了检测与纠正的最优深度不同（检测层 14，纠正层 16）。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在生成过程中频繁犯下不可恢复的推理错误：一旦走错一步，后续的标记会加剧错误而非纠正它。我们提出了\(\textbf{隐式相位偏移回滚}\)（LPSR）：在每个生成步骤中，我们在关键层 \(l_{\text{crit}}\) 监控残差流，通过余弦相似度加熵的双门检测突然的方向反转（相位偏移），并通过回滚 KV 缓存和注入预计算的引导向量进行响应。无需微调、梯度计算或额外的前向传播。LPSR 在 MATH-500 上使用 8B 模型达到 \(\mathbf{44.0\%}\)，而标准自回归为 \(28.8\%\)（+15.2 个百分点；McNemar \(\chi^2 = 66.96\)，\(p < 10^{-15}\)）。关键的是，提示自我纠正（最自然的推理时基线）仅得 \(19.8\%\)，低于标准自回归；LPSR 超过它 \(+24.2\) 个百分点（\(\chi^2 = 89.4\)，\(p \approx 0\)）。LPSR 还以 \(5.4\times\) 更低的令牌成本优于 Best-of-16（+7.8 个百分点），并以约 \(3\times\) 的令牌预算超过标准 70B 模型（\(35.2\%\)），参数少 \(8.75\times\)。一个 32 层的扫描揭示了一种新颖的 \(\textbf{检测-纠正分离}\)：错误检测 AUC 在层 14 达到峰值（\(0.718\)），但任务准确率在层 16 达到峰值（\(44.0\%\) 对比 \(29.2\%\)），表明检测和纠正的最优监控深度不同。

Original abstract: Large language models frequently commit unrecoverable reasoning errors mid-generation: once a wrong step is taken, subsequent tokens compound the mistake rather than correct it. We introduce $\textbf{Latent Phase-Shift Rollback}$ (LPSR): at each generation step, we monitor the residual stream at a critical layer lcrit, detect abrupt directional reversals (phase shifts) via a cosine-similarity $+$ entropy dual gate, and respond by rolling back the KV-cache and injecting a pre-computed steering vector. No fine-tuning, gradient computation, or additional forward passes are required. LPSR achieves $\mathbf{44.0\%}$ on MATH-500 with an 8B model versus $28.8\%$ for standard AR ($+15.2$ pp; McNemar $χ^2 = 66.96$, $p < 10^{-15}$). Critically, prompted self-correction, the most natural inference-time baseline, scores only $19.8\%$, below standard AR; LPSR exceeds it by $+24.2$ pp ($χ^2 = 89.4$, $p \approx 0$). LPSR also outperforms Best-of-16 ($+7.8$ pp) at $5.4\times$ lower token cost, and surpasses a standard 70B model ($35.2\%$) with $8.75\times$ fewer parameters at ${\sim}3\times$ the token budget. A 32-layer sweep reveals a novel \textbf{detection-correction dissociation}: error-detection AUC peaks at layer~14 ($0.718$) but task accuracy peaks at layer~16 ($44.0\%$ vs.\ $29.2\%$), demonstrating that optimal monitoring depth differs for detection and correction.

</details>


### [107] [When Can LLMs Learn to Reason with Weak Supervision?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18574v1)
*Salman Rahman,Jingyan Shen,Anna Mordvina,Hamid Palangi,Saadia Gabriel,Pavel Izmailov*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究弱监督下RLVR泛化条件，对训练coding agent有参考价值

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型在弱监督强化学习下的推理泛化机制，发现训练奖励饱和动力学和推理忠实性是关键因素，并表明结合持续预训练和监督微调可显著提升泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型能力增强，构建高质量奖励信号变得越来越困难，因此需要理解在弱监督（如稀缺数据、噪声奖励、自监督代理奖励）下强化学习何时能成功，以指导实际应用。

Method: 跨多个模型系列和推理领域，在三种弱监督设置（稀缺数据、噪声奖励、自监督代理奖励）下进行系统性实证研究，分析训练奖励饱和动力学，并分离持续预训练和监督微调的贡献。

Result: 泛化受训练奖励饱和动力学控制；推理忠实性是预测模型泛化能力的预强化学习属性；监督微调是泛化的必要条件，持续预训练放大其效果；结合两者可使基础模型在三种弱监督设置下均实现泛化。

Conclusion: 在弱监督强化学习中，推理忠实性是关键预测指标，而结合持续预训练和监督微调可以有效提升模型的泛化能力，为在奖励信号较弱的场景下应用强化学习提供了可行路径。

中文摘要：大型语言模型通过可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在推理方面取得了显著改进。然而，随着模型能力的增长，构建高质量奖励信号变得越来越困难，因此理解在弱监督形式下RLVR何时能够成功至关重要。我们跨多个模型系列和推理领域，在三种弱监督设置下进行了系统性实证研究：稀缺数据、噪声奖励和自监督代理奖励。我们发现泛化由训练奖励饱和动力学控制：能够泛化的模型表现出一个延长的预饱和阶段，在此期间训练奖励和下游性能共同上升，而快速饱和的模型则记忆而非学习。我们将推理忠实性定义为中间步骤在逻辑上支持最终答案的程度，并确定其为预测模型属于哪种状态的预强化学习属性，而输出多样性本身则无信息价值。受这些发现启发，我们分离了持续预训练和监督微调的贡献，发现在弱监督下，针对显式推理轨迹的监督微调是实现泛化的必要条件，而领域数据的持续预训练则放大了这一效果。将这两种干预措施应用于Llama3.2-3B-Base，使得模型在基础模型先前失败的所有三种设置下都能实现泛化。

Original abstract: Large language models have achieved significant reasoning improvements through reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). Yet as model capabilities grow, constructing high-quality reward signals becomes increasingly difficult, making it essential to understand when RLVR can succeed under weaker forms of supervision. We conduct a systematic empirical study across diverse model families and reasoning domains under three weak supervision settings: scarce data, noisy rewards, and self-supervised proxy rewards. We find that generalization is governed by training reward saturation dynamics: models that generalize exhibit a prolonged pre-saturation phase during which training reward and downstream performance climb together, while models that saturate rapidly memorize rather than learn. We identify reasoning faithfulness, defined as the extent to which intermediate steps logically support the final answer, as the pre-RL property that predicts which regime a model falls into, while output diversity alone is uninformative. Motivated by these findings, we disentangle the contributions of continual pre-training and supervised fine-tuning, finding that SFT on explicit reasoning traces is necessary for generalization under weak supervision, while continual pre-training on domain data amplifies the effect. Applied together to Llama3.2-3B-Base, these interventions enable generalization across all three settings where the base model previously failed.

</details>


### [108] [HELM: Harness-Enhanced Long-horizon Memory for Vision-Language-Action Manipulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18791v1)
*Zijian Zeng,Fei Ding,Huiming Yang,Xianwei Li*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 长时程记忆框架（记忆、验证、恢复），可迁移至coding agent的验证与回滚机制

TL;DR: VLA模型在长视域任务中因记忆、验证和恢复缺陷而失败，HELM框架通过情景记忆、状态验证器和操控控制器解决这些问题，在LIBERO-LONG上提升23.1%成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型在长视域操作任务中系统性失败，且仅扩展上下文窗口无法解决，必须解决执行循环中的记忆、验证和恢复缺陷。

Method: 提出HELM框架，包含三个组件：EMM（基于CLIP索引关键帧检索任务历史）、SV（学习的状态验证器，预测动作失败）、HC（回滚和重新规划）。SV依赖情景记忆。

Result: 在LIBERO-LONG上，HELM比OpenVLA提升23.1个百分点（58.4%→81.5%），远超扩展上下文（5.4点）和LoRA（12.2点）；在CALVIN上提升长视域性能；受控扰动下恢复成功率大幅提升。

Conclusion: HELM有效解决了VLA在长视域操作中的记忆、验证和恢复缺陷，为提高长视域任务成功率提供了模型无关的框架，并发布了LIBERO-Recovery评估协议。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在短视域任务中表现优异，但在长视域操作任务中系统性失败。我们证明，在当前的反应式执行设置中，仅通过扩展上下文长度无法解决这一失败；相反，它源于三个反复出现的执行循环缺陷：记忆鸿沟、验证鸿沟和恢复鸿沟。我们提出了HELM，一个模型无关的框架，通过三个组件解决这些缺陷：一个情景记忆模块（EMM），通过基于CLIP索引的关键帧检索关键任务历史；一个学习的状态验证器（SV），从观测、动作、子目标和记忆条件上下文中预测执行前的动作失败；以及一个操控控制器（HC），执行回滚和重新规划。SV是核心学习贡献：它持续优于基于规则的可行性检查和集成不确定性基线，其有效性关键取决于对情景记忆的访问。在LIBERO-LONG上，HELM相对于OpenVLA将任务成功率提高了23.1个百分点（从58.4%提升到81.5%），而将上下文窗口扩展到H=32仅带来5.4个百分点的提升，同等预算的LoRA适应仍比HELM低12.2个百分点。HELM还提高了CALVIN上的长视域性能，并在受控扰动下显著提升了恢复成功率。消融和机制分析分离了每个组件的贡献，我们发布了LIBERO-Recovery作为注入扰动协议，用于评估长视域操作中的失败恢复。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models fail systematically on long-horizon manipulation tasks despite strong short-horizon performance. We show that this failure is not resolved by extending context length alone in the current reactive execution setting; instead, it stems from three recurring execution-loop deficiencies: the memory gap, the verification gap, and the recovery gap. We present HELM, a model-agnostic framework that addresses these deficiencies with three components: an Episodic Memory Module (EMM) that retrieves key task history via CLIP-indexed keyframes, a learned State Verifier (SV) that predicts action failure before execution from observation, action, subgoal, and memory-conditioned context, and a Harness Controller (HC) that performs rollback and replanning. The SV is the core learning contribution: it consistently outperforms rule-based feasibility checks and ensemble uncertainty baselines, and its effectiveness depends critically on access to episodic memory. On LIBERO-LONG, HELM improves task success rate by 23.1 percentage points over OpenVLA (58.4% to 81.5%), while extending the context window to H=32 yields only a 5.4-point gain and same-budget LoRA adaptation remains 12.2 points below HELM. HELM also improves long-horizon performance on CALVIN and substantially boosts recovery success under controlled perturbations. Ablations and mechanism analyses isolate the contribution of each component, and we release LIBERO-Recovery as a perturbation-injection protocol for evaluating failure recovery in long-horizon manipulation.

</details>


### [109] [One Step Forward and K Steps Back: Better Reasoning with Denoising Recursion Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18839v1)
*Chris Cameron,Wangzheng Wang,Nikita Ivanov,Ashmita Bhattacharyya,Didier Chételat,Yingxue Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出多步去噪推理训练策略，可能启发agent的迭代规划与反思。

TL;DR: 提出去噪递归模型，通过多步递归去噪训练循环变换器，解决训练-测试不一致问题，在ARC-AGI上超越TRM。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 循环变换器在长细化轨迹上训练困难，监督缺失，而扩散模型的单步去噪导致训练与测试行为不一致。

Method: 使用噪声破坏数据，训练模型在多个递归步骤中逐步反转噪声，提供中间状态课程，对齐训练与测试。

Result: 在ARC-AGI基准上优于Tiny Recursion Model (TRM)。

Conclusion: 去噪递归模型通过多步递归去噪有效训练循环变换器，提升困难任务性能，激励非贪心生成。

中文摘要：循环变换器通过重复应用共享的变换器块来增加计算深度而不增加参数数量，并可用于迭代细化，其中每个循环并行地重写完整的固定大小预测。在需要类搜索计算的困难问题上，从噪声开始到达高度结构化解决方案可能需要长的细化轨迹。学习这样的轨迹具有挑战性，因为训练只指定目标解决方案，而不提供中间细化路径的监督。扩散模型通过用不同幅度的噪声破坏数据并训练模型在单步中反转它来解决这个问题。然而，这个过程使训练和测试行为不一致。我们引入了去噪递归模型，一种类似地用噪声破坏数据但训练模型在多个递归步骤中反转破坏的方法。该策略提供了中间状态的可处理课程，同时更好地对齐训练和测试，并激励非贪心的、前瞻性的生成。通过大量实验，我们展示了这种方法在ARC-AGI上优于Tiny Recursion Model (TRM)，后者最近取得了突破性性能。

Original abstract: Looped transformers scale computational depth without increasing parameter count by repeatedly applying a shared transformer block and can be used for iterative refinement, where each loop rewrites a full fixed-size prediction in parallel. On difficult problems, such as those that require search-like computation, reaching a highly structured solution starting from noise can require long refinement trajectories. Learning such trajectories is challenging when training specifies only the target solution and provides no supervision over the intermediate refinement path. Diffusion models tackle this issue by corrupting data with varying magnitudes of noise and training the model to reverse it in a \textit{single step}. However, this process misaligns training and testing behaviour. We introduce Denoising Recursion Models, a method that similarly corrupts data with noise but trains the model to reverse the corruption over \textit{multiple} recursive steps. This strategy provides a tractable curriculum of intermediate states, while better aligning training with testing and incentivizing non-greedy, forward-looking generation. Through extensive experiments, we show this approach outperforms the Tiny Recursion Model (TRM) on ARC-AGI, where it recently achieved breakthrough performance.

</details>


### [110] [Gradient-Based Program Synthesis with Neurally Interpreted Languages](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18907v1)
*Matthew V. Macfarlane,Clément Bonnet,Herke van Hoof,Levi H. S. Lelis*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出可微分神经执行器实现端到端程序合成，并支持测试时梯度下降优化，可迁移至自动代码优化 agent 的训练与推理。

TL;DR: NLI通过端到端学习离散、符号化的编程语言，结合可微执行器与Gumbel-Softmax松弛，在组合泛化和快速适应任务上超越了现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 符号方法提供组合泛化和数据效率但受限于DSL的可扩展性，神经网络灵活但泛化能力差，需要一种结合两者优点的方法。

Method: 提出神经语言解释器（NLI），自主学习离散原始操作词汇表，使用可微神经执行器解释变长程序序列，通过Gumbel-Softmax松弛实现端到端训练，并利用梯度下降进行测试时适应。

Result: 在需要组合泛化和快速适应的任务上，NLI优于上下文学习、测试时训练和连续潜在程序网络等基线方法。

Conclusion: NLI证明了将离散语言的组合性与神经网络的梯度搜索和端到端学习相结合是一条可行且有效的路径。

中文摘要：程序归纳中的一个核心挑战长期以来一直是符号方法与神经方法之间的权衡。符号方法提供了组合泛化和数据效率，但其可扩展性受到领域特定语言（DSL）等形式体系的限制，这些形式体系需要大量人工创建，且可能无法迁移到新领域。相比之下，神经网络灵活地从数据中学习，但在组合和分布外设置中往往泛化能力较差。我们通过一个潜在适应网络架构的实例——神经语言解释器（NLI）——弥合了这一鸿沟，该解释器以端到端的方式自主学习其自身的离散、符号化编程语言。NLI自主发现原始操作的词汇表，并使用一种新颖的可微神经执行器来解释这些原语的变长序列。这使得NLI能够表示不受限于恒定计算步数的程序，从而解决比训练时所见更复杂的问题。为了使这些离散的、组合的程序结构适用于基于梯度的优化，我们采用了Gumbel-Softmax松弛，使整个模型能够进行端到端训练。关键在于，这种可微性还实现了强大的测试时适应。在推理时，NLI的程序归纳器提供初始程序猜想，然后通过神经执行器的梯度下降进行优化，从而高效搜索最能解释给定数据的神经程序。我们证明，在需要组合泛化和快速适应未见任务的任务上，NLI优于上下文学习、测试时训练和连续潜在程序网络。我们的结果为结合离散语言的组合性与神经网络的基于梯度搜索和端到端学习的新模型铺平了道路。

Original abstract: A central challenge in program induction has long been the trade-off between symbolic and neural approaches. Symbolic methods offer compositional generalisation and data efficiency, yet their scalability is constrained by formalisms such as domain-specific languages (DSLs), which are labour-intensive to create and may not transfer to new domains. In contrast, neural networks flexibly learn from data but tend to generalise poorly in compositional and out-of-distribution settings. We bridge this divide with an instance of a Latent Adaptation Network architecture named Neural Language Interpreter (NLI), which learns its own discrete, symbolic-like programming language end-to-end. NLI autonomously discovers a vocabulary of primitive operations and uses a novel differentiable neural executor to interpret variable-length sequences of these primitives. This allows NLI to represent programs that are not bound to a constant number of computation steps, enabling it to solve more complex problems than those seen during training. To make these discrete, compositional program structures amenable to gradient-based optimisation, we employ the Gumbel-Softmax relaxation, enabling the entire model to be trained end-to-end. Crucially, this same differentiability enables powerful test-time adaptation. At inference, NLI's program inductor provides an initial program guess. This guess is then refined via gradient descent through the neural executor, enabling efficient search for the neural program that best explains the given data. We demonstrate that NLI outperforms in-context learning, test-time training, and continuous latent program networks on tasks that require combinatorial generalisation and rapid adaptation to unseen tasks. Our results establish a new path toward models that combine the compositionality of discrete languages with the gradient-based search and end-to-end learning of neural networks.

</details>

### [111] [Poster: EdgeCitadel -- Hybrid NATS-MQTT Orchestration for Edge Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14710v1)
*Zhonghao Zhan,Yefan Zhang,Hamed Haddadi*

Main category: cs.DC

Selection reason: 边缘多agent编排平台，直接与多agent系统相关。

TL;DR: EdgeCitadel是一个基于NATS和MQTT的边缘多代理编排平台，通过混合架构实现异构设备的高效协调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有边缘AI代理协调堆栈依赖云风格传输或中央中继，无法适应边缘环境的异构性和低延迟需求。

Method: 使用单个NATS 2.10服务器和内置MQTT适配器，结合MQTT连接、JetStream持久化与重放、直接对等委派以及被动聚合器，构建混合架构。

Result: 成功从MQTT中继原型迁移到混合架构，并在ARM64、x64和Android设备上搭建了跨设备测试平台。

Conclusion: EdgeCitadel证明了混合架构在边缘多代理编排中的可行性和有效性，为未来边缘AI应用提供了基础。

中文摘要：边缘驻留的AI代理越来越多地分布在家庭服务器、物联网中心、笔记本电脑和手机上，但它们的协调堆栈仍然采用云风格的传输或中央中继。我们提出了EdgeCitadel，一个基于单个NATS 2.10服务器并带有内置MQTT适配器的边缘多代理编排平台。该设计结合了用于异构代理的MQTT连接、用于后端服务的JetStream支持的持久化和重放、通过共享主题命名空间的直接对等委派，以及一个在不位于传输路径上的被动聚合器，用于可视化和存储流量。我们的海报重点介绍了从（物联网通信中常见的）MQTT中继原型到当前混合架构的迁移，并展示了一个跨越ARM64、x64和Android客户端的工作跨设备测试平台。

Original abstract: Edge-resident AI agents increasingly span home servers, IoT hubs, laptops, and phones, yet their coordination stacks still assume cloud-style transports or a central relay. We present EdgeCitadel, an edge multi-agent orchestration platform built around a single NATS 2.10 server with the built-in MQTT adapter. The design combines MQTT connectivity for heterogeneous agents, JetStream-backed persistence and replay for backend services, direct peer delegation over a shared subject namespace, and a passive aggregator that visualizes and stores traffic without sitting on the delivery path. Our poster highlights the migration from MQTT relay prototypes (common in IoT communication) to the current hybrid architecture and demonstrates a working cross-device testbed spanning ARM64, x64, and Android clients.

</details>
